[#MBCA120k3i]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(3)(i) (filed document means document filed by secretary under any Act provision except chapter 15 and section 16.21).

[#MBCA120k3ii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(3)(ii) (plan means plan of domestication, conversion, merger, or share exchange).

[#MBCA120k4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4) (specified core provisions of plan or filed document may NOT depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k4i]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4)(i) (name and address of any person required in filed document may not depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k4ii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4)(ii) (registered office of any entity required in filed document may not depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k4iii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4)(iii) (registered agent of any entity required in filed document may not depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k4iv]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4)(iv) (number of authorized shares and designation of each class or series may not depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k4v]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4)(v) (effective date of filed document may not depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k4vi]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(4)(vi) (statement of approval date or manner of approval may not depend on extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA120k5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.20(k)(5) (if provision depends on non-public extrinsic fact and shareholders not notified, corporation must file amendment stating fact promptly after ascertainable or changed).

[#MBCA121]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21 (secretary of state authority to prescribe forms).

[#MBCA121a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(a) (secretary may prescribe and furnish mandatory forms for five specified documents).

[#MBCA121ai]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(a)(i) (mandatory form for certificate of existence or registration application).

[#MBCA121aii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(a)(ii) (mandatory form for foreign corporation registration statement).

[#MBCA121aiii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(a)(iii) (mandatory form for foreign corporation withdrawal statement).

[#MBCA121aiv]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(a)(iv) (mandatory form for foreign corporation transfer of registration statement).

[#MBCA121av]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(a)(v) (mandatory form for annual report).

[#MBCA121b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.21(b) (secretary may prescribe optional forms for other documents; use not mandatory).

[#MBCA122]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.22 (filing, service, and copying fees collected by secretary of state).

[#MBCA122a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.22(a) (secretary shall collect specified fees when enumerated documents delivered for filing).

[#MBCA122b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.22(b) (secretary shall collect fee for each service of process; prevailing party entitled to recover as costs).

[#MBCA122c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.22(c) (secretary shall collect fees for copying and certifying filed documents).

[#MBCA123]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23 (effective date and time of filed documents).

[#MBCA123a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23(a) (document accepted for filing becomes effective as specified in subsections (1)-(4)).

[#MBCA123a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23(a)(1) (effective on date and time of filing as determined under section 1.25(b)).

[#MBCA123a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23(a)(2) (effective on date of filing at later time specified in document).

[#MBCA123a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23(a)(3) (effective at specified delayed date and time not more than 90 days after filing).

[#MBCA123a4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23(a)(4) (if delayed date specified without time, effective at 12:01 a.m. on that date, up to 90 days after filing).

[#MBCA123b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.23(b) (if document does not specify time zone, default is time zone of place of filing in this state).

[#MBCA124]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24 (procedure for correcting filed documents containing inaccuracies or defects).

[#MBCA124a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(a) (document may be corrected if it contains inaccuracy or specified defects).

[#MBCA124ai]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(a)(i) (correction permitted if document contains inaccuracy).

[#MBCA124aii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(a)(ii) (correction permitted if document defectively signed, attested, sealed, verified, or acknowledged).

[#MBCA124aiii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(a)(iii) (correction permitted if electronic transmission was defective).

[#MBCA124b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(b) (document corrected by preparing and delivering articles of correction).

[#MBCA124b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(b)(1) (articles of correction must meet specified requirements).

[#MBCA124b1i]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(b)(1)(i) (articles must describe document being corrected, including filing date, or attach copy).

[#MBCA124b1ii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(b)(1)(ii) (articles must specify inaccuracy or defect to be corrected).

[#MBCA124b1iii]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(b)(1)(iii) (articles must correct the inaccuracy or defect).

[#MBCA124b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(b)(2) (articles of correction must be delivered to secretary of state for filing).

[#MBCA124c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24(c) (articles of correction effective on original effective date except as to persons detrimentally relying on uncorrected document; effective when filed as to those persons).

[#MBCA124cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.24 Official Comment (articles of correction cannot create retroactive filing where original defect prevented any filing).

[#MBCA125]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25 (secretary of state's duty to file documents and procedures for filing or refusal).

[#MBCA125a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25(a) (if document satisfies section 1.20 requirements, secretary of state shall file it).

[#MBCA125b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25(b) (secretary files by recording as filed on date and time of receipt; returns copy with acknowledgment).

[#MBCA125c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25(c) (if secretary refuses filing, must return document within five days with brief written explanation).

[#MBCA125d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25(d) (secretary's filing duty is ministerial; filing or refusal creates no presumptions about validity).

[#MBCA125d1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25(d)(1) (no presumption that document does or does not conform to Act requirements).

[#MBCA125d2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25(d)(2) (no presumption that information in document is correct or incorrect).

[#MBCA125cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.25 Official Comment (validity may be tested by affected parties or attorney general despite ministerial filing).

[#MBCA126]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.26 (judicial appeal from secretary of state's refusal to file document).

[#MBCA126a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.26(a) (person may petition court to compel filing in summary proceeding).

[#MBCA126b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.26(b) (court may order secretary to file or take other appropriate action).

[#MBCA126c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.26(c) (court's final decision may be appealed as in other civil proceedings).

[#MBCA127]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.27 (certificate from secretary of state delivered with copy of filed document is conclusive evidence original is on file).

[#MBCA128]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28 (procedure for obtaining certificate of existence or registration from secretary of state).

[#MBCA128a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(a) (any person may apply to secretary for certificate of existence for domestic corporation or certificate of registration for foreign corporation).

[#MBCA128b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b) (certificate of existence sets forth seven specified categories of information).

[#MBCA128b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(1) (certificate states domestic corporation's corporate name).

[#MBCA128b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(2) (certificate states corporation duly incorporated, date of incorporation, and duration if less than perpetual).

[#MBCA128b3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(3) (certificate states fees, taxes, and penalties paid if payment reflected in secretary's records and nonpayment affects existence).

[#MBCA128b4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(4) (certificate states most recent annual report filed with secretary).

[#MBCA128b5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(5) (certificate states articles of dissolution have not been filed).

[#MBCA128b6]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(6) (certificate states corporation not administratively dissolved and no proceeding pending under section 14.21).

[#MBCA128b7]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(b)(7) (certificate may state other facts of record in secretary's office requested by applicant).

[#MBCA128c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(c) (certificate of registration sets forth foreign corporation's name, registration status, fees and taxes paid, annual report filed, and other requested facts).

[#MBCA128d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28(d) (subject to any qualification stated in certificate, certificate may be relied upon as conclusive evidence of facts stated).

[#MBCA128cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.28 Official Comment (secretary makes judgment from public records only without extensive investigation; may issue qualified certificate).

[#MBCA129]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.29 (criminal penalty for signing false document intended for filing).

[#MBCA129a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.29(a) (person commits offense by signing document person knows is materially false with intent it be delivered to secretary for filing).

[#MBCA129b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.29(b) (offense is misdemeanor punishable by fine not to exceed specified amount).


[#MBCA130]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.30 (secretary of state has power reasonably necessary to perform duties required by Act).


[#MBCA140]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.40 (general definitions applicable throughout Act unless otherwise specified).

[#MBCA140cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.40 Official Comment (beneficial shareholder means person who owns beneficial interest in shares but does not include voting trust beneficial owner).

[#MBCA141]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41 (requirements for delivery and effectiveness of notices and other communications to shareholders and corporation).

[#MBCA141a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(a) (notice or other communication under Act or articles or bylaws must be in writing unless oral communication is reasonable under circumstances).

[#MBCA141b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(b) (notice to domestic or foreign corporation may be in writing or by electronic transmission and is effective as specified in this section).

[#MBCA141c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(c) (notice or other communication to shareholder may be delivered by mail, private carrier, or electronically).

[#MBCA141d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(d) (written notice or other written communication to shareholder may be delivered by electronic transmission if shareholder consents).

[#MBCA141e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(e) (corporation's authority to deliver by electronic transmission ceases if unable to deliver two consecutive transmissions and inability becomes known to officers or agents).

[#MBCA141f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(f) (electronic transmission is received when it enters information processing system designated by recipient or enters system under recipient's control).

[#MBCA141g]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(g) (receipt of electronic acknowledgment establishes that transmission was received but not content or whether read).

[#MBCA141h]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(h) (electronic transmission is received even if recipient or individual is unaware of its receipt).

[#MBCA141i]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(i) (notice or other communication is effective when received except as otherwise provided in this section).

[#MBCA141j]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(j) (use of electronic transmissions only retrievable in perceivable form and not directly reproducible requires specific written consent).

[#MBCA141k]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(k) (oral notice or other oral communication is effective when communicated in comprehensible manner).

[#MBCA141l]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(l) (if sections 1.41c or 1.41d condition delivery on information or acts, requirement is met when shareholder provides information or takes required acts).

[#MBCA141m]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(m) (corporation not required to give notice to shareholder if two consecutive notices or distributions sent to shareholder were undeliverable and remain undeliverable).

[#MBCA141m1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(m)(1) (if undeliverable notice is annual meeting notice, corporation need not send further notices until shareholder provides new address and requests notice).

[#MBCA141m2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.41(m)(2) (if undeliverable notice is not annual meeting notice, undeliverable period begins with first undeliverable notice and continues through second undeliverable notice).


[#MBCA142]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.42 (rules for determining number of shareholders for purposes of Act).

[#MBCA142a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.42(a) (for purposes of Act, following identified as shareholder in corporation's current record of shareholders constitutes one shareholder).

[#MBCA142a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.42(a)(1) (three or fewer co-owners constitute one shareholder).

[#MBCA142a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.42(a)(2) (corporation, partnership, trust, estate, or other entity constitutes one shareholder).

[#MBCA142a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.42(a)(3) (trustees, guardians, custodians, or other fiduciaries of single trust, estate, or account constitute one shareholder).

[#MBCA142b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.42(b) (shareholdings registered in substantially similar names constitute one shareholder if reasonable to believe names represent same person).


[#MBCA143]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43 (definition of qualified director for purposes of specific corporate actions under Act).

[#MBCA143a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(a) (qualified director is director who meets specified criteria at time action is to be taken under enumerated sections).

[#MBCA143a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(a)(1) (for section 2.02(b)(6) actions, qualified director is not director to whom officer opportunity limitation would apply or who has material relationship with such person).

[#MBCA143a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(a)(2) (for section 7.44 derivative proceeding dismissal, qualified director does not have material interest in outcome or material relationship with person who has such interest).

[#MBCA143a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(a)(3) (for sections 8.53 and 8.55 indemnification actions, qualified director is not party to proceeding and not director with conflicting interest transaction or business opportunity disclaimer being challenged).

[#MBCA143a4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(a)(4) (for section 8.62 director transaction approval, qualified director is not director for whom transaction is conflicting interest transaction or who has material relationship with such director).

[#MBCA143a5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(a)(5) (for section 8.70 business opportunity disclaimer, qualified director is not director who pursues opportunity or who has material relationship with director or officer who pursues opportunity).

[#MBCA143b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(b) (definitions of material relationship and material interest for qualified director purposes).

[#MBCA143b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(b)(1) (material relationship means familial, financial, professional, employment or other relationship that would reasonably impair objectivity of director's judgment).

[#MBCA143b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(b)(2) (material interest means actual or potential benefit or detriment beyond what would devolve on corporation or shareholders generally that would reasonably impair objectivity).

[#MBCA143c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(c) (specified circumstances that do not by themselves prevent director from being qualified director).

[#MBCA143c1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(c)(1) (nomination or election by nonqualified director or defendant does not alone prevent director from being qualified).

[#MBCA143c2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(c)(2) (service as director of another corporation where nonqualified director also serves does not alone prevent qualification).

[#MBCA143c3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43(c)(3) (for section 7.44 derivative proceeding actions, status as named defendant or director who approved challenged conduct does not alone prevent qualification).

[#MBCA143cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.43 Official Comment (qualified director embraces both disinterest and independence requirements, applied in situation-specific manner based on directly relevant facts).


[#MBCA144]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44 (procedure for delivering single copy of notices, reports, or statements to shareholders who share common address).

[#MBCA144a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44(a) (corporation has delivered written notice or report to all shareholders who share common address if specified conditions met).

[#MBCA144a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44(a)(1) (corporation delivers one copy of notice, report or statement to common address).

[#MBCA144a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44(a)(2) (corporation addresses notice to shareholders as group, individually, or in form to which each consented).

[#MBCA144a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44(a)(3) (each of those shareholders consents to delivery of single copy to common address).

[#MBCA144b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44(b) (consent to householding is revocable by written notice; corporation must begin individual delivery within 30 days of revocation).

[#MBCA144c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.44(c) (shareholder who fails to object within 60 days of corporation's written notice of intention to household is deemed to have consented).


[#MBCA145]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (definitions applicable to subchapter on ratification of defective corporate actions).

[#MBCA145corpact]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (corporate action means any action taken by or on behalf of corporation, including by incorporator, board, committee, officer, agent, or shareholders).

[#MBCA145date]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (date of defective corporate action means date or approximate date defective action was purported to have been taken).

[#MBCA145defect]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (defective corporate action means corporate action purportedly taken within corporation's power but void or voidable due to failure of authorization, and includes overissue).

[#MBCA145failure]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (failure of authorization means failure to authorize, approve, or effect corporate action in compliance with Act, articles, bylaws, resolution, or agreement to extent failure would render action void or voidable).

[#MBCA145overissue]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (overissue means purported issuance of shares in excess of authorized number or of class or series not then authorized).

[#MBCA145putative]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (putative shares means shares created or issued as result of defective corporate action that but for failure of authorization would be valid or cannot be determined to be valid).

[#MBCA145valid]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (valid shares means shares duly authorized and validly issued in accordance with Act, including as result of ratification or validation).

[#MBCA145valtime]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.45 (validation effective time means later of shareholder approval time or articles of validation effective time, unaffected by judicial proceeding unless court orders otherwise).

[#MBCA146]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.46 (effect of ratification or validation of defective corporate actions).

[#MBCA146a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.46(a) (defective corporate action not void or voidable if ratified under section 1.47 or validated under section 1.52).

[#MBCA146b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.46(b) (ratification under this subchapter not exclusive means; absence or failure of ratification does not affect validity of action properly ratified under common law or create presumption of defect).

[#MBCA146c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.46(c) (in overissue case, putative shares become valid shares effective as of date originally issued upon effectiveness of articles amendment or other ratifying corporate action).

[#MBCA147]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47 (procedure for board of directors to ratify defective corporate actions).

[#MBCA147a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(a) (to ratify defective corporate action other than initial board election, board takes action in accordance with section 1.48 stating specified information).

[#MBCA147a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(a)(1) (board action must state defective corporate action to be ratified and, if involved putative shares, number and type purportedly issued).

[#MBCA147a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(a)(2) (board action must state date of defective corporate action).

[#MBCA147a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(a)(3) (board action must state nature of failure of authorization with respect to defective action).

[#MBCA147a4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(a)(4) (board action must state that board approves ratification of defective corporate action).

[#MBCA147b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(b) (for defective initial board election, majority of persons exercising director powers may ratify by taking action stating specified information).

[#MBCA147c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(c) (if ratification requires approval by shareholders under this section or other Act provision, action taken under subsection (a) must be submitted to shareholders for approval).

[#MBCA147d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.47(d) (unless otherwise provided in board action, board may abandon ratification before validation effective time without further shareholder action).

[#MBCA148]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48 (quorum, voting, notice, and procedural requirements for ratification actions).

[#MBCA148a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48(a) (quorum and voting requirements for board ratifying action are same as for corporate action proposed to be ratified).

[#MBCA148b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48(b) (if shareholder approval required and given at meeting, corporation must notify holders of valid and putative shares as of record dates with specified information).

[#MBCA148c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48(c) (quorum and voting requirements for shareholder approval of ratification are same as for corporate action being ratified).

[#MBCA148d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48(d) (approval of director election ratification requires votes favoring ratification to exceed votes opposing at meeting with quorum present).

[#MBCA148e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48(e) (putative shares as of record date not entitled to vote on ratification and not counted for quorum purposes).

[#MBCA148f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.48(f) (if putative share approval would cause overissue, approval of articles amendment to eliminate overissue also required).

[#MBCA149]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.49 (notice requirements for ratification of defective corporate actions).

[#MBCA149a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.49(a) (unless shareholder approval required under section 1.47(c), prompt notice of board ratification action must be given to holders of valid and putative shares).

[#MBCA149b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.49(b) (notice must contain copy of board action or required information and statement regarding 120-day claim period).

[#MBCA149c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.49(c) (no notice under this section required for shareholder-approved action if notice given under section 1.48(b)).

[#MBCA149d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.49(d) (notice may be given in any manner permitted by section 1.41 or for public companies by SEC filing).

[#MBCA150]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.50 (effect of ratification of defective corporate actions from and after validation effective time).

[#MBCA150a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.50(a) (each defective corporate action ratified under section 1.47 not void or voidable and deemed valid effective as of date of defective action).

[#MBCA150b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.50(b) (issuance of each putative share pursuant to ratified defective action not void or voidable and deemed identical to valid share as of time purportedly issued).

[#MBCA150c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.50(c) (corporate action taken subsequent to defective action in reliance on it and subsequent defective actions resulting from original defective action are valid as of time taken).

[#MBCA151]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51 (filing requirements for articles of validation when defective corporate action required or would have required filing).

[#MBCA151a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51(a) (if ratified defective action would have required filing, corporation must file articles of validation in lieu of other filing otherwise required).

[#MBCA151b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51(b) (articles of validation must set forth defective action, date, nature of failure, ratification dates, and information required by subsection (c)).

[#MBCA151c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51(c) (articles of validation must contain specified information depending on whether prior filing was made and whether changes required).

[#MBCA151c1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51(c)(1) (if prior filing made and no changes required to give effect to ratification, articles must identify prior filing and state copy is attached).

[#MBCA151c2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51(c)(2) (if prior filing made and changes required, articles must identify prior filing and attach corrected filing with effective date and time).

[#MBCA151c3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.51(c)(3) (if no prior filing made and defective action would have required filing, articles must attach required filing and state effective date and time).

[#MBCA152]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.52 (judicial proceedings regarding validity of corporate actions, including ratified defective actions).

[#MBCA152a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.52(a) (court may determine validity of any corporate action, defective action, ratification, or putative shares and may modify or waive ratification procedures upon application by enumerated parties).

[#MBCA152b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.52(b) (court may make findings or orders and consider any factors or considerations deemed proper under circumstances).

[#MBCA152c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.52(c) (service on corporation permitted in manner provided by statute or court rule; no other party need be joined for court to adjudicate matter).

[#MBCA152d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.52(d) (any action asserting ratification should not be effective or should be effective only on conditions must be brought within 120 days of validation effective time).

[#MBCA152cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 1.52 Official Comment (court has plenary jurisdiction over validity of corporate actions and shares, not limited to reviewing actions ratified under section 1.47; courts may consider any relevant factors).



[#MBCA201]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.01 (one or more persons may act as incorporator by delivering articles of incorporation for filing with secretary of state).

[#MBCA201cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.01 Official Comment (incorporator’s only functions are to sign and deliver articles and, if applicable, complete organization under § 2.05; “person” includes individuals and entities).


[#MBCA202]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02 (contents of articles of incorporation; exculpation, indemnification, and opportunity-waiver provisions).

[#MBCA202a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(a) (articles must state: (1) corporate name meeting § 4.01; (2) number of authorized shares; (3) street and mailing addresses of initial registered office and name of initial registered agent; (4) name and address of each incorporator).

[#MBCA202b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(b) (articles may also state: (1) names and addresses of initial directors; (2) optional provisions on purposes, management, and powers, par value, and shareholder “interest holder liability”; (3) any provision that could be in bylaws; (4) director/officer monetary liability limits; (5) director indemnification; (6) advance limitation or elimination of duty to present corporate opportunities, subject to qualified-director approval when applied to officers or their related persons).

[#MBCA202b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(b)(2) (articles may include: (i) specific corporate purposes; (ii) provisions on managing business and regulating corporate affairs; (iii) provisions defining, limiting, and regulating powers of corporation, board, and shareholders; (iv) optional par value terms; (v) imposition of shareholder interest holder liability).

[#MBCA202b3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(b)(3) (articles may include any provision this Act requires or permits to be set forth in bylaws).

[#MBCA202b4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(b)(4) (articles may eliminate or limit money-damages liability of director or specified officers to corporation or shareholders, but not for: (i) improper financial benefit; (ii) intentional infliction of harm; (iii) in case of director, violation of § 8.32 (unlawful distributions); (iv) intentional violation of criminal law; or (v) in case of officer, any claim by or in right of corporation).

[#MBCA202b5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(b)(5) (articles may require or permit indemnification of director for “liability” under § 8.50, but not for: (i) improper financial benefit; (ii) intentional infliction of harm; (iii) violation of § 8.32; (iv) intentional criminal law violation).

[#MBCA202b6]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(b)(6) (articles may limit or eliminate any duty of director or other person to offer specified business opportunities to corporation before pursuit; application to an officer or related person of an officer requires post-effective authorization by qualified directors under procedures paralleling § 8.62 and may be limited by that authorizing action).

[#MBCA202c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(c) (articles need not recite statutory corporate powers).

[#MBCA202d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(d) (articles may use “facts objectively ascertainable” outside articles, consistent with § 1.20(k)).

[#MBCA202e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(e) (“related person” has meaning in § 8.60 for purposes of opportunity provisions).

[#MBCA202f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02(f) (for § 2.02(b)(4): “officer” means (i) an individual appointed or elected under § 8.40 as president, chief executive officer, chief operating officer, chief financial officer, chief legal officer, secretary, controller, treasurer, or chief accounting officer; and (ii) any other officer expressly designated by board resolution as covered; board may later remove such designation prospectively by resolution).

[#MBCA202cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02 Official Comment (corporation has perpetual duration and broad lawful-purpose default unless articles narrow duration or purposes; required provisions limited to name, shares, registered office/agent, and incorporators).

[#MBCA202cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.02 Official Comment (lists options that must be in articles versus those that may be in articles or bylaws; explains optional par value, shareholder liability, exculpation, director indemnification, and business-opportunity waivers, and cross-references relevant sections such as §§ 3.01, 3.02, 6.01, 6.02, 6.21, 6.22, 6.30, 7.32, 8.30, 8.32, 8.40, 8.50–8.59, 8.70, 9.21, 9.32, 10.03, 10.22, 11.04).


[#MBCA203]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.03 (time corporate existence begins and evidentiary effect of filing on conditions precedent).

[#MBCA203a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.03(a) (unless delayed effective date is specified, corporate existence begins when articles of incorporation are filed, with effective date determined under § 1.23).

[#MBCA203b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.03(b) (secretary of state’s filing of articles is conclusive proof that incorporators satisfied all conditions precedent to incorporation, except in state proceedings to cancel, revoke, or involuntarily dissolve).


[#MBCA204]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.04 (joint and several liability for those acting as or on behalf of nonexistent corporation with knowledge that no incorporation has occurred).

[#MBCA204cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.04 Official Comment (limited liability generally arises only upon filing, but liability under § 2.04 is imposed only on persons who know no corporation exists; preserves possibility of estoppel where third parties insisted on use of corporate name knowing no incorporation).


[#MBCA205]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.05 (organizational meeting and alternative methods to complete organization after incorporation).

[#MBCA205a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.05(a)(1) (if initial directors are named in articles, they must, at call of a majority, hold organizational meeting to appoint officers, adopt bylaws, and conduct other business to complete organization).

[#MBCA205a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.05(a)(2) (if initial directors not named, incorporators must, at call of a majority, hold organizational meeting either (i) to elect initial directors and complete organization, or (ii) to elect a board that will complete organization).

[#MBCA205b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.05(b) (incorporators may take organizational actions without a meeting by unanimous written consent describing the action).

[#MBCA205c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.05(c) (organizational meeting may be held in or out of the state of incorporation).

[#MBCA205cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.05 Official Comment (explains customary organizational steps: bylaws, officers, agents, initial share issuances, board election; describes choice between incorporator-centered or board-centered organization).


[#MBCA206]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06 (adoption and content of bylaws; proxy access and proxy-expense reimbursement bylaws).

[#MBCA206a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06(a) (incorporators or board must adopt initial bylaws).

[#MBCA206b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06(b) (bylaws may contain any provision not inconsistent with law or articles; may not contradict director managerial authority under § 8.01(b)).

[#MBCA206c1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06(c)(1) (bylaws may require corporation, when soliciting proxies or consents for director elections, to include in its proxy statement and proxy or consent forms one or more shareholder-nominated director candidates, subject to bylaw-specified procedures and conditions).

[#MBCA206c2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06(c)(2) (bylaws may require corporation to reimburse shareholder’s reasonable expenses for proxy or consent solicitations in director elections, subject to bylaw procedures and conditions; such a bylaw does not apply retroactively to elections with earlier record dates).

[#MBCA206d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06(d) (even if shareholders adopt or amend a § 2.06(c) bylaw, they may not wholly preclude board from amending or repealing conditions or procedures or adding new ones to ensure a reasonable, practical, orderly process).

[#MBCA206cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.06 Official Comment (allocates initial bylaw adoption to incorporators or board; clarifies that proxy-access and reimbursement bylaws are consistent with § 8.01(b) and gives examples of permissible conditions, such as ownership thresholds, holding periods, caps on reimbursement, informational requirements, and anti-control-change limits).


[#MBCA207]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.07 (authorization and effect of bylaws operative only during an “emergency”).

[#MBCA207a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.07(a) (unless articles provide otherwise, bylaws may contain provisions effective only during an emergency; such emergency bylaws may be adopted only in advance and may cover: (1) procedures for calling board meetings; (2) quorum requirements; (3) designation of additional or substitute directors).

[#MBCA207b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.07(b) (regular bylaws remain effective during emergency insofar as not inconsistent with emergency bylaws).

[#MBCA207c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.07(c) (corporate action taken in good faith under emergency bylaws: (1) binds the corporation; and (2) may not be used to impose liability on directors, officers, employees, or agents because of such action).

[#MBCA207d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.07(d) (an “emergency” exists if a quorum of the board cannot readily be assembled because of a catastrophic event).

[#MBCA207cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.07 Official Comment (explains examples of catastrophic events, such as nuclear disasters, cyberattacks, epidemics, or declared states of emergency; emphasizes continuity of governance and broad immunity for good-faith actions; notes that emergency powers under § 3.03 can be used even without emergency bylaws).


[#MBCA208]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.08 (permitted forum-selection provisions for “internal corporate claims”).

[#MBCA208a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.08(a) (articles or bylaws may require that any or all internal corporate claims be brought exclusively in specified court or courts of the state of incorporation, and, if specified, in additional courts in that state or in other jurisdictions with a reasonable relationship to the corporation).

[#MBCA208b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.08(b) (forum bylaw or charter provision does not itself confer jurisdiction or apply if specified courts lack personal or subject-matter jurisdiction; if specified state court lacks such jurisdiction but another state court has it, claim may be brought in that other state court and any other specified court with jurisdiction).

[#MBCA208c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.08(c) (articles or bylaws may not prohibit bringing an internal corporate claim in courts of the state of incorporation or require such claims to be resolved by arbitration).

[#MBCA208d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.08(d) (“internal corporate claim” includes: (i) claims based on violation of duty under state law by current or former director, officer, or shareholder in that capacity; (ii) derivative proceedings; (iii) claims arising under this Act or the articles or bylaws; and (iv) other claims governed by internal-affairs doctrine not already included).

[#MBCA208cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 2.08 Official Comment (authorizes exclusive-forum provisions keyed to internal corporate claims; requires at least one in-state court; clarifies operation when specified courts lack jurisdiction and preserves at least one in-state forum if any has jurisdiction).



[#MBCA301]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.01 (default and limited-purpose clauses for corporations).

[#MBCA301a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.01(a) (every corporation has the purpose of engaging in any lawful business unless the articles of incorporation state a more limited purpose).

[#MBCA301b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.01(b) (a corporation engaging in a regulated business may incorporate under this Act only if permitted by, and subject to, applicable regulatory statute).

[#MBCA301cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.01 Official Comment (any-lawful-business purpose is standard; even with a narrow purpose clause, ultra vires is sharply limited in outsider litigation; special statutes may constrain incorporation for banking, insurance, professional practice, and similar fields).


[#MBCA302]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02 (perpetual duration and broad powers comparable to those of an individual).

[#MBCA302lead]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02 (unless articles provide otherwise, every corporation has perpetual duration and all powers necessary or convenient to carry out its business and affairs).

[#MBCA302a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(a) (power to sue and be sued in corporate name).

[#MBCA302b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(b) (power to have and alter corporate seal and use it or a facsimile in any manner).

[#MBCA302c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(c) (power to make and amend bylaws, consistent with articles and state law, for managing business and regulating corporate affairs).

[#MBCA302d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(d) (power to acquire, own, hold, improve, use, and otherwise deal with real or personal property, or any legal or equitable interest, wherever located).

[#MBCA302e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(e) (power to sell, convey, mortgage, pledge, lease, exchange, or otherwise dispose of all or any part of corporate property).

[#MBCA302f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(f) (power to acquire, own, hold, vote, use, sell, mortgage, lend, pledge, or otherwise deal in shares, interests, or obligations of any other entity).

[#MBCA302g]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(g) (power to make contracts and guarantees, incur liabilities, borrow money, issue notes, bonds, and other securities or obligations, including those convertible into or with options to purchase corporate securities, and to secure obligations with corporate property, franchises, or income).

[#MBCA302h]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(h) (power to lend money, invest and reinvest funds, and receive and hold property as security).

[#MBCA302i]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(i) (power to be a promoter, partner, member, associate, or manager of any partnership, joint venture, trust, or other entity).

[#MBCA302j]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(j) (power to conduct business, locate offices, and exercise corporate powers within or outside the state).

[#MBCA302k]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(k) (power to elect directors; appoint officers, employees, and agents; define their duties; fix compensation; and lend them money and credit).

[#MBCA302l]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(l) (power to pay pensions and establish pension, profit-sharing, share-bonus, share-option, and other benefit or incentive plans for current or former directors, officers, employees, and agents).

[#MBCA302m]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(m) (power to make donations for public welfare or for charitable, scientific, or educational purposes).

[#MBCA302n]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(n) (power to transact any lawful business that will aid governmental policy).

[#MBCA302o]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02(o) (power to make payments or donations or to do any other lawful act that furthers corporate business and affairs).

[#MBCA302cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.02 Official Comment (corporate powers are as broad as an individual’s unless narrowed in articles; narrow purpose clauses do not generally constrain these powers in dealings with third parties; ultra vires is handled through § 3.04 rather than by restricting apparent authority in ordinary transactions).


[#MBCA303]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03 (special governance rules and protections applicable during emergencies).

[#MBCA303a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03(a)(1) (during an emergency, unless emergency bylaws provide otherwise, notice of a board meeting need be given only to directors whom it is practicable to reach and may be given in any practicable manner).

[#MBCA303a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03(a)(2) (during an emergency, unless emergency bylaws provide otherwise, officers present at a board meeting may be deemed directors, in rank and seniority order, to the extent needed for a quorum).

[#MBCA303b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03(b) (during an emergency, unless emergency bylaws provide otherwise, the board may postpone a noticed shareholders’ meeting or authorize shareholders to participate by remote communication consistent with § 7.09(b), giving shortened, reasonable notice of changes and remote means).

[#MBCA303c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03(c) (corporate action taken in good faith under § 3.03 during an emergency to further corporate business: (1) binds the corporation; and (2) may not be used to impose liability on any director, officer, employee, or agent because of such action).

[#MBCA303d1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03(d)(1) (for board procedures under subsection (a), an emergency exists if a quorum of the board cannot readily be assembled because of a catastrophic event).

[#MBCA303d2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03(d)(2) (for shareholder-meeting procedures under subsection (b), an emergency exists if, because of a catastrophic event, it is impracticable to convene a shareholders’ meeting as required by the Act, the bylaws, or prior notice).

[#MBCA303cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.03 Official Comment (to be read with § 2.07; corporations have baseline emergency powers even without emergency bylaws; “catastrophic event” is broad and includes circumstances such as disasters or public emergencies; directors remain subject to § 8.30’s conduct standards, but enjoy strong protection for good-faith emergency decisions).


[#MBCA304]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04 (modern ultra vires rule limiting when lack of corporate power can be asserted).

[#MBCA304a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04(a) (except as provided in subsection (b), the validity of corporate action may not be challenged on the ground that the corporation lacks or lacked power to act).

[#MBCA304b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04(b)(1) (lack of corporate power may be raised in a proceeding by a shareholder against the corporation to enjoin the act).

[#MBCA304b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04(b)(2) (lack of corporate power may be raised in a proceeding by or in the right of the corporation, including through a receiver or similar representative, against an incumbent or former director, officer, employee, or agent).

[#MBCA304b3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04(b)(3) (lack of corporate power may be raised in a proceeding by the attorney general under § 14.30).

[#MBCA304c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04(c) (in a shareholder action to enjoin an unauthorized act, the court may enjoin or set aside the act if equitable and if all affected persons are parties, and may award damages for loss other than anticipated profits caused by the injunction).

[#MBCA304cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04 Official Comment (persons dealing with a corporation need not investigate purpose or power limits; a counterparty unaware of those limits is not bound by them and may enforce transactions despite internal restrictions).

[#MBCA304cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04 Official Comment (ultra vires cannot be used as sword or shield in ordinary contract litigation; the statute does not validate conduct that is independently illegal and does not address lack of proper internal authorization or breaches of fiduciary duty, which are governed by agency and duty-of-loyalty principles).

[#MBCA304cmt3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04 Official Comment (a shareholder may seek to enjoin an ultra vires act only if all affected parties are before the court and equitable factors favor relief; even then, the court may award damages, excluding anticipated profits, to either side for losses caused by the injunction).

[#MBCA304cmt4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 3.04 Official Comment (the corporation may still sue insiders for causing ultra vires acts, and the attorney general may still proceed under judicial-dissolution statutes; section 3.04 preserves, rather than defines, those remedies).


[#MBCA401]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01 (requirements for corporate name, including corporate designator, permissible purposes, and distinguishability on secretary of state records).

[#MBCA401a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(a)(1) (corporate name must contain “corporation,” “incorporated,” “company,” or “limited,” or an accepted abbreviation or equivalent words in another language).

[#MBCA401a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(a)(2) (corporate name may not state or imply a purpose not permitted by § 3.01 and the corporation’s articles of incorporation).

[#MBCA401b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b) (except as allowed by subsections (c) and (d), corporate name must be distinguishable on the secretary of state’s records from specified existing, reserved, registered, foreign, nonprofit, unincorporated, and assumed names).

[#MBCA401b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(1) (name must be distinguishable from the corporate name of any domestic business corporation not administratively dissolved).

[#MBCA401b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(2) (name must be distinguishable from any corporate name reserved or registered under §§ 4.02 or 4.03 or under similar state law).

[#MBCA401b3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(3) (name must be distinguishable from the name of any foreign business corporation registered to do business in the state, or any alternate name it has adopted because its real name is unavailable).

[#MBCA401b4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(4) (name must be distinguishable from the corporate name of any domestic nonprofit corporation not administratively dissolved).

[#MBCA401b5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(5) (name must be distinguishable from the name, or alternate name, of any foreign nonprofit corporation registered to conduct activities in the state).

[#MBCA401b6]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(6) (name must be distinguishable from the name of any domestic filing entity or limited liability partnership not administratively dissolved).

[#MBCA401b7]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(7) (name must be distinguishable from the name, or alternate name, of any foreign unincorporated entity registered to do business or conduct activities in the state).

[#MBCA401b8]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(b)(8) (name must be distinguishable from any assumed name registered under the state’s assumed‑name statute).

[#MBCA401c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(c) (a corporation may obtain authorization to use a non‑distinguishable name if the other entity consents and undertakes to change its name to a distinguishable one, or if a final court judgment establishes the applicant’s right to use the name).

[#MBCA401d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01(d) (the Act does not regulate the use of fictitious names; that is left to other law such as assumed‑name or unfair‑competition statutes).

[#MBCA401cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01 Official Comment (two baseline requirements: a corporate name must signal corporateness and must be distinguishable on the secretary of state’s records; the statute is not a surrogate unfair‑competition or anti‑fraud regime).

[#MBCA401cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01 Official Comment (distinctiveness is judged in terms of administrative and service‑of‑process clarity, not marketplace confusion; trivial changes such as different corporate suffixes, punctuation, capitalization, or numerals ordinarily do not make a name distinguishable).

[#MBCA401cmt3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01 Official Comment (the Act leaves most issues involving assumed or fictitious names to other statutes and common‑law unfair competition; the secretary of state generally does not police commercial name conflicts).

[#MBCA401cmt4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.01 Official Comment (secretary of state’s consent mechanism allows business‑continuity structures, such as having a successor entity take over an existing official name, provided the prior user commits to adopt a distinguishable name within an agreed period).

[#MBCA402]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.02 (reservation of an exclusive corporate name for a short, nonrenewable period, including fictitious or alternate names for foreign corporations).

[#MBCA402a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.02(a) (any person may reserve exclusive use of a corporate name by filing an application with the secretary of state; if available, the name is reserved for a nonrenewable 120‑day period).

[#MBCA402b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.02(b) (the holder of a reserved name may transfer the reservation by signed notice to the secretary of state identifying the transferee).

[#MBCA402cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.02 Official Comment (name reservation is an administrative convenience to facilitate planning for new entities or foreign registrations; no showing of specific incorporation intent or special status is required).

[#MBCA402cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.02 Official Comment (a reserved name must still meet § 4.01’s requirements when used for incorporation or registration; reservation is useful for domestic formations, foreign qualifications, or protecting a chosen alternate name).

[#MBCA402cmt3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.02 Official Comment (only a single, 120‑day, nonrenewable reservation is available, though the same name can later be reserved again by anyone; longer‑term protection can be achieved by forming an inactive “name‑holding” corporation).

[#MBCA403]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03 (registration of a foreign corporation’s corporate name, or a compliant variant, for exclusive use in the state).

[#MBCA403a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03(a) (a foreign corporation may register its corporate name, with an added corporate designator if needed, if the name is distinguishable on the secretary of state’s records from names listed in § 4.01(b)).

[#MBCA403b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03(b) (registration application must state the corporate name, jurisdiction and date of incorporation, and a brief description of the business to be conducted in the state).

[#MBCA403c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03(c) (a registered name is exclusive from the effective date of registration through the remainder of the calendar year, unless renewed).

[#MBCA403d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03(d) (registration may be renewed for successive calendar years by filing a compliant renewal application between October 1 and December 31 of the preceding year).

[#MBCA403e1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03(e)(1) (a foreign corporation with an effective name registration may subsequently register to do business under that name if it satisfies § 4.01(a)(2)).

[#MBCA403e2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03(e)(2) (a foreign corporation with an effective name registration may consent to domestic or foreign use of the registered name; the registration terminates when the new entity is incorporated or registered under that name).

[#MBCA403cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03 Official Comment (name registration lets a foreign corporation “park” its corporate name for potential future qualification, but is not a mechanism for protecting trademarks, trade names, or broad assumed‑name rights).

[#MBCA403cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03 Official Comment (a foreign corporation whose name lacks a required corporate suffix may register a minimally modified version that satisfies § 4.01(a)(1) and then use that name for later qualification if it also meets § 4.01(a)(2)).

[#MBCA403cmt3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 4.03 Official Comment (compares reservation under § 4.02 and registration under § 4.03: reservations are short, nonrenewable, and available for fictitious names, while registrations protect an actual foreign corporate name through year‑end and are renewable; foreign corporations choose between them based on their expansion plans).


[#MBCA501]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.01 (requires every domestic corporation and registered foreign corporation to maintain a registered office and registered agent in the state).

[#MBCA501a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.01(a)(1) (each corporation must continuously maintain a registered office in the state, which may be the same as any of its places of business).

[#MBCA501a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.01(a)(2) (each corporation must continuously maintain a registered agent in the state: either (i) an in‑state individual whose business office is identical with the registered office, or (ii) a domestic or foreign corporation or eligible entity whose business office is identical with the registered office and, if foreign, is registered to do business in the state).

[#MBCA501b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.01(b) (for Chapter 5, “corporation” includes both a domestic corporation and a registered foreign corporation).

[#MBCA501cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.01 Official Comment (registered office and agent provide a publicly recorded, physical location for service of process and notices; a post office box alone is insufficient, and many corporations use counsel or commercial service companies as registered agents).

[#MBCA502]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.02 (provides streamlined procedures for changing a corporation’s registered office or registered agent).

[#MBCA502a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.02(a) (a corporation may change its registered office or agent by filing a statement of change that identifies the corporation, current and new registered office addresses, current and new agent (with written consent), and confirms that the registered office and agent’s business office will share the same address after the change).

[#MBCA502b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.02(b) (if a registered agent’s own business address changes, the agent must notify each affected corporation and file a combined statement of change, certifying that the corporations have been notified).

[#MBCA502cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.02 Official Comment (changes of office or agent are routine and should not require amending articles or obtaining board or shareholder approval; this section centralizes notice and keeps the public record current at low transaction cost).

[#MBCA503]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03 (allows a registered agent to resign and, in effect, discontinue the registered office by following a simple filing and notice procedure).

[#MBCA503a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03(a) (a registered agent resigns by filing a signed statement of resignation that identifies the corporation, the agent, states the resignation, and gives the address where the corporation will be notified).

[#MBCA503b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03(b) (a resignation becomes effective at the earlier of: (1) 12:01 a.m. on the 31st day after filing; or (2) the corporation’s designation of a new registered agent).

[#MBCA503c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03(c) (the resigning agent must promptly notify the corporation of the date the resignation statement was delivered for filing).

[#MBCA503d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03(d) (once the resignation is effective, the former agent has no further statutory responsibilities as agent; the resignation does not affect any separate contractual rights between the corporation and the agent).

[#MBCA503e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03(e) (an agent may resign regardless of whether the corporation is in good standing).

[#MBCA503cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.03 Official Comment (this section facilitates orderly disengagement by agents and permits discontinuation of the registered office; corporations must then appoint a new agent or risk administrative consequences such as dissolution or termination of foreign registration).

[#MBCA504]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.04 (specifies primary and fallback methods for serving process, notices, and demands on corporations).

[#MBCA504a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.04(a) (the registered agent is the corporation’s agent for service of any process, notice, or demand required or permitted by law).

[#MBCA504b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.04(b) (if a corporation has no registered agent or the agent cannot with reasonable diligence be served, service may be made by registered or certified mail, return receipt requested, addressed to the secretary at the corporation’s principal office; service is effective when received, when the receipt is signed, or five days after mailing, whichever is earliest).

[#MBCA504c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.04(c) (if service cannot be made under subsections (a) or (b), or if the target is a withdrawn or administratively terminated registered foreign corporation, the secretary of state becomes the corporation’s agent for service; the secretary accepts duplicate copies, forwards one by registered or certified mail to the last recorded address, and service is effective when received, when the receipt is signed, or five days after the secretary mails it).

[#MBCA504d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.04(d) (the section’s service methods are nonexclusive; other statutes and procedural rules may provide additional or alternative means of service).

[#MBCA504cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 5.04 Official Comment (the section solves the “missing agent” problem by allowing mail service to the principal office and, failing that, service through the secretary of state, while preserving compatibility with general civil procedure and special service statutes).



[#MBCA601]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01 (requires articles to authorize classes and series of shares and sets baseline rules for voting, residual rights, preferences, and flexibility in share terms).

[#MBCA601a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01(a) (articles must state each authorized class and series and the number of shares of each; if more than one class or series, articles must give each a distinguishing designation and describe its terms, including preferences, rights, and limitations; shares within the same class or series must have identical terms unless varied under this section).

[#MBCA601b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01(b) (articles must authorize at least one class or series with full voting rights and at least one class or series, which may be the same, entitled to receive the net assets on dissolution).

[#MBCA601c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01(c) (articles may authorize one or more classes or series that: (1) have special, conditional, limited, or no voting rights; (2) are redeemable or convertible at specified times, by specified persons, for specified property, and at prices set or formula‑based; (3) carry distributions calculated in any manner; and (4) have distribution preferences, including on dissolution).

[#MBCA601d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01(d) (terms of shares may be made dependent on extrinsic, objectively ascertainable facts, consistent with § 1.20(k)).

[#MBCA601e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01(e) (terms of shares may vary among holders within a class or series if the variations are expressly stated in the articles).

[#MBCA601f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01(f) (the list of possible preferences, rights, and limitations in subsection (c) is non‑exhaustive).

[#MBCA601cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01 Official Comment (articles must define authorized share architecture; if there is only one class, it is understood to have voting and residual rights and need not be labeled “common”; multiple classes or series require clear allocation of rights before issuance).

[#MBCA601cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01 Official Comment (every corporation must always have authorized and, under § 6.03, outstanding shares that together have full voting rights and residual entitlement; the two characteristics may reside in one or be split across classes or series).

[#MBCA601cmt3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01 Official Comment (the statute permits broad customization: multiple or fractional votes, nonvoting shares, redemption and conversion features, and flexible dividend structures, subject to distribution constraints in § 6.40).

[#MBCA601cmt4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01 Official Comment (terms may be keyed to extrinsic facts such as market indices, interest rates, or currency ratios, and may vary by holder—for example, limiting voting rights above specified ownership thresholds).

[#MBCA601cmt5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.01 Official Comment (provides non‑exclusive examples of classes and series structures used in practice, emphasizing the enabling, rather than restrictive, nature of § 6.01).

[#MBCA602]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.02 (permits the board, when authorized by articles, to classify or reclassify unissued shares into new classes or series and to set their terms without shareholder approval, subject to filing an amendment).

[#MBCA602a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.02(a) (if the articles so provide, the board may: (1) classify unissued shares into one or more classes or series; (2) reclassify unissued shares of a class into one or more classes or series; or (3) reclassify unissued shares of a series into one or more classes or series).

[#MBCA602b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.02(b) (when acting under subsection (a), the board sets terms, including preferences, rights, and limitations, to the same extent permitted by § 6.01, for any new class or series before issuing shares of it).

[#MBCA602c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.02(c) (before issuing any shares of a class or series created or reclassified under § 6.02, the corporation must file articles of amendment specifying the terms determined by the board).

[#MBCA602cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.02 Official Comment (a “blank check” provision lets the board tailor new classes and series to market or transactional needs without shareholder votes; the required amendment to the articles creates a public record, and shareholder approval is not needed for that amendment).

[#MBCA603]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.03 (defines when shares are issued and outstanding and imposes a continuous requirement that some shares with voting and residual rights remain outstanding).

[#MBCA603a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.03(a) (a corporation may issue the number of shares of each class and series authorized in the articles; once issued, shares are “outstanding” until reacquired, redeemed, converted, or cancelled).

[#MBCA603b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.03(b) (reacquisition, redemption, or conversion of outstanding shares is subject to § 6.03(c) and the distribution limitations in § 6.40).

[#MBCA603c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.03(c) (while any shares are outstanding, there must always be at least one or more shares outstanding that together have full voting rights and at least one or more shares outstanding that together are entitled to receive net assets upon dissolution).

[#MBCA603cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.03 Official Comment (reacquired shares generally become authorized but unissued, unless the articles prohibit reissue under § 6.31; the continuous‑rights requirement prevents corporations from eliminating all voting or residual‑equity shares through redemptions and similar transactions).

[#MBCA604]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.04 (authorizes corporations to handle fractional share interests flexibly, including by cashing out or issuing scrip).

[#MBCA604a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.04(a) (a corporation may: (1) issue fractions of a share; (2) pay cash instead of issuing fractions; (3) issue scrip, certificated or uncertificated, exchangeable for full shares; or (4) dispose of fractional shares and remit proceeds to affected holders).

[#MBCA604b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.04(b) (scrip certificates must be conspicuously labeled “scrip” and contain the information required by § 6.25(b); bearer scrip is prohibited; for uncertificated scrip, the corporation must promptly deliver a written information statement).

[#MBCA604c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.04(c) (a fractional share carries all shareholder rights proportionally, including voting, dividends, and liquidation rights; scrip confers no such rights unless its terms expressly grant them).

[#MBCA604d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.04(d) (the board may condition scrip, including making it void if not exchanged by a specified date and authorizing sale of the underlying shares with proceeds payable to scripholders).

[#MBCA604cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.04 Official Comment (fractional interests commonly arise from stock splits, dividends, and reclassifications; the statute permits full‑right fractional shares but encourages practical alternatives such as cash‑outs or scrip arrangements that aggregate interests and reduce administrative burdens).

[#MBCA620]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.20 (governs enforceability, payment terms, and default remedies for preincorporation share subscription agreements).

[#MBCA620a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.20(a) (a preincorporation subscription is irrevocable for six months unless the agreement specifies a different period or all subscribers agree to revocation).

[#MBCA620b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.20(b) (unless the subscription specifies payment terms, the board sets them; calls for payment must be uniform as practicable within a class or series).

[#MBCA620c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.20(c) (shares issued on preincorporation subscriptions become fully paid and nonassessable when the corporation receives the agreed consideration).

[#MBCA620d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.20(d) (on subscriber default, the corporation may sue for the unpaid amount or, after 20 days’ written demand without cure and absent contrary agreement, may rescind and resell the shares).

[#MBCA620cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.20 Official Comment (provides clear default rules making preincorporation subscriptions enforceable by the formed corporation; addresses irrevocability period, effect of acceptance, and interaction with later cancellation or nonpayment issues).

[#MBCA621]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21 (defines permissible consideration, board’s adequacy determination, cancellation mechanics, and shareholder‑approval triggers for large non‑cash issuances).

[#MBCA621a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(a) (the articles may reserve to shareholders, rather than the board, the power to authorize issuances).

[#MBCA621b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(b) (board may authorize issuance for any tangible or intangible benefit to the corporation, including cash, notes, performed or future services, contracts for services, or the corporation’s own securities).

[#MBCA621c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(c) (before issuing, the board must determine that consideration is adequate; that determination is conclusive as to whether shares are validly issued, fully paid, and nonassessable).

[#MBCA621d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(d) (upon receipt of the authorized consideration, the shares issued are fully paid and nonassessable).

[#MBCA621e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(e) (for shares issued for future services, benefits, or notes, the corporation may escrow or restrict the shares, credit distributions against the price, and, on nonperformance, cancel the shares and credited distributions).

[#MBCA621f1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(f)(1) (shareholder approval is required for non‑cash or mixed‑consideration issuances (including convertible securities or rights) if, in a transaction or integrated series, the resulting voting power exceeds 20 percent of the pre‑transaction voting power).

[#MBCA621f2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21(f)(2) (defines how to measure voting power for purposes of subsection (f), including counting shares issuable on conversion or exercise and defining when multiple transactions are “integrated”).

[#MBCA621cmt1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21 Official Comment (rejects par‑value/stated‑capital concepts; validates broad forms of consideration, relies on board fiduciary duties for adequacy, and treats the board’s determination as conclusive for paid‑up status).

[#MBCA621cmt2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21 Official Comment (explains escrow and cancellation of shares issued for future performance as a rescission‑type remedy, leaving other remedies and third‑party rights primarily to general law and the UCC).

[#MBCA621cmt3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.21 Official Comment (details the 20‑percent non‑cash issuance voting rule, including treatment of contingent issuances, earn‑outs, antidilution adjustments, and integration principles).

[#MBCA622]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.22 (confirms limited payment obligation of purchasers from the corporation and codifies general shareholder nonliability for corporate debts).

[#MBCA622a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.22(a) (a purchaser of shares from the corporation is liable only to pay the agreed consideration or subscription price; no further liability to the corporation or its creditors with respect to those shares).

[#MBCA622b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.22(b) (shareholders are not personally liable for corporate obligations solely by virtue of being shareholders, subject to any express liability in the articles and any personal obligations they separately assume).

[#MBCA622cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.22 Official Comment (confines a shareholder’s exposure to the unpaid issue price; leaves questions about unpaid consideration, transferees, and good‑faith purchasers to commercial law, especially the UCC).

[#MBCA623]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.23 (authorizes share dividends, defines them as pro rata, no‑consideration issuances, and regulates cross‑class share dividends).

[#MBCA623a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.23(a) (unless the articles provide otherwise, the corporation may issue pro rata, no‑consideration share dividends to all shareholders or to one or more classes or series).

[#MBCA623b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.23(b) (shares of one class or series may not be distributed as share dividends on another class or series unless authorized in the articles, approved by a majority of the votes of the issuing class or series, or there are no outstanding shares of the issuing class or series).

[#MBCA623c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.23(c) (the board may set a non‑retroactive record date for share dividends; otherwise the record date is the authorization date).

[#MBCA623cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.23 Official Comment (treats share dividends as purely intra‑equity adjustments, not “distributions” of corporate assets, while tying mechanics such as record date and fractional‑share handling to other share provisions).

[#MBCA624]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.24 (governs issuance and structuring of rights, options, warrants, and equity‑based awards, including “poison pill”‑style features and delegated award programs).

[#MBCA624a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.24(a) (a corporation may issue rights, options, or warrants to purchase shares or other securities; the board sets the terms, including exercise consideration, and its authorization also authorizes the underlying issuances).

[#MBCA624b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.24(b) (terms may include ownership‑ or acquisition‑based variations, such as scaled exercise prices, different terms for large holders, and limitations linked to specified ownership thresholds).

[#MBCA624c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.24(c) (the board may delegate to officers authority to issue rights or awards as compensation within limits and terms set by the board, including the maximum number and type of securities, eligible recipients, and general award terms).

[#MBCA624cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.24 Official Comment (confirms the statutory basis for complex option and rights structures, including shareholder‑rights plans, and clarifies permitted officer‑level delegation for routine compensatory issuances).

[#MBCA625]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25 (specifies minimum form and informational requirements for share certificates and confirms parity of rights between certificated and uncertificated shares).

[#MBCA625a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25(a) (shares may but need not be certificated; bearer certificates are prohibited; certificated and uncertificated shares carry identical substantive rights).

[#MBCA625b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25(b) (each certificate must state the corporate name and state of organization, the shareholder’s name, and the number, class, and series designation of the shares).

[#MBCA625c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25(c) (if multiple classes or series exist, certificates must either summarize key terms, including variations and board “blank check” authority, or conspicuously state that the corporation will provide that information on written request without charge).

[#MBCA625d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25(d) (certificates must be signed by two officers designated in the bylaws).

[#MBCA625e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25(e) (a certificate remains valid even if the signing officer has left office before issuance).

[#MBCA625cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.25 Official Comment (implements minimal, notice‑oriented certificate formalities; permits facsimile signatures; and preserves equivalence between certificated and uncertificated holdings apart from transfer mechanics).

[#MBCA626]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.26 (authorizes uncertificated shares and requires delivery of an information statement in lieu of a certificate).

[#MBCA626a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.26(a) (unless the articles or bylaws provide otherwise, the board may authorize some or all shares of any class or series to be uncertificated; existing certificates remain effective until surrendered).

[#MBCA626b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.26(b) (after issuing or transferring uncertificated shares, the corporation must promptly send the holder a written statement containing the information required on certificates and any transfer‑restriction notation required by § 6.27).

[#MBCA626cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.26 Official Comment (facilitates book‑entry systems while ensuring holders receive the same substantive notice as certificate owners; bars treating certificated shares as uncertificated until the certificate is surrendered).

[#MBCA627]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27 (authorizes, and regulates notice and enforceability of, restrictions on transfer or registration of transfer of shares).

[#MBCA627a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27(a) (restrictions may be imposed by articles, bylaws, shareholder agreements, or shareholder‑corporation agreements; they do not bind pre‑restriction shares unless affected holders are parties or voted in favor).

[#MBCA627b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27(b) (a restriction is enforceable against a holder or transferee only if authorized by § 6.27 and noted conspicuously on a certificate or included in the § 6.26(b) information statement; otherwise it is ineffective against persons without knowledge).

[#MBCA627c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27(c) (authorizes restrictions to: maintain status dependent on shareholder number or identity, preserve securities‑law exemptions, or advance any other reasonable purpose).

[#MBCA627d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27(d) (permissible restrictions include rights of first offer, mandatory buy‑sell obligations, approval‑rights regimes, and prohibitions on transfers to specified persons or classes so long as not manifestly unreasonable).

[#MBCA627e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27(e) (for this section, “shares” includes securities convertible into or carrying rights to acquire shares).

[#MBCA627cmt]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.27 Official Comment (endorses broad, reasonableness‑bounded use of transfer restrictions, especially in closely held firms and for tax, regulatory, or listing‑status reasons, while requiring clear notice for enforceability).

[#MBCA630]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.30 (provides an opt‑in regime for shareholder preemptive rights and a default model of such rights when elected).

[#MBCA630a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.30(a) (shareholders have no preemptive rights unless the articles affirmatively provide for them).

[#MBCA630b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.30(b)(1) (an election of preemptive rights in the articles gives shareholders, on uniform, fair, and reasonable terms set by the board, a right to acquire proportional amounts of unissued shares when the board decides to issue them).

[#MBCA630b2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.30(b)(2) (a shareholder may waive preemptive rights; a written waiver is irrevocable even without consideration).

[#MBCA630b3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.30(b)(3) (no preemptive rights exist with respect to: (i) shares issued as compensation to directors, officers, employees, or agents of the corporation or its affiliates; (ii) shares issued on exercise of compensatory options or conversion rights; (iii) shares authorized in the articles and issued within six months after incorporation; or (iv) shares sold otherwise than for cash).

[#MBCA630b4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 6.30(b)(4) (holders of nonvoting but distribution‑preferred shares have no preemptive rights with respect to any shares).
