Act § 9.33 (converting entity files articles stating converting and converted entities, their jurisdictions and types, reciting approval, and attaching public organic record for domestic converted entity; effectiveness governed by section 1.23 with special rules for foreign converted entities; foreign converting entity's registration automatically cancelled).

[#MBCA934]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 9.34 (amendment and abandonment of conversion).

[#MBCA934]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 9.34 (plan may be amended as originally approved or as plan provides; material adverse changes require renewed shareholder consent; board may abandon before effectiveness without shareholder action, including by filing articles of abandonment).

[#MBCA935]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 9.35 (effect of conversion).

[#MBCA935]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 9.35 (converted entity is same entity as converting entity; all property, rights, liabilities, and proceedings continue without transfer or impairment; preserves appraisal enforcement against foreign converted entities via secretary-of-state agency; interest holder liability preserved or cut off using before-after effectiveness framework).



[#MBCA1001]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.01 (authority to amend articles).

[#MBCA1001a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.01(a) (corporation may amend articles at any time to add or change provision not required to be in articles, or to delete provision not required to be in articles).

[#MBCA1001b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.01(b) (shareholder approval required unless section 10.05 board-only amendment applies).

[#MBCA1002]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.02 (amendment by board and shareholders).

[#MBCA1002a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.02(a) (board must adopt proposed amendment unless section 10.05 applies).

[#MBCA1002b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.02(b) (board must recommend amendment to shareholders unless conflicts or section 8.26 justify withholding recommendation; basis for not recommending must be disclosed).

[#MBCA1002c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.02(c) (board may condition shareholder approval or amendment effectiveness).

[#MBCA1002d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.02(d) (corporation must give shareholders entitled to vote notice stating purpose includes amendment consideration; notice must include or summarize proposed amendment).

[#MBCA1002e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.02(e) (default approval requires majority of votes entitled to be cast plus separate majority of each voting group entitled to vote separately unless articles require greater vote).

[#MBCA1003]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.03 (amendment by board).

[#MBCA1003a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.03(a) (board may adopt specified amendments without shareholder approval if no shares issued).

[#MBCA1003b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.03(b) (if shares issued and amendment would not require shareholder approval under section 10.04, board may adopt if permitted by subsection (c) or section 6.02).

[#MBCA1003c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.03(c) (board may condition amendment's effectiveness on facts, including third-party approvals).

[#MBCA1004]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.04 (voting on amendments by voting groups).

[#MBCA1004a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.04(a) (holders of shares of class or series entitled to vote as separate voting group on proposed amendment if amendment would exchange or reclassify shares, change rights or preferences, create senior class, limit preemptive rights, cancel distributions, dissolve redemption rights, alter conversion terms, or impose interest holder liability).

[#MBCA1004b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.04(b) (separate voting-group rights extend to series if amendment affects series in manner described in subsection (a)).

[#MBCA1004c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.04(c) (if amendment affects two or more classes or series in same or substantially similar way, holders vote together as single voting group unless articles provide otherwise or board adds voting-group condition).

[#MBCA1004d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.04(d) (class or series has voting rights under this section even if articles describe shares as nonvoting).

[#MBCA1005]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.05 (amendment by board without shareholder approval).

[#MBCA1005]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.05 (board may adopt without shareholder approval ministerial or technical amendments including extending formerly limited duration, deleting initial-director or registered-office data, effecting share splits or share-dividend increases in single-class corporation, conforming name format, and adjusting share-count provisions after reissue prohibited and shares acquired under section 6.31(b)).

[#MBCA1006]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.06 (articles of amendment).

[#MBCA1006]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.06 (articles of amendment must state corporation's name, text of each amendment or section 1.20(k)(5) information, implementation provisions for exchanges or reclassifications, and approval confirmation; effectiveness governed by section 1.23).

[#MBCA1007]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.07 (restated articles of incorporation).

[#MBCA1007a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.07(a) (board may restate articles at any time to consolidate prior amendments into single document).

[#MBCA1007b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.07(b) (shareholder approval required if restatement itself includes new amendments).

[#MBCA1007c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.07(c) (articles of restatement must state corporation's name, whether restatement includes amendments requiring shareholder approval, and full text of restated articles; may state no new amendments included).

[#MBCA1008]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.08 (amendment pursuant to reorganization).

[#MBCA1008]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.08 (court-ordered plan-of-reorganization amendments under federal law may be implemented via articles filed by court-designated person without board or shareholder action).

[#MBCA1009]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.09 (effect of amendment).

[#MBCA1009a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.09(a) (amendment does not affect existing causes of action or proceedings; name change does not affect proceedings in former name).

[#MBCA1009b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.09(b) (shareholder who becomes subject to new interest holder liability has that liability only for post-amendment obligations).

[#MBCA1009c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.09(c) (for shareholder with interest holder liability before and after amendment, prior liability not discharged for pre-amendment obligations; prior provisions continue for collection, contribution rights preserved, and no liability for post-amendment obligations by reason of prior liability).


[#MBCA1020]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.20 (authority to amend bylaws).

[#MBCA1020a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.20(a) (shareholders may amend or repeal corporation's bylaws).

[#MBCA1020b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.20(b) (board may amend or repeal bylaws unless articles reserve power to shareholders or shareholders restrict board amendment authority in exercise of power reserved to shareholders, consistent with section 2.06(d) for proxy-access and reimbursement bylaws).

[#MBCA1020c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.20(c) (bylaw provision does not give shareholders vested property right).

[#MBCA1021]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.21 (bylaw-level changes to director quorum and voting).

[#MBCA1021a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.21(a) (bylaw increasing board quorum or voting requirement may be amended or repealed by shareholders if originally adopted by shareholders unless bylaw provides otherwise, or by shareholders or board if adopted by board).

[#MBCA1021b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.21(b) (bylaw adopted or amended by shareholders that increases quorum or voting requirement may specify it can be amended or repealed only by specified vote of shareholders or board).

[#MBCA1021c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.21(c) (board action to amend or repeal bylaw changing quorum or voting requirement must meet same quorum and be adopted by same vote as then in effect or proposed, whichever greater).

[#MBCA1022]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.22 (bylaw provisions on director elections).

[#MBCA1022a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.22(a) (unless articles prohibit, alter section 7.28(a) vote, or provide cumulative voting, corporation may elect in bylaws to allow votes for or against candidates and require plurality for election, but nominee receiving more against than for serves only 90 days or until board fills office).

[#MBCA1022b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.22(b) (subsection (a) does not apply if at determination date there are more candidates than directorships, one or more properly proposed by shareholders, unless board determines candidacy does not create bona fide election contest).

[#MBCA1022c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 10.22(c) (bylaw electing to be governed by section 10.22 may be repealed only by shareholders if originally adopted by shareholders unless bylaw provides otherwise, or by board or shareholders if adopted by board).


[#MBCA1101]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.01 (chapter 11 definitions).

[#MBCA1101]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.01 (defines acquired entity, acquiring entity, new interest holder liability, party to a merger, and survivor for purposes of chapter 11).

[#MBCA1102]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02 (merger authorized).

[#MBCA1102a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02(a) (domestic corporations may merge with each other, with foreign corporations, or with domestic or foreign eligible entities, subject to organic law of foreign or eligible entities).

[#MBCA1102b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02(b) (allows merger of foreign entities to create new domestic corporation survivor).

[#MBCA1102c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02(c) (domestic eligible entity may participate in merger using this section's procedures if its organic law does not prohibit or supply approval procedures).

[#MBCA1102d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02(d) (plan of merger must specify parties to merger, survivor's name and jurisdiction, consideration or conversion terms for shares and eligible interests, and organic documents as amended or full text of new organic documents).

[#MBCA1102e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02(e) (plan terms may depend on section 1.20(k) extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA1102f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.02(f) (plan may be amended if parties consent and shareholders provide renewed consent for materially adverse changes; plan or board action may authorize plan abandonment).

[#MBCA1103]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.03 (share exchange authorized).

[#MBCA1103a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.03(a) (domestic corporation or eligible entity may acquire all shares or eligible interests of one or more classes or series of another domestic corporation, foreign corporation if its organic law permits, or domestic or foreign eligible entity if its organic law does not prohibit).

[#MBCA1103b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.03(b) (domestic eligible entity may participate in share exchange using this section's procedures if its organic law does not prohibit or supply approval procedures).

[#MBCA1103c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.03(c) (plan of share exchange must specify parties, classes or series to be acquired, consideration or conversion terms, and organic document amendments for acquired entity if domestic).

[#MBCA1103d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.03(d) (plan terms may depend on section 1.20(k) extrinsic facts).

[#MBCA1103e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.03(e) (plan may be amended if parties consent and shareholders provide renewed consent for materially adverse changes; plan or board action may authorize abandonment).

[#MBCA1104]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04 (action on plan of merger or share exchange).

[#MBCA1104a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(a) (board must adopt plan of merger or share exchange).

[#MBCA1104b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(b) (board must recommend plan to shareholders unless conflicts or section 8.26 justifies withholding recommendation or unless subsections (h), (j), or (l) or section 11.05 applies; basis for not recommending must be disclosed).

[#MBCA1104c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(c) (board may condition shareholder approval or plan effectiveness).

[#MBCA1104d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(d) (meeting notice must state plan consideration purpose, include or summarize plan, and attach or summarize survivor's and any new entity's articles or organic rules).

[#MBCA1104e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(e) (default approval requires majority of votes entitled to be cast plus separate majority by each voting group entitled to vote separately unless articles require greater vote).

[#MBCA1104f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(f) (separate voting-group approval required when merger converts class or series into other consideration or when plan includes amendment requiring separate vote under section 10.04; in share exchange, each class or series being acquired votes separately).

[#MBCA1104g]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(g) (articles may eliminate separate voting-group rights for class or series in mergers or share exchanges effecting substantive business combinations, but not when plan includes amendments requiring separate vote under section 10.04).

[#MBCA1104h]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(h) (shareholder approval not required when corporation will survive, articles remain unchanged except as permitted by section 10.05, shareholders retain identical shares, and no section 6.21(f) vote required for merger share issuances).

[#MBCA1104i]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(i) (shareholders newly subject to interest holder liability must provide separate written consent unless new terms substantially identical or reduce liability).

[#MBCA1104j]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(j) (permits two-step transaction without shareholder vote when offeror makes offer open at least 10 days, acquires sufficient shares to satisfy vote otherwise required, and second-step merger or share exchange provides same consideration as first step).

[#MBCA1104k]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(k) (defines parent and wholly owned subsidiary for purposes of subsections (h) and (j) and section 11.05).

[#MBCA1104l]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.04(l) (shareholder approval not required for acquiring entity in share exchange).

[#MBCA1105]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.05 (merger between parent and subsidiary or between subsidiaries).

[#MBCA1105a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.05(a) (parent owning at least 90% of voting power of each class and series of subsidiary's shares may merge subsidiary into itself or another subsidiary, or itself into subsidiary, without subsidiary board or shareholder approval by adopting plan setting forth manner and basis of merger and articles for survivor if domestic).

[#MBCA1105b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.05(b) (parent must mail notice to subsidiary shareholders within 10 days after merger effectiveness).

[#MBCA1105c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.05(c) (section 11.04(i) applies to parent-subsidiary mergers).

[#MBCA1106]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.06 (articles of merger or share exchange).

[#MBCA1106]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.06 (after proper approval, party files articles stating parties' names, jurisdiction, and entity type, survivor's name and type or statement that new entity being created, confirmation of proper approval, and full text of any new or amended articles or public organic record; effectiveness governed by section 1.23 with special timing when survivor or acquiring entity is foreign).

[#MBCA1107]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07 (effect of merger or share exchange).

[#MBCA1107a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07(a) (upon effectiveness, non-surviving parties' separate existence ceases; survivor or newly created entity continues or comes into existence; all property, rights, liabilities, and proceedings vest in or continue against survivor by operation of law; creditor rights and liens unimpaired).

[#MBCA1107b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07(b) (shares converted as provided in plan; in share exchange, acquired shares exchanged as provided).

[#MBCA1107c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07(c) (all rights and privileges of non-survivors vest in survivor).

[#MBCA1107d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07(d) (preserves appraisal enforcement against foreign survivor via secretary-of-state agency).

[#MBCA1107e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07(e) (shareholder newly subject to interest holder liability has that liability only for obligations arising after merger effectiveness).

[#MBCA1107f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.07(f) (for shareholder with interest holder liability before and after merger, prior liability not discharged for pre-merger obligations, prior provisions continue to apply, contribution rights preserved, and shareholder does not have liability for post-merger obligations by reason of prior liability).

[#MBCA1108]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.08 (abandonment of merger or share exchange).

[#MBCA1108]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 11.08 (domestic corporation that is party to plan may abandon transaction after adoption and approval but before effectiveness, without shareholder action, on terms of plan or by board unless plan prohibits abandonment).


[#MBCA1201]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.01 (disposition of assets not requiring shareholder approval).

[#MBCA1201]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.01 (shareholder approval not required, unless articles otherwise provide, for sales, leases, exchanges, or dispositions in usual and regular course of business, mortgages or encumbrances regardless of whether in usual and regular course, transfers to wholly owned subsidiaries, or pro rata distributions to holders of one or more classes or series).

[#MBCA1202]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02 (shareholder approval of certain dispositions).

[#MBCA1202a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(a) (shareholder approval required for disposition of assets not covered by section 12.01 if disposition would leave corporation without significant continuing business activity; safe harbor conclusively deems retention of significant continuing business activity if corporation retains at least 25% of total assets and either 25% of income from continuing operations before taxes or 25% of revenues from continuing operations, measured on consolidated basis as of end of most recently completed fiscal year).

[#MBCA1202b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(b) (board must adopt resolution authorizing disposition and recommend approval to shareholders, unless conflicts or section 8.26 justify withholding recommendation, in which case basis must be disclosed).

[#MBCA1202c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(c) (board may condition shareholder approval or effectiveness of disposition).

[#MBCA1202d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(d) (for approval at meeting, notice to all shareholders must state that meeting will consider disposition and describe disposition, including terms, conditions, and consideration to be received).

[#MBCA1202e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(e) (default approval requires majority of votes entitled to be cast at meeting with quorum present unless higher thresholds imposed).

[#MBCA1202f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(f) (disposition may be abandoned after shareholder approval but before consummation, without further shareholder action, subject to contractual rights of other parties).

[#MBCA1202g]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(g) (dispositions in course of dissolution under chapter 14 not governed by section 12.02).

[#MBCA1202h]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 12.02(h) (assets of direct or indirect consolidated subsidiaries deemed to be assets of parent corporation for purposes of section 12.02).



[#MBCA1301]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.01 (chapter 13 definitions; defines key terms for appraisal including acquiror, affiliate, control, corporation, excluded shares, fair value, interested person, interested transaction, measurement date, shareholder, and voting power).

[#MBCA1301fairvalue]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.01 (fair value defined as the portion of corporate value attributable to the share, determined immediately before effectiveness of the corporate action, without discounts for lack of marketability or minority status).

[#MBCA1301interested]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.01 (interested person defined based on beneficial ownership of 15% or more of voting power, power to cause appointment of 15% or more of directors, or senior executives and directors who collectively own more than 5% of voting power).

[#MBCA1301interestedtxn]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.01 (interested transaction defined to identify conflict-of-interest scenarios including financial benefits to interested persons not generally available to shareholders, interested persons having voting power in acquiror, or board majorities with acquiror relationships or special benefits).

[#MBCA1301votingpower]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.01 (voting power defined as power to vote in election of directors or governors, to select or appoint directors or governors, or to vote on the corporate action giving rise to appraisal, with detailed attribution rules for aggregating beneficial ownership among related persons).

[#MBCA1302]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02 (right to appraisal; grants appraisal for interested-transaction mergers, share exchanges, domestications, conversions, and asset dispositions).

[#MBCA1302a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(a)(1) (appraisal available for interested-transaction mergers, share exchanges, domestications, conversions, and asset dispositions, except for shares that remain outstanding after merger or are not acquired in share exchange).

[#MBCA1302a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(a)(2) (appraisal available when there is an interested person for fractional-share amendments requiring the corporation to repurchase the resulting fractional shares).

[#MBCA1302a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(a)(3) (appraisal available in short-form mergers under § 11.05 when the corporation is the subsidiary, except for shares owned by the parent).

[#MBCA1302a4]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(a)(4) (appraisal available when shares become or are converted into eligible interests in mergers, share exchanges, domestications, conversions, or amendments, subject to market exception).

[#MBCA1302a5]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(a)(5) (appraisal available for asset dispositions under § 12.02 when consideration includes eligible interests, unless those interests will not be distributed to shareholders for at least one year, subject to market exception).

[#MBCA1302a6]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(a)(6) (articles of incorporation, bylaws, or board resolution may provide appraisal for other mergers, share exchanges, domestications, conversions, asset dispositions, or amendments).

[#MBCA1302b1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(b)(1) (market exception; appraisal not available under §§ 13.02(a)(4) or (5) for shares listed on national exchange, traded in organized market with at least 2,000 shareholders and $20 million market value, or redeemable mutual fund shares).

[#MBCA1302b3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(b)(3) (market exception inapplicable if shareholders must accept consideration other than cash or shares meeting market exception standards).

[#MBCA1302c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.02(c) (articles of incorporation may limit or eliminate appraisal for preferred shares with respect to actions on which the class or series votes, subject to specified conditions).

[#MBCA1303]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.03 (shares for which appraisal may be asserted; limits appraisal to shares owned as of effective time, requires continued ownership if shares remain outstanding, and when notice of intent required, restricts appraisal to shares owned as of notice date and continuously through effectiveness).

[#MBCA1304]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.04 (consequences of voting, consenting, or tendering; bars beneficial shareholder from appraisal if it voted, consented, or tendered shares of the same class or series in favor of the action, and bars voting trust beneficial owner from appraisal if any shares in the voting trust were so voted, consented, or tendered).


[#MBCA1320]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.20 (notice of appraisal rights; requires meeting notices, consent solicitations, or post-effective notices to state whether appraisal rights are, are not, or may be available).

[#MBCA1320b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.20(b) (when corporation concludes appraisal rights are or may be available, requires accompanying or making available financial statements for most recent year and latest interim period, plus copy of chapter 13, subject to shareholder waiver).

[#MBCA1321]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.21 (notice of intent to assert appraisal rights; requires shareholder wishing to assert appraisal for transaction submitted to vote or § 11.04(j) two-step offer to deliver notice of intent before vote or before shares purchased in offer).

[#MBCA1321b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.21(b) (notice of intent must be signed by record shareholder and specify beneficial shareholder or voting trust beneficial owner, record holder and intermediaries, voting trust identification, and number of shares for which appraisal intended).

[#MBCA1321c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.21(c) (identified beneficial shareholder or voting trust beneficial owner authorized to take subsequent appraisal actions and receive further notices).

[#MBCA1322]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.22 (appraisal notice and form; requires corporation to deliver appraisal notice and form within 10 days after effectiveness to specified shareholders).

[#MBCA1322recipients]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.22(a) (appraisal notice must be delivered to all shareholders who gave notice of intent, to nonconsenting or nonvoting shareholders if consent approval, or in short-form mergers and certain § 13.02(a)(6) cases to all record shareholders at effectiveness).

[#MBCA1322b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.22(b) (appraisal notice must include form requiring identifying information, representation that § 13.04 satisfied, optional request for acquisition date statement, and disclosure of first announcement date).

[#MBCA1322c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.22(c) (appraisal notice must state where to return form and deposit certificates, deadlines for returning form and withdrawing, corporation's fair value estimate, availability of additional information, and who may sign form).

[#MBCA1322d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.22(d) (appraisal notice must be accompanied by or make available copy of chapter 13).

[#MBCA1323]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.23 (assertion of appraisal rights, right to withdraw, restoration of rights; provides that to receive payment shareholder must by deadline return signed form, deposit certificates, and provide evidence of transfer or ownership).

[#MBCA1323b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.23(b) (shareholder may withdraw appraisal assertion by written notice to corporation by withdrawal deadline).

[#MBCA1323c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.23(c) (upon withdrawal, deemed withdrawal, or court determination of non-entitlement, restores shareholder's rights as if appraisal had not been asserted, except shares not treated as having had voting rights during appraisal period).

[#MBCA1324]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.24 (payment; except as provided in § 13.25, requires corporation within 30 days after form deadline to make cash payment to each entitled shareholder of corporation's fair value estimate plus interest).

[#MBCA1324b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.24(b) (payment must be accompanied by or make available financial statements, statement of corporation's fair value estimate, and statement that shareholder may demand further payment under § 13.26 within 30 days or be deemed to have accepted payment).

[#MBCA1324c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.24(c) (corporation may decline payment and give notice if it determines shareholder not entitled to assert appraisal or receive payment, with notice stating determination, right to contest under § 13.26 within 30 days, and including financial and fair value information).

[#MBCA1325]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.25 (after-acquired shares; if form requested acquisition-date statement, permits corporation to withhold payment for shares acquired after first-announcement date).

[#MBCA1325b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.25(b) (corporation must within 30 days after form deadline notify shareholders from whom payment withheld of withholding, fair value estimate, and right to demand payment or accept estimate within 30 days).

[#MBCA1325c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.25(c) (corporation must pay within 10 days after receiving acceptance or after demand deadline for shareholders who accepted estimate).

[#MBCA1326]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.26 (procedure if shareholder dissatisfied with payment or offer or denied payment; allows dissatisfied shareholder to notify corporation of shareholder's fair value estimate and demand that amount less any § 13.24 payment plus interest).

[#MBCA1326b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.26(b) (failure to notify corporation by deadline waives right to demand and entitles shareholder only to payment or estimate plus interest).

[#MBCA1326c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.26(c) (shareholder given notice under § 13.24(c) may notify corporation it contends it is entitled to payment and either accept § 13.24(b)(2) estimate or state own estimate and demand payment).

[#MBCA1326d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.26(d) (failure to notify by deadline deems shareholder to have waived contention and withdrawn from appraisal).


[#MBCA1330]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.30 (court action; if shareholder gives notice and makes demand under § 13.26 that remains unsettled, requires corporation within 60 days after demand deadline to commence judicial proceeding to determine fair value and related matters).

[#MBCA1330a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.30(a) (failure to commence proceeding within 60 days triggers payment obligation of demanded amount plus interest within 10 days).

[#MBCA1330b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.30(b) (corporation must make all beneficial shareholders or voting trust beneficial owners whose demands remain unsettled parties to proceeding, with exclusive jurisdiction in named court).

[#MBCA1330c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.30(c) (court has authority to appoint appraisers, parties entitled to discovery, no jury trial right, and court may not dismiss as to any person without approval on terms court deems just).

[#MBCA1330d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.30(d) (judgment for each entitled shareholder for amount by which fair value exceeds any § 13.24 payment plus interest on excess, or fair value plus interest for shares for which no payment made).

[#MBCA1331]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.31 (court costs and expenses; requires court to determine all court costs including appraisers' compensation and assess those costs against corporation, except court may assess costs against shareholders who acted arbitrarily, vexatiously, or not in good faith).

[#MBCA1331b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.31(b) (court may assess expenses of parties in amounts court finds equitable against corporation if it did not substantially comply with §§ 13.20, 13.22, 13.24, or 13.25, or against either party if that party acted arbitrarily, vexatiously, or not in good faith).

[#MBCA1331c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.31(c) (court may direct that shareholder expenses of substantial benefit to similarly situated shareholders be paid from amounts awarded to benefited shareholders).

[#MBCA1331d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 13.31(d) (shareholder may sue directly for required payments corporation failed to make and recover all suit expenses).



[#MBCA1401]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.01 (dissolution by incorporators or initial directors; permits incorporators or initial directors to dissolve corporation if no shares have been issued or business has not commenced).

[#MBCA1402]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.02 (dissolution by board and shareholders; for corporation with issued shares, requires board to propose dissolution and shareholders to approve).

[#MBCA1402a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.02(a) (board must adopt resolution proposing dissolution).

[#MBCA1402b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.02(b) (board must recommend dissolution to shareholders unless conflicts or § 8.26 justify not recommending, in which case basis must be disclosed).

[#MBCA1402c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.02(c) (board may condition shareholder approval or dissolution's effectiveness on specified terms).

[#MBCA1402d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.02(d) (requires notice to all shareholders stating meeting will consider dissolution).

[#MBCA1402e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.02(e) (sets default quorum and voting requirements: approval by majority of votes entitled to be cast at quorum-satisfied meeting, unless higher thresholds imposed).

[#MBCA1403]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.03 (articles of dissolution; after adoption and approval, requires filing articles stating corporation's name, dissolution's effective date, that dissolution authorized, and method of authorization).

[#MBCA1403c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.03(c) (corporation dissolved upon effective date of articles of dissolution or upon delayed date specified therein).

[#MBCA1403d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.03(d) (defines "dissolved corporation" as one whose dissolution has become effective, excluding administratively dissolved corporations).

[#MBCA1404]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.04 (revocation of dissolution; permits revocation before effectiveness by board action or within 120 days after effectiveness if revocation approved by board and shareholders, requiring filing of articles of revocation).

[#MBCA1405]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.05 (effect of dissolution; provides that dissolved corporation continues corporate existence but may not carry on business except to wind up and liquidate, and does not terminate registered agent's authority, abate proceedings, or change shareholders' rights).

[#MBCA1406]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.06 (known claims against dissolved corporation; requires dissolved corporation to notify known claimants in writing of dissolution and claims-filing deadline, with claims rejected or not timely filed barred).

[#MBCA1406b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.06(b) (notice must state deadline to file claim of not less than 120 days from notice date, provide mailing or delivery address, state claim will be barred if requirements not met, and for rejected claims include brief description and reason for rejection).

[#MBCA1406d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.06(d) (claim barred unless claimant commences proceeding within 90 days after rejection notice for claims rejected in whole or part, or by deadline stated in notice for other claims).

[#MBCA1407]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.07 (other claims against dissolved corporation; permits dissolved corporation to publish notice of dissolution and claims-filing deadline for unknown or contingent claimants).

[#MBCA1407b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.07(b) (published notice must describe required information for claims, provide mailing or delivery address, state claims will be barred unless proceeding commenced within three years after publication, and include corporation's name and dissolution date).

[#MBCA1407c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.07(c) (if dissolved corporation publishes notice, claim barred unless claimant commences proceeding within three years after publication).

[#MBCA1407d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.07(d) (unbarred claimants may enforce claims against dissolved corporation to extent of undistributed assets or against shareholders receiving liquidating distributions up to pro rata share of claim or amount received, whichever less).

[#MBCA1408]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.08 (court proceedings; permits dissolved corporation that published § 14.07 notice to file application for court determination of amount and form of security for contingent or unknown claims reasonably estimated to arise after dissolution).

[#MBCA1408d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.08(d) (provision for security in amount and form ordered by court satisfies dissolved corporation's obligations with respect to contingent, unknown, or post-effectiveness claims).

[#MBCA1409]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.09 (director duties; requires directors to cause dissolved corporation to discharge or make reasonable provision for claims and make liquidating distributions after payment or provision for claims).

[#MBCA1409b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.09(b) (directors not liable under subsection (a) with respect to claims disposed of under §§ 14.06, 14.07, or 14.08).


[#MBCA1420]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.20 (grounds for administrative dissolution; secretary of state may commence proceeding if corporation does not pay fees or taxes within 60 days, does not deliver annual report within 60 days, is without registered agent or office for 60 days or more, fails to notify of agent or office changes within 60 days, or period of duration expires).

[#MBCA1421]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.21 (procedure for and effect of administrative dissolution; requires secretary of state to provide notice and 60-day cure period before filing certificate of dissolution).

[#MBCA1421c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.21(c) (administratively dissolved corporation continues existence but may not carry on business except to wind up and liquidate and notify claimants).

[#MBCA1421d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.21(d) (administrative dissolution does not terminate authority of registered agent).

[#MBCA1422]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.22 (reinstatement following administrative dissolution; permits corporation to apply for reinstatement within two years after dissolution by delivering application, filing annual reports, paying fees and penalties, and demonstrating cure or nonexistence of dissolution grounds).

[#MBCA1422c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.22(c) (if secretary of state approves reinstatement, files application and issues certificate of reinstatement, dissolution is deemed never to have occurred).

[#MBCA1423]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.23 (appeal from denial of reinstatement; permits corporation to appeal denial to specified court within 30 days).


[#MBCA1430]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.30 (grounds for judicial dissolution; permits court to dissolve corporation in proceeding by attorney general for fraud or ultra vires acts, by shareholder for deadlock or oppressive conduct, by creditor if judgment unsatisfied or admitted debt and insolvency, by corporation to continue voluntary dissolution under supervision, or by shareholder if corporation abandoned business and failed to liquidate).

[#MBCA1430a1]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.30(a)(1) (attorney general may seek dissolution if corporation obtained articles through fraud or has continued to exceed or abuse authority conferred by law).

[#MBCA1430a2]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.30(a)(2) (shareholder may seek dissolution if directors deadlocked, directors or controllers acting illegally, oppressively, or fraudulently, shareholders deadlocked in voting for at least two consecutive annual meeting dates, or corporate assets being misapplied or wasted).

[#MBCA1430a3]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.30(a)(3) (creditor may seek dissolution if claim reduced to judgment and execution returned unsatisfied and corporation insolvent, or corporation admitted in writing claim is due and owing and is insolvent).

[#MBCA1430b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.30(b) (§ 14.30(a)(2) available only for corporation that does not have shares listed on national exchange, does not have 300 or more shareholders, or does not meet § 14.30(b)(3) asset and revenue thresholds).

[#MBCA1430c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.30(c) (beneficial shareholders and unrestricted voting trust beneficial owners may seek dissolution under § 14.30(a)(2)).

[#MBCA1431]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.31 (procedure for judicial dissolution; specifies venue, provides that shareholders need not be made parties unless relief sought against them individually, and permits court to issue injunctions, appoint receiver or custodian, or take other action to preserve assets).

[#MBCA1431d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.31(d) (within 10 days of commencing § 14.30(a)(2) proceeding, corporation must deliver notice to all shareholders except petitioner stating shareholders entitled to avoid dissolution by electing to purchase under § 14.34).

[#MBCA1432]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.32 (receivership or custodianship; unless election to purchase filed under § 14.34, permits court to appoint receiver to wind up and liquidate or custodian to manage business and affairs).

[#MBCA1432c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.32(c) (court shall describe powers and duties of receiver or custodian in appointing order, which may be amended from time to time).

[#MBCA1433]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.33 (decree of dissolution; after hearing determines grounds exist, court enters decree specifying effective date, and clerk delivers certified copy to secretary of state for filing).

[#MBCA1433b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.33(b) (court shall direct winding-up and liquidation under § 14.05 and notification of claimants under §§ 14.06 and 14.07).

[#MBCA1434]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34 (election to purchase in lieu of dissolution; in § 14.30(a)(2) proceeding, permits corporation or other shareholders to elect to purchase all shares owned by petitioning shareholder at fair value).

[#MBCA1434a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34(a) (election irrevocable unless court determines equitable to set aside or modify).

[#MBCA1434b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34(b) (election may be filed within 90 days after petition filed or at later time court allows).

[#MBCA1434c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34(c) (after election filed, petitioner and electing parties have 60 days to agree on fair value, and if agreement reached, court enters order directing purchase on agreed terms).

[#MBCA1434d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34(d) (if parties unable to reach agreement, any party may apply to court to determine fair value).

[#MBCA1434e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34(e) (upon determining fair value, court enters order directing purchase on terms court deems appropriate, which may include installments, security, and allocation among shareholders).

[#MBCA1434f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.34(f) (upon entry of order under subsections (c) or (e), court dismisses dissolution petition and petitioning shareholder no longer has shareholder rights or status except right to receive amounts awarded).


[#MBCA1440]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 14.40 (deposit with state treasurer; assets of dissolved corporation that should be transferred to creditor, claimant, or shareholder who cannot be found or is not competent shall be reduced to cash and deposited with state treasurer for safekeeping).



[#MBCA1501]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.01 (registration required; foreign corporation shall not do business in this state until it registers with secretary of state).

[#MBCA1502]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.02 (consequences of doing business without registration; foreign corporation doing business without registration may not maintain proceeding in state courts until registered, successors and assignees also barred, but state may defend proceeding brought against it, failure to register does not impair contract validity or prevent corporation from defending proceeding, and limitations period not tolled during nonregistration).

[#MBCA1503]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.03 (foreign registration statement; to register, foreign corporation must deliver statement to secretary of state setting forth corporate name, jurisdiction of formation, date of formation, principal office address, registered office and agent information, names and addresses of directors and principal officers, and brief description of nature of business to be conducted).

[#MBCA1504]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.04 (amendment of foreign registration statement; when information changes, foreign corporation must deliver amended statement within required time).

[#MBCA1505]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.05 (activities not constituting doing business; lists activities that do not require registration including maintaining accounts, maintaining offices for securities transfers, creating or acquiring indebtedness, conducting isolated transactions, and other specified activities).

[#MBCA1505m]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.05(m) (activities not constituting doing business include conducting affairs in furtherance of interstate or foreign commerce).

[#MBCA1506]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.06 (noncomplying name of foreign corporation; if name does not comply with § 4.01, foreign corporation may not register until it adopts alternate name complying with § 4.01 for purpose of doing business in this state).

[#MBCA1506a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.06(a) (foreign corporation adopting alternate name need not file under assumed or fictitious name statute with respect to that alternate name, and after registration may do business under alternate name, foreign corporation's name with jurisdiction added, or name authorized under assumed name statute).

[#MBCA1506b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.06(b) (if registered foreign corporation changes name to one not complying with § 4.01, it may not do business until it amends registration to adopt complying alternate name).


[#MBCA1507]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.07 (withdrawal of registration; registered foreign corporation may withdraw by delivering statement of withdrawal to secretary of state stating corporation not doing business in state, withdraws registration, and revokes registered agent's authority, with address for service of process).

[#MBCA1507b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.07(b) (after withdrawal, service of process in proceeding based on cause of action arising during registration may be made as provided in § 5.04).

[#MBCA1508]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.08 (deemed withdrawal upon domestication or conversion to certain domestic entities; registered foreign corporation that domesticates to domestic business corporation or converts to domestic nonprofit corporation, filing entity, or limited liability partnership is deemed to have withdrawn registration on effectiveness of such event).

[#MBCA1509]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.09 (withdrawal upon dissolution or conversion to certain nonfiling entities; registered foreign corporation that has dissolved and completed winding up or converted to nonfiling entity other than limited liability partnership must deliver statement of withdrawal).

[#MBCA1509a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.09(a) (statement of withdrawal must state name and jurisdiction, that it withdraws registration and revokes registered agent's authority, and address for service of process).

[#MBCA1509b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.09(b) (after withdrawal, service of process in proceeding based on cause of action arising during registration may be made as provided in § 5.04).

[#MBCA1510]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.10 (transfer of registration; if registered foreign corporation merges into nonregistered foreign corporation or converts to foreign corporation required to register, foreign corporation must deliver transfer of registration statement to secretary of state).

[#MBCA1510b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.10(b) (on effective date of transfer statement, registration transfers without interruption to foreign corporation into which it merged or to which it converted).

[#MBCA1511]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.11 (administrative termination of registration; secretary of state may terminate registration if foreign corporation does not pay fees or taxes within 60 days, does not deliver annual report within 60 days, is without registered agent or office for 60 days or more, or fails to notify of changes within 60 days).

[#MBCA1511b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.11(b) (secretary of state may terminate by filing certificate of termination and delivering copy to registered agent or principal office).

[#MBCA1511c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.11(c) (certificate must state effective date at least 60 days after delivery and grounds for termination).

[#MBCA1511d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.11(d) (registration ceases on effective date unless foreign corporation cures each ground before that date, in which case secretary of state files statement that certificate is withdrawn).

[#MBCA1512]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 15.12 (action by attorney general; attorney general may maintain action to enjoin foreign corporation from doing business in violation of this Act).



[#MBCA1601]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.01 (corporate records; corporation shall maintain articles and bylaws as currently in effect, § 1.20(k)(5) notices to shareholders, written communications to shareholders for past three years, meeting minutes and action records, list of current directors and officers, most recent annual report, and current alphabetical record of shareholders by class or series showing address and share numbers).

[#MBCA1601b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.01(b) (corporation shall maintain annual financial statements for last three fiscal years or shorter period of existence and any related audit or other reports).

[#MBCA1601c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.01(c) (corporation shall maintain accounting records in form permitting preparation of financial statements).

[#MBCA1601d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.01(d) (shareholder record must include electronic mail address if shareholder provided it or consented to electronic communications).

[#MBCA1602]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02 (inspection rights of shareholders; shareholder entitled to inspect and copy records described in § 16.01(a) except board minutes during regular business hours at principal office with five business days' signed written notice).

[#MBCA1602a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02(a) (shareholder entitled to inspect and copy articles, bylaws, shareholder communications, and certain other records at principal office with five days' notice).

[#MBCA1602b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02(b) (shareholder entitled to inspect and copy financial statements, accounting records, board minutes excerpts, and shareholder record at reasonable location if requirements of subsection (c) met with five days' notice).

[#MBCA1602c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02(c) (shareholder may inspect and copy § 16.02(b) records only if demand made in good faith and for proper purpose, describes with reasonable particularity purpose and desired records, and records directly connected with purpose).

[#MBCA1602d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02(d) (corporation may impose reasonable restrictions on confidentiality, use, or distribution of § 16.02(b) records).

[#MBCA1602e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02(e) (person who becomes shareholder after notice record date but entitled to vote at meeting is entitled to obtain meeting notice and information from corporation).

[#MBCA1602f]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.02(f) (inspection right may not be abolished or limited by articles or bylaws).

[#MBCA1603]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.03 (scope of inspection right; shareholder may appoint agent or attorney to exercise inspection rights, corporation may satisfy copying right by furnishing copies by chosen means including electronic transmission, and may impose reasonable charge for costs).

[#MBCA1603c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.03(c) (corporation may satisfy demand to inspect shareholder record by providing list compiled no earlier than demand date).

[#MBCA1604]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.04 (court-ordered inspection; if corporation does not allow § 16.02(a) inspection, court may summarily order inspection at corporation's expense).

[#MBCA1604b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.04(b) (if corporation does not allow § 16.02(b) inspection within reasonable time, shareholder may apply for court order on expedited basis).

[#MBCA1604c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.04(c) (if court orders § 16.02(b) inspection, may impose reasonable restrictions on confidentiality and shall order corporation to pay shareholder's expenses unless corporation establishes good faith basis for refusal or required reasonable restrictions).

[#MBCA1605]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.05 (inspection rights of directors; director entitled to inspect and copy corporation's books, records, and documents at reasonable time to extent reasonably related to performance of duties but not for any other purpose or in manner violating duty to corporation).

[#MBCA1605b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.05(b) (court may order inspection at corporation's expense on expedited basis upon director's application if refused such inspection rights, and may order corporation to reimburse director's expenses).


[#MBCA1620]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.20 (financial statements for shareholders; upon written request, corporation shall deliver or make available annual financial statements for most recent fiscal year).

[#MBCA1620a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.20(a) (if financial statements prepared on GAAP basis, corporation shall deliver or make available those statements; if audited or reported upon by public accountant, report shall also be provided).

[#MBCA1620b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.20(b) (corporation shall deliver or make available financial statements within five business days of written request).

[#MBCA1620d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.20(d) (corporation may require requesting shareholder to agree to reasonable confidentiality restrictions, and may decline delivery if reasonably determines request not made in good faith or for proper purpose).

[#MBCA1620e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.20(e) (if corporation does not respond within five business days, shareholder may apply for court order on expedited basis; court may impose reasonable restrictions, and shall order corporation to pay shareholder's expenses unless corporation establishes it had reasonably required restrictions or determined request not made in good faith or for proper purpose).

[#MBCA1621]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.21 (annual report for secretary of state; each domestic corporation shall deliver annual report setting forth name, registered office and agent, principal office address, names and addresses of directors and principal officers, brief business description, and authorized and issued shares itemized by class and series).

[#MBCA1621b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.21(b) (each registered foreign corporation shall deliver annual report with similar information plus jurisdiction of formation and principal office in that jurisdiction if required there).

[#MBCA1621d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.21(d) (first annual report delivered between January 1 and April 1 of year following incorporation or registration; subsequent reports delivered between January 1 and April 1 of following years).

[#MBCA1621e]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 16.21(e) (if report does not contain required information, secretary of state shall notify corporation and return report; if corrected within 30 days, deemed timely filed).


[#MBCA1701]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.01 (application and definitions; corporation electing benefit corporation status subject to chapter's additional requirements).

[#MBCA1701a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.01(a) (corporation electing to be benefit corporation subject to this chapter in addition to other Act provisions).

[#MBCA1701b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.01(b) (defines "benefit corporation," "public benefit," "public benefit provision," and "responsible and sustainable manner").

[#MBCA1702]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.02 (name and share certificates; benefit corporation may but need not use that term in name; certificates must note benefit corporation status).

[#MBCA1703]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.03 (certain amendments and transactions requiring supermajority votes).

[#MBCA1703a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.03(a) (becoming benefit corporation or merging into one requires two-thirds vote).

[#MBCA1703b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.03(b) (terminating benefit corporation status or merging into non-benefit corporation requires two-thirds vote).

[#MBCA1704]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.04 (duties of directors; must act in responsible and sustainable manner and pursue public benefits).

[#MBCA1704a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.04(a) (director shall act in responsible and sustainable manner pursuing public benefits).

[#MBCA1704b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.04(b) (director shall consider stakeholder interests including shareholders, employees, customers, community, environment).

[#MBCA1704c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.04(c) (director not personally liable except as provided in § 8.31).

[#MBCA1704d]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.04(d) (director does not breach duty by good faith action consistent with responsible and sustainable manner even if harmful to short-term financial interests).

[#MBCA1705]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.05 (annual benefit report addressing efforts to operate responsibly and pursue public benefits).

[#MBCA1705a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.05(a) (report must include objectives, standards, factual information on progress, and performance assessment).

[#MBCA1705b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.05(b) (benefit corporation shall send report to shareholders within 120 days after fiscal year end).

[#MBCA1705c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.05(c) (benefit corporation shall post report on public website or provide on request).

[#MBCA1706]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.06 (shareholder rights of action to enforce director duties under chapter).

[#MBCA1706b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.06(b) (derivative suit requires ownership of at least five percent of class or $5 million market value at time of violation).

[#MBCA1706c]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 17.06(c) (suit may not be maintained if shareholding falls below threshold during pendency).


[#MBCA1801]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.01 (application to existing domestic corporations; Act applies to all domestic corporations in existence on effective date if power to amend or repeal statute under which incorporated was reserved).

[#MBCA1802]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.02 (application to existing foreign corporations; foreign corporation registered or authorized on effective date subject to Act, deemed registered, and not required to file new foreign registration statement).

[#MBCA1803]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.03 (saving provisions; Act does not affect pending actions or accrued rights before effective date).

[#MBCA1803a]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.03(a) (pending action or proceeding or right accrued before effective date not affected and may be completed or enforced as if Act not effective).

[#MBCA1803b]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.03(b) (if penalty or punishment reduced by Act, shall be imposed in accordance with Act if not already imposed).

[#MBCA1804]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.04 (severability; invalidity of provision or application does not affect other provisions or applications that can be given effect without invalid provision).

[#MBCA1805]: Model Bus. Corp. Act § 18.05 (repeal; earlier general corporation laws repealed).

[#R3RUE52]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 52 (2011) (stating measure of benefit from performance of services).

[#R3RUE53]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 53 (2011) (addressing measure of benefit from use of another's property).

[#R3RUE54]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 54 (2011) (permitting rescission and restitution).

[#R3RUE55]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 55 (2011) (allowing constructive trust).

[#R3RUE56]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 56 (2011) (permitting equitable lien).

[#R3RUE57]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 57 (2011) (allowing subrogation).

[#R3RUE58]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 58 (2011) (addressing tracing and restitution via rights in identifiable property).

[#R3RUE59]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 59 (2011) (defining benefit in restitution claims).

[#R3RUE60]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 60 (2011) (limiting restitution based on bona fide purchaser defense).

[#R3RUE61]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 61 (2011) (addressing effect of discharge in bankruptcy on restitution claims).

[#R3RUE62]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 62 (2011) (permitting laches defense to restitution claims).

[#R3RUE63]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 63 (2011) (addressing unclean hands defense).

[#R3RUE64]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 64 (2011) (permitting passing on defense when burden has been shifted to third parties).

[#R3RUE65]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 65 (2011) (allowing change of position defense).

[#R3RUE66]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 66 (2011) (limiting restitution against bona fide purchaser).

[#R3RUE67]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 67 (2011) (protecting bona fide payee).

[#R3RUE68]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 68 (2011) (defining value requirement for bona fide purchaser protection).

[#R3RUE69]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 69 (2011) (defining notice for bona fide purchaser defense).

[#R3RUE70]: American Law Institute, *Restatement (Third) of Restitution and Unjust Enrichment* § 70 (2011) (addressing statutes of limitation).




[#ULLCA101]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 101 (short title).

[#ULLCA102]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102 (definitions).

[#ULLCA102(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(1) (definition of "certificate of organization" as certificate required by § 201, including as amended or restated).

[#ULLCA102(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(2) (definition of "contribution" as property or benefit provided to become member or in member capacity).

[#ULLCA102(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(3) (definition of "debtor in bankruptcy" under federal or comparable insolvency law).

[#ULLCA102(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(4) (definition of "distribution" as transfer on account of transferable interest or member capacity).

[#ULLCA102(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(4)(A) (distribution includes redemption or purchase of transferable interest and transfer in return for relinquishment of participation rights).

[#ULLCA102(4)(A)(i)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(4)(A)(i) (distribution includes redemption or purchase of transferable interest).

[#ULLCA102(4)(A)(ii)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(4)(A)(ii) (distribution includes transfer in return for relinquishment of management participation or information access rights).

[#ULLCA102(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(4)(B) (distribution does not include reasonable compensation or bona fide retirement/benefits payments).

[#ULLCA102(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(5) (definition of "foreign limited liability company" as unincorporated entity formed under another jurisdiction's law).

[#ULLCA102(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(6) (definition of "jurisdiction" as political entity including states and foreign countries).

[#ULLCA102(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(7) (definition of "jurisdiction of formation" as jurisdiction governing internal affairs).

[#ULLCA102(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(8) (definition of "limited liability company" as entity formed under act or subject to act under Article 10 or § 110).

[#ULLCA102(9)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(9) (definition of "manager" as person responsible for performing management functions under § 407(c)).

[#ULLCA102(10)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(10) (definition of "manager-managed limited liability company" as company qualifying under § 407(a)).

[#ULLCA102(11)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(11) (definition of "member" as person becoming member under § 401 or existing when company became subject to act).

[#ULLCA102(11)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(11)(A) (member includes person becoming member under § 401 or when company became subject to act under § 110).

[#ULLCA102(11)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(11)(B) (member has not dissociated under § 602).

[#ULLCA102(12)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(12) (definition of "member-managed limited liability company" as company not manager-managed).

[#ULLCA102(13)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(13) (definition of "operating agreement" as agreement of all members on matters in § 105(a), whether oral, implied, or in record).

[#ULLCA102(14)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(14) (definition of "organizer" as person acting under § 201 to form company).

[#ULLCA102(15)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(15) (definition of "person" as individual, entity, or other legal or commercial entity).

[#ULLCA102(16)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(16) (definition of "principal office" as principal executive office location).

[#ULLCA102(17)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(17) (definition of "property" as all property real, personal, tangible, or intangible).

[#ULLCA102(18)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(18) (definition of "record" as information inscribed on tangible or electronic medium).

[#ULLCA102(19)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(19) (definition of "registered agent" authorized to receive service of process).

[#ULLCA102(20)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(20) (definition of "registered foreign limited liability company" registered to do business pursuant to filed statement).

[#ULLCA102(21)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(21) (definition of "sign" as execution/adoption of symbol with intent to authenticate).

[#ULLCA102(21)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(21)(A) (sign includes execution or adoption of tangible symbol).

[#ULLCA102(21)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(21)(B) (sign includes attachment or logical association of electronic symbol, sound, or process).

[#ULLCA102(22)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(22) (definition of "state" as US state, DC, Puerto Rico, or territorial possession).

[#ULLCA102(23)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23) (definition of "transfer" includes assignment, conveyance, sale, lease, encumbrance, gift, operation of law).

[#ULLCA102(23)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23)(A) (transfer includes assignment).

[#ULLCA102(23)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23)(B) (transfer includes conveyance).

[#ULLCA102(23)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23)(C) (transfer includes sale).

[#ULLCA102(23)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23)(D) (transfer includes lease).

[#ULLCA102(23)(E)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23)(E) (transfer includes encumbrance, mortgage, or security interest).

[#ULLCA102(23)(F)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(23)(F) (transfer includes gift).

[#ULLCA102(24)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(24) (definition of "transferable interest" as right to receive distributions, applying to any fraction by whomever owned).

[#ULLCA102(25)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 102(25) (definition of "transferee" as person to which transferable interest transferred, including person owning interest under § 603(a)(3)).

[#ULLCA103]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103 (knowledge; notice).

[#ULLCA103(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(a) (person knows fact if has actual knowledge or deemed to know under subsection (d)(1)).

[#ULLCA103(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(a)(1) (person knows fact if has actual knowledge).

[#ULLCA103(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(a)(2) (person knows fact if deemed to know under subsection (d)(1) or other law).

[#ULLCA103(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(b) (person has notice if has reason to know or deemed to have notice under subsection (d)(2)).

[#ULLCA103(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(b)(1) (person has notice if has reason to know fact from all facts known at time).

[#ULLCA103(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(b)(2) (person has notice if deemed to have notice under subsection (d)(2)).

[#ULLCA103(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(c) (person notifies another by taking steps reasonably required in ordinary course, subject to § 210(f)).

[#ULLCA103(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 103(d)(2) (non-member deemed to have notice of company dissolution, termination, or structural change 90 days after effective filing).

[#ULLCA105(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(a) (operating agreement governs relations, rights, activities, and amendment conditions except as provided in subsections (c) and (d)).

[#ULLCA105(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(a)(1) (operating agreement governs relations among members and between members and company).

[#ULLCA105(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(a)(2) (operating agreement governs rights and duties of manager).

[#ULLCA105(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(a)(3) (operating agreement governs activities and affairs and conduct thereof).

[#ULLCA105(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(a)(4) (operating agreement governs means and conditions for amending agreement).

[#ULLCA105(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(b) (act governs matters not provided for in operating agreement).

[#ULLCA105(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c) (operating agreement may not vary specified provisions).

[#ULLCA105(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(1) (cannot vary law applicable under § 104).

[#ULLCA105(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(2) (cannot vary company capacity under § 109 to sue and be sued).

[#ULLCA105(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(3) (cannot vary requirements pertaining to registered agents or Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA105(c)(3)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(3)(B) (cannot vary provisions pertaining to Secretary of State filings).

[#ULLCA105(c)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(5) (cannot alter or eliminate duty of loyalty or care except as provided in subsection (d)).

[#ULLCA105(c)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(6) (cannot eliminate contractual obligation of good faith and fair dealing under § 409(d), but may prescribe standards if not manifestly unreasonable).

[#ULLCA105(c)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(7) (cannot relieve or exonerate person from liability for bad faith, willful or intentional misconduct, or knowing violation of law).

[#ULLCA105(c)(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(8) (cannot unreasonably restrict duties and rights under § 410, but may impose reasonable restrictions and remedies).

[#ULLCA105(c)(14)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(14) (cannot vary required contents of structural change plans under §§ 1022(a), 1032(a), 1042(a), or 1052(a)).

[#ULLCA105(c)(15)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(c)(15) (cannot restrict rights of non-member or non-manager except as provided in §§ 106 and 107(b)).

[#ULLCA105(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(1) (operating agreement may specify authorization/ratification method for duty of loyalty violations and alter § 405(a)(2) prohibition).

[#ULLCA105(d)(1)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(1)(A) (operating agreement may specify method for authorization/ratification after full disclosure).

[#ULLCA105(d)(1)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(1)(B) (operating agreement may alter § 405(a)(2) prohibition to require only that total assets not less than total liabilities).

[#ULLCA105(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(2) (if operating agreement relieves member of responsibility and imposes on others, may eliminate or limit fiduciary duty of relieved member).

[#ULLCA105(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(3) (if not manifestly unreasonable, operating agreement may alter duties).

[#ULLCA105(d)(3)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(3)(A) (may alter or eliminate duty of loyalty aspects under § 409(b) and (i)).

[#ULLCA105(d)(3)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(3)(B) (may identify specific activities not violating duty of loyalty).

[#ULLCA105(d)(3)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(3)(C) (may alter duty of care but not authorize bad faith, willful or intentional misconduct, or knowing violation of law).

[#ULLCA105(d)(3)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(d)(3)(D) (may alter or eliminate any other fiduciary duty).

[#ULLCA105(e)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(e)(1) (court determines manifestly unreasonable as of time term became part of agreement considering only circumstances at that time).

[#ULLCA105(e)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(e)(2) (court may invalidate term only if readily apparent objective unreasonable or term unreasonable means to achieve objective).

[#ULLCA105(e)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(e)(2)(A) (court may invalidate if objective unreasonable).

[#ULLCA105(e)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 105(e)(2)(B) (court may invalidate if term unreasonable means to achieve objective).

[#ULLCA106(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 106(c) (intending initial members may make preformation agreement to become operating agreement upon formation).

[#ULLCA107(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 107(a) (operating agreement may require approval or condition for amendment; amendment ineffective without required approval or satisfaction of condition).

[#ULLCA107(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 107(b)(2) (post-transfer/dissociation amendment not effective to impose new obligations on transferee or dissociated member).

[#ULLCA107(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 107(d)(2) (filed record prevails as to third parties reasonably relying on record).

[#ULLCA112]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112 (permitted names).

[#ULLCA112(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(a) (name must contain "limited liability company," "limited company," or specified abbreviations).

[#ULLCA112(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b) (name must be distinguishable from specified existing names, except as provided in subsection (d)).

[#ULLCA112(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b)(1) (must be distinguishable from name of existing person whose formation required filing and not administratively dissolved).

[#ULLCA112(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b)(2) (must be distinguishable from name of limited liability partnership with effective statement of qualification).

[#ULLCA112(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b)(3) (must be distinguishable from name under which person registered to do business by filing).

[#ULLCA112(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b)(4) (must be distinguishable from name reserved under § 113 or other law).

[#ULLCA112(b)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b)(5) (must be distinguishable from name registered under § 114 or other law).

[#ULLCA112(b)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(b)(6) (must be distinguishable from name registered under assumed or fictitious name statute).

[#ULLCA112(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(c) (consent to use name and undertaking to change name allows use of consenting person's name).

[#ULLCA112(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(d) (in determining distinguishability, entity type indicators not considered except as provided in subsection (e)).

[#ULLCA112(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(e) (person may consent to use of name differing only by entity type indicator without name change requirement).

[#ULLCA112(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(f) (name may not contain prohibited words).

[#ULLCA112(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 112(g) (company may use non-distinguishable name if delivers certified copy of court judgment establishing right).

[#ULLCA113]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 113 (reservation of name).

[#ULLCA113(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 113(a) (person may reserve name for 120 days by delivering application to Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA113(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 113(b) (owner may transfer reservation by delivering signed notice to Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA114]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 114 (registration of name).

[#ULLCA114(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 114(a) (foreign company not registered to do business may register name if distinguishable under § 112).

[#ULLCA114(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 114(b) (to register name, foreign company delivers application stating name, jurisdiction, formation date, and alternate name).

[#ULLCA114(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 114(c) (name registration effective for one year).

[#ULLCA114(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 114(d) (foreign company may renew registration for successive one-year periods by delivering renewal application).

[#ULLCA114(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 114(e) (foreign company with name registration may register or consent to use of name).

[#ULLCA115]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115 (registered agent).

[#ULLCA115(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115(a) (each company and registered foreign company shall designate and maintain registered agent; designation affirms consent to serve).

[#ULLCA115(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115(b) (registered agent must have place of business in this state).

[#ULLCA115(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115(c) (registered agent duties limited to forwarding process, providing resignation notice, and keeping information current).

[#ULLCA115(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115(c)(1) (duty to forward process, notice, or demand to company at address supplied).

[#ULLCA115(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115(c)(2) (if resigning, duty to provide notice under § 117(c) to company at address supplied).

[#ULLCA115(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 115(c)(3) (duty to keep current information in certificate of organization or foreign registration statement).

[#ULLCA116]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116 (change of registered agent or address by company).

[#ULLCA116(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(a) (company may change registered agent or address by delivering statement of change to Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA116(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(a)(1) (statement of change must state company name).

[#ULLCA116(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(a)(2) (statement of change must state information to be in effect).

[#ULLCA116(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(b) (members or managers need not approve statement of change or similar filing).

[#ULLCA116(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(b)(1) (members or managers need not approve statement of change under this section).

[#ULLCA116(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(b)(2) (members or managers need not approve similar filing in other jurisdiction).
