[#ULLCA116(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(c) (statement of change designating new agent affirms agent consent to serve).

[#ULLCA116(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 116(d) (company may alternatively amend certificate of organization).

[#ULLCA117]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117 (resignation of registered agent).

[#ULLCA117(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(a) (registered agent may resign by delivering statement of resignation to Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA117(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(a)(1) (statement must state company or foreign company name).

[#ULLCA117(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(a)(2) (statement must state agent name).

[#ULLCA117(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(a)(3) (statement must state agent resigns).

[#ULLCA117(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(a)(4) (statement must state company address to which agent will send notice).

[#ULLCA117(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(b) (resignation effective on earlier of 31st day after filing or designation of new agent).

[#ULLCA117(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(b)(1) (resignation effective 31st day after filing).

[#ULLCA117(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(b)(2) (resignation effective upon designation of new agent).

[#ULLCA117(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(c) (agent shall promptly furnish company notice of filing date).

[#ULLCA117(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(d) (when effective, agent ceases responsibility for matters tendered thereafter; does not affect contractual rights).

[#ULLCA117(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 117(e) (agent may resign whether or not company in good standing).

[#ULLCA118]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118 (change of name or address by registered agent).

[#ULLCA118(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118(a) (if agent changes name or address, may deliver statement of change to Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA118(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118(a)(1) (statement must state company or foreign company name).

[#ULLCA118(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118(a)(2) (statement must state agent name as currently shown).

[#ULLCA118(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118(a)(3) (if agent name changed, statement must state new name).

[#ULLCA118(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118(a)(4) (if agent address changed, statement must state new address).

[#ULLCA118(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 118(b) (agent shall promptly furnish company notice of filing and changes).

[#ULLCA119]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119 (service of process, notice, or demand).

[#ULLCA119(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(a) (company or registered foreign company may be served by serving registered agent).

[#ULLCA119(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(b) (if no agent or agent cannot be served with reasonable diligence, may serve by mail to principal office; effective on earliest of receipt, return receipt, or five days after deposit).

[#ULLCA119(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(b)(1) (service effective on date company receives mail or delivery).

[#ULLCA119(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(b)(2) (service effective on date shown on return receipt if signed by company).

[#ULLCA119(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(b)(3) (service effective five days after deposit if correctly addressed with sufficient postage).

[#ULLCA119(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(c) (if cannot serve under subsections (a) or (b), may serve by handing copy to individual in charge of regular place of business if individual not plaintiff).

[#ULLCA119(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(d) (service on registered agent must be in written record).

[#ULLCA119(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 119(e) (service may be made by other means under other law).

[#ULLCA120]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 120 (delivery of record).

[#ULLCA120(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 120(a) (permissible delivery means include hand, mail, conventional commercial practice, and electronic transmission).

[#ULLCA120(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 120(b) (delivery to Secretary of State effective only when received).

[#ULLCA121]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 121 (legislature has power to amend or repeal; all companies governed by amendment or repeal).


[#ULLCA201]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201 (formation of limited liability company; certificate of organization).

[#ULLCA201(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(a) (one or more persons may act as organizers to form company by delivering certificate of organization to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA201(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(b) (certificate of organization must state company name, principal office addresses, and registered agent information).

[#ULLCA201(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(b)(1) (certificate must state company name complying with § 112).

[#ULLCA201(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(b)(2) (certificate must state street and mailing addresses of company's principal office).

[#ULLCA201(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(b)(3) (certificate must state registered agent's name and street and mailing addresses in this state).

[#ULLCA201(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(c) (certificate may contain statements on other matters but may not vary § 105(c) and (d) provisions inconsistently; statement in certificate not effective as statement of authority).

[#ULLCA201(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 201(d) (company formed when certificate becomes effective and at least one person has become member).

[#ULLCA202]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202 (amendment or restatement of certificate of organization).

[#ULLCA202(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(a) (certificate of organization may be amended or restated at any time).

[#ULLCA202(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(b) (to amend certificate, company must deliver amendment to Secretary of State for filing stating company name, initial certificate filing date, and amendment text).

[#ULLCA202(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(b)(1) (amendment must state name of company).

[#ULLCA202(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(b)(2) (amendment must state date of filing of company's initial certificate).

[#ULLCA202(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(b)(3) (amendment must state text of amendment).

[#ULLCA202(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(c) (to restate certificate, company must deliver restatement to Secretary of State for filing, designated as restatement in its heading).

[#ULLCA202(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(d) (if member or manager knows filed certificate information was inaccurate when filed or became inaccurate due to changed circumstances, member or manager shall promptly cause amendment or file corrective statement).

[#ULLCA202(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(d)(1) (member or manager shall cause certificate to be amended).

[#ULLCA202(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 202(d)(2) (if appropriate, member or manager shall deliver to Secretary of State for filing a statement of change under § 116 or statement of correction under § 209).

[#ULLCA203]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203 (signing of records to be delivered for filing to Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA203(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(a) (record delivered to Secretary of State for filing must be signed as specified in paragraphs (1) through (5)).

[#ULLCA203(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(a)(1) (record signed on behalf of company must be signed by person authorized by company, except as provided in paragraphs (2) and (3)).

[#ULLCA203(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(a)(2) (company's initial certificate of organization must be signed by at least one person acting as organizer).

[#ULLCA203(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(a)(3) (record delivered on behalf of dissolved company with no member must be signed by person winding up activities and affairs under § 702(c) or person appointed under § 702(d) to wind up).

[#ULLCA203(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(a)(4) (statement of denial by person under § 303 must be signed by that person).

[#ULLCA203(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(a)(5) (any other record delivered on behalf of person to Secretary of State for filing must be signed by that person).

[#ULLCA203(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(b) (record delivered for filing may be signed by agent; if individual required to sign is deceased or incompetent, record may be signed by legal representative).

[#ULLCA203(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 203(c) (person signing record as agent or legal representative affirms as fact that person is authorized to sign record).

[#ULLCA204]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204 (signing and filing pursuant to judicial order).

[#ULLCA204(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204(a) (if person required to sign or deliver record does not do so, aggrieved person may petition court to order signing, delivery, or unsigned filing).

[#ULLCA204(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204(a)(1) (court may order person to sign record).

[#ULLCA204(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204(a)(2) (court may order person to deliver record to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA204(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204(a)(3) (court may order Secretary of State to file record unsigned).

[#ULLCA204(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204(b) (if petitioner is not company or foreign company to which record pertains, petitioner shall make company or foreign company party to action).

[#ULLCA204(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 204(c) (record filed under subsection (a)(3) is effective without being signed).

[#ULLCA205]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205 (liability for inaccurate information in filed record).

[#ULLCA205(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a) (person suffering loss by reliance on inaccurate information in filed record may recover damages from signer who knew of inaccuracy or from member or manager who had knowledge or notice and could have corrected).

[#ULLCA205(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(1) (person may recover from person who signed record, or caused another to sign on person's behalf, and knew information inaccurate at time record signed).

[#ULLCA205(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(2) (person may recover from member or manager who knew or had notice of inaccuracy for sufficient time to correct before reliance, subject to subsection (b)).

[#ULLCA205(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(2)(A) (liability attaches if record was delivered for filing on behalf of company).

[#ULLCA205(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(2)(B) (liability attaches if member or manager knew or had notice of inaccuracy for reasonably sufficient time before reliance to have corrected via available remedies).

[#ULLCA205(a)(2)(B)(i)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(2)(B)(i) (member or manager could have corrected by effecting amendment under § 202).

[#ULLCA205(a)(2)(B)(ii)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(2)(B)(ii) (member or manager could have corrected by filing petition under § 204).

[#ULLCA205(a)(2)(B)(iii)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(a)(2)(B)(iii) (member or manager could have corrected by delivering to Secretary of State for filing statement of change under § 116 or statement of correction under § 209).

[#ULLCA205(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(b) (if operating agreement of member-managed company expressly relieves member of responsibility for maintaining accuracy of filed information and imposes responsibility on other members, liability under subsection (a)(2) applies to other members and not to relieved member).

[#ULLCA205(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 205(c) (individual who signs record authorized or required to be filed affirms under penalty of perjury that information stated in record is accurate).

[#ULLCA206]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206 (filing requirements).

[#ULLCA206(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(a) (to be filed by Secretary of State, record must be received by Secretary of State, comply with act, and satisfy enumerated requirements).

[#ULLCA206(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(a)(1) (filing of record must be required or permitted by act).

[#ULLCA206(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(a)(2) (record must be physically delivered in written form unless and to extent Secretary of State permits electronic delivery of records).

[#ULLCA206(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(a)(3) (words in record must be in English and numbers in Arabic or Roman numerals, but entity name need not be in English if written in English letters or Arabic or Roman numerals).

[#ULLCA206(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(a)(4) (record must be signed by person authorized or required under act to sign record).

[#ULLCA206(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(a)(5) (record must state name and capacity, if any, of each individual who signed, on behalf of individual or person authorized individual to sign, but need not contain seal, attestation, acknowledgment, or verification).

[#ULLCA206(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(b) (if law other than act prohibits disclosure of information contained in record, Secretary of State shall file record if otherwise compliant but may redact information).

[#ULLCA206(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(c) (when record delivered to Secretary of State for filing, required fees, taxes, interest, and penalties owed to and collected by Secretary of State must be paid).

[#ULLCA206(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(d) (Secretary of State may require delivery of identical or conformed copy of record for filing).

[#ULLCA206(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(e) (Secretary of State may provide forms for filings required or permitted to be made, but use of forms not required except as otherwise provided in subsection (f)).

[#ULLCA206(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 206(f) (Secretary of State may require cover sheet for record delivered for filing on prescribed form).

[#ULLCA207]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 207 (effective date and time of filed record).

[#ULLCA207(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 207(1) (except as otherwise provided in § 208 and subject to § 209(d), record is effective on date and time of filing by Secretary of State as provided in § 210(b)).

[#ULLCA207(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 207(2) (record is effective on date of filing and at time specified in record if later than time under paragraph (1)).

[#ULLCA207(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 207(3) (record is effective at specified delayed date and time not more than 90 days after filing).

[#ULLCA207(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 207(4) (if delayed effective date specified but no time specified, record effective at 12:01 a.m. on date not more than 90 days after date of filing).

[#ULLCA208]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208 (withdrawal of filed record before effectiveness).

[#ULLCA208(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208(a) (except as otherwise provided in §§ 1024, 1034, 1044, and 1054, record delivered to Secretary of State for filing may be withdrawn before effectiveness by delivering statement of withdrawal for filing).

[#ULLCA208(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208(b) (statement of withdrawal must be signed by each signer of withdrawn record, identify record, and if signed by fewer than all signers state withdrawal per agreement).

[#ULLCA208(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208(b)(1) (statement of withdrawal must be signed by each person who signed record being withdrawn, or on whose behalf another signed, unless as provided in paragraph (3)).

[#ULLCA208(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208(b)(2) (statement of withdrawal must identify record to be withdrawn).

[#ULLCA208(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208(b)(3) (if statement of withdrawal signed by fewer than all persons who signed record, must state withdrawal is effective and has been authorized by persons who have not signed statement).

[#ULLCA208(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 208(c) (upon filing of statement of withdrawal, action or transaction evidenced by original record does not take effect).

[#ULLCA209]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209 (correcting filed record).

[#ULLCA209(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(a) (person on whose behalf filed record was delivered to Secretary of State for filing may correct record if inaccurate, defectively signed, or electronically defective at time of filing).

[#ULLCA209(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(a)(1) (may correct if record was inaccurate at time of filing).

[#ULLCA209(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(a)(2) (may correct if record was defectively signed).

[#ULLCA209(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(a)(3) (may correct if electronic transmission was defective).

[#ULLCA209(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(b) (to correct filed record, person must deliver to Secretary of State for filing statement of correction).

[#ULLCA209(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(c) (statement of correction must comply with enumerated requirements).

[#ULLCA209(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(c)(1) (statement of correction may not state delayed effective date).

[#ULLCA209(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(c)(2) (statement of correction must be signed by person correcting filed record).

[#ULLCA209(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(c)(3) (statement of correction must identify filed record to be corrected).

[#ULLCA209(c)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(c)(4) (statement of correction must specify inaccuracy or defect to be corrected).

[#ULLCA209(c)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(c)(5) (statement of correction must correct inaccuracy or defect).

[#ULLCA209(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 209(d) (statement of correction is effective as of effective date of record it corrects except for purposes of § 103(d) and as to persons relying on uncorrected record; for those purposes, effective when filed).

[#ULLCA210]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210 (duty of Secretary of State to file; review of refusal to file; delivery of record by Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA210(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(a) (Secretary of State shall file record delivered to Secretary of State for filing which satisfies act; filing is ministerial duty).

[#ULLCA210(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(b) (when Secretary of State files record, Secretary of State shall record date and time of filing and deliver copy of record with acknowledgment of filing date and time to person who submitted record; for statement of denial, also deliver copy to company).

[#ULLCA210(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(c) (if Secretary of State refuses to file record, Secretary of State shall within 15 business days after record delivered return record or notify submitter of refusal with brief explanation).

[#ULLCA210(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(c)(1) (Secretary of State shall return record or notify person submitting record of refusal to file).

[#ULLCA210(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(c)(2) (Secretary of State shall provide brief explanation of refusal to file).

[#ULLCA210(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(d) (if Secretary of State refuses to file record, person submitting may petition court to compel filing; court may summarily decide matter with record and explanation attached to petition).

[#ULLCA210(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(e) (Secretary of State's filing or refusal to file record does not affect validity of record or create presumption regarding accuracy of information in record).

[#ULLCA210(e)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(e)(1) (filing or refusal to file does not affect validity or invalidity of record in whole or part).

[#ULLCA210(e)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(e)(2) (filing or refusal to file does not create presumption information in record is correct or incorrect).

[#ULLCA210(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(f) (except as otherwise provided by § 119 or other law, Secretary of State may deliver record or notice to person by specified methods).

[#ULLCA210(f)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(f)(1) (delivery in person to submitter).

[#ULLCA210(f)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(f)(2) (delivery to address of company's or foreign company's registered agent).

[#ULLCA210(f)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(f)(3) (delivery to principal office of company or foreign company).

[#ULLCA210(f)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 210(f)(4) (delivery to other address provided by person for delivery).

[#ULLCA211]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211 (certificate of good standing or registration).

[#ULLCA211(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(a) (on request of any person, Secretary of State shall issue certificate of good standing for company or certificate of registration for registered foreign company).

[#ULLCA211(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b) (certificate must state enumerated information).

[#ULLCA211(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(1) (certificate must state company's name or name used in this state by foreign company).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2) (for company, certificate must state that certificate of organization filed and effective, effective date, period of duration if less than perpetual, and absence of dissolution or termination filings or proceedings).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(A) (certificate of organization has been filed).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(B) (date certificate of organization became effective).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(C) (period of duration if less than perpetual as reflected in records of Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(D) (statement of dissolution, administrative dissolution, or termination not filed, records do not reflect dissolution or termination, and no § 708 proceeding pending).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(D)(i)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(D)(i) (statement of dissolution, statement of administrative dissolution, or statement of termination has not been filed).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(D)(ii)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(D)(ii) (records of Secretary of State do not otherwise reflect that company has been dissolved or terminated).

[#ULLCA211(b)(2)(D)(iii)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(2)(D)(iii) (proceeding under § 708 is not pending).

[#ULLCA211(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(3) (for registered foreign company, certificate must state company registered to do business in this state).

[#ULLCA211(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(4) (all fees, taxes, interest, and penalties owed to and collected by Secretary of State have been paid, if payment reflected in records and nonpayment affects standing or registration).

[#ULLCA211(b)(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(4)(A) (payment is reflected in records of Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA211(b)(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(4)(B) (nonpayment of fees, taxes, interest, or penalties affects good standing or registration).

[#ULLCA211(b)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(5) (most recent annual or biennial report required by § 212 has been delivered to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA211(b)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(b)(6) (other facts of record in office of Secretary of State which person requesting certificate reasonably requests).

[#ULLCA211(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 211(c) (subject to any qualification stated in certificate, certificate may be relied on as conclusive evidence facts stated in certificate are correct).

[#ULLCA212]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212 (annual or biennial report for Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA212(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a) (company or registered foreign company shall deliver to Secretary of State for filing annual or biennial report stating enumerated information).

[#ULLCA212(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a)(1) (report must state company's or foreign company's name).

[#ULLCA212(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a)(2) (report must state name and street and mailing addresses of company's or foreign company's registered agent in this state).

[#ULLCA212(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a)(3) (report must state street and mailing addresses of company's or foreign company's principal office).

[#ULLCA212(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a)(4) (if company or foreign company is member-managed, report must state name of at least one member).

[#ULLCA212(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a)(5) (if company or foreign company is manager-managed, report must state name of at least one manager).

[#ULLCA212(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(a)(6) (for foreign company, report must state its jurisdiction of formation and alternate name adopted under § 906(a)).

[#ULLCA212(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(b) (information in annual or biennial report must be current as of date report is signed on behalf of company or foreign company).

[#ULLCA212(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(c) (first report must be delivered after January 1 and before April 1 of year following formation or registration; subsequent reports delivered after January 1 and before April 1 of each second calendar year thereafter).

[#ULLCA212(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(d) (if report does not contain required information, Secretary of State shall promptly notify reporting company or foreign company in record and return report for correction).

[#ULLCA212(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 212(e) (if report contains name or address of registered agent differing from information in Secretary of State records, differing information considered statement of change under § 116).

[#ULLCA301]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 301 (no agency power of member as member).

[#ULLCA301(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 301(a) (member is not agent of company solely by reason of being member).

[#ULLCA301(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 301(b) (person's status as member does not prevent or restrict other law from imposing liability on company because of person's conduct).

[#ULLCA302]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302 (statement of limited liability company authority).

[#ULLCA302(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a) (company may deliver statement of authority to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA302(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(1) (statement must include company name and registered agent name and addresses).

[#ULLCA302(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(2) (statement may state authority or limitations on authority of persons holding positions to sign real property instruments or enter into transactions on behalf of company).

[#ULLCA302(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(2)(A) (may state authority or limitations on authority to sign instrument transferring real property held in company name).

[#ULLCA302(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(2)(B) (may state authority or limitations on authority to enter into other transactions on behalf of, or otherwise act for or bind, company).

[#ULLCA302(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(3) (statement may state authority or limitations on authority of specific person to sign real property instruments or enter into transactions on behalf of company).

[#ULLCA302(a)(3)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(3)(A) (may state specific person's authority or limitations on authority to sign instrument transferring real property held in company name).

[#ULLCA302(a)(3)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(a)(3)(B) (may state specific person's authority or limitations on authority to enter into other transactions on behalf of, or otherwise act for or bind, company).

[#ULLCA302(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(b) (to amend or cancel filed statement of authority, company must deliver amendment or cancellation to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA302(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(b)(1) (amendment or cancellation must state company name).

[#ULLCA302(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(b)(2) (amendment or cancellation must state name and street and mailing addresses of company's registered agent).

[#ULLCA302(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(b)(3) (amendment or cancellation must state date statement being affected became effective).

[#ULLCA302(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(b)(4) (amendment or cancellation must state contents of amendment or declaration that statement is canceled).

[#ULLCA302(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(c) (statement of authority affects only power of person to bind company to persons that are not members).

[#ULLCA302(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(d) (subject to subsection (c) and § 103(d), and except as provided in subsections (f), (g), and (h), limitation on authority in effective statement not by itself evidence of any person's knowledge or notice of limitation).

[#ULLCA302(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(e) (grant of authority in effective statement conclusive in favor of person giving value relying on grant, except as otherwise provided in subsections (f), (g), and (h)).

[#ULLCA302(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(f) (grant of authority to transfer real property held in company name in effective statement conclusive in favor of person giving value without knowledge to contrary, if statement filed in office for recording transfers and person reasonably relies on grant).

[#ULLCA302(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(g) (limitation on authority to transfer real property held in company name contained in effective statement is not by itself evidence of knowledge or notice of limitation unless statement filed in office for recording transfers).

[#ULLCA302(h)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 302(h) (except as otherwise provided in subsections (f) and (g), person not member is deemed to know of limitation on authority to transfer real property contained in effective statement 90 days after statement filed in office for recording transfers).

[#ULLCA303]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 303 (statement of denial).

[#ULLCA303(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 303(a) (person named in filed statement of authority granting person authority may deliver to Secretary of State for filing statement of denial stating name of person denying authority and company name).

[#ULLCA303(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 303(b) (statement of denial operates as restrictive amendment under § 302).

[#ULLCA303(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 303(c) (person's failure to file statement of denial does not affect whether person has authority to act for company).

[#ULLCA304]: Rev. Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 304 (Unif. L. Comm'n 2006) (establishing that debts, obligations, or other liabilities of an LLC are solely the debts of the company, and do not become the debts of members or managers solely by reason of their acting as such).

[#ULLCA401]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401 (becoming member).

[#ULLCA401(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(a) (if company to have only one member upon formation, person becomes member as agreed by that person and organizer).

[#ULLCA401(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(b) (if company to have more than one member upon formation, persons become members as agreed before formation).

[#ULLCA401(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(c) (after formation, person becomes member as provided in operating agreement, by transaction under Article 10, with affirmative vote or consent of all members, or as provided in § 701(a)(3)).

[#ULLCA401(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(c)(1) (person becomes member as provided in operating agreement).

[#ULLCA401(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(c)(2) (person becomes member as result of transaction effective under Article 10).

[#ULLCA401(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(c)(3) (person becomes member with affirmative vote or consent of all members).

[#ULLCA401(c)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(c)(4) (person becomes member as provided in § 701(a)(3)).

[#ULLCA401(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(d) (person may become member without acquiring transferable interest or making or being obligated to make contribution).

[#ULLCA401(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(d)(1) (person may become member without acquiring transferable interest).

[#ULLCA401(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 401(d)(2) (person may become member without making or being obligated to make contribution to company).

[#ULLCA402]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 402 (form of contribution may be property, services, or other benefit to company or agreement to provide same).

[#ULLCA403]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 403 (liability for contributions).

[#ULLCA403(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 403(a) (person's obligation to make contribution not excused by death, disability, termination, or other inability to perform personally).

[#ULLCA403(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 403(b) (if person does not fulfill obligation to contribute other than money, person obligated at company's option to contribute money equal to value of unfulfilled contribution).

[#ULLCA403(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 403(c) (obligation to make contribution may be compromised only by affirmative vote or consent of all members; creditor extending credit in reliance on obligation without knowledge or notice of compromise may enforce obligation).

[#ULLCA404]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 404 (sharing of and right to distributions before dissolution).

[#ULLCA404(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 404(a) (distribution before dissolution and winding up must be in equal shares among members and dissociated persons, except to comply with transfer under § 502 or charging order under § 503).

[#ULLCA404(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 404(b) (person has right to distribution before dissolution only if company decides to make interim distribution; dissociation does not entitle person to distribution).

[#ULLCA404(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 404(c) (person does not have right to demand or receive distribution in form other than money; company may distribute asset in kind only if each part fungible and each person receives percentage equal in value to person's share).

[#ULLCA404(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 404(d) (if member or transferee entitled to receive distribution, has status of and remedies available to creditor with respect to distribution; company's obligation to distribute subject to offset for amount owed by member or dissociated member).

[#ULLCA405]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405 (limitation on distribution).

[#ULLCA405(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(a) (company may not make distribution if after distribution company's total assets would be less than sum of total liabilities plus amount needed to satisfy preferential rights upon dissolution).

[#ULLCA405(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(a)(1) (total assets must not be less than total liabilities).

[#ULLCA405(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(a)(2) (total assets must not be less than amount needed to satisfy preferential rights upon dissolution of members and transferees whose preferential rights superior to rights of persons receiving distribution).

[#ULLCA405(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(b) (company may base determination that distribution not prohibited under subsection (a) on financial statements or other written financial information reasonably believed accurate, fair valuation, or other method reasonable under circumstances).

[#ULLCA405(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(c) (except as otherwise provided in subsection (e), effect of distribution measured at earlier of distribution date or date person ceases to be member if distribution in exchange for person ceasing to be member).

[#ULLCA405(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(d) (company's indebtedness incurred by issuing distribution rights or other indebtedness incurred as distribution is treated as distribution for purposes of subsection (a) only to extent company makes payment on account of indebtedness to person in person's capacity as member or transferee).

[#ULLCA405(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 405(e) (for distribution to departing member to purchase member's interest based on liquidation value, effect measured as of date company required to purchase departing member's interest).

[#ULLCA406]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406 (liability for improper distributions).

[#ULLCA406(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(a) (if member or manager consents to distribution in violation of § 405 and in consenting fails to comply with § 409, member or manager personally liable to company for amount exceeding what could have been distributed without violation, except as otherwise provided in subsection (b)).

[#ULLCA406(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(b) (if operating agreement of member-managed company expressly relieves member of authority and responsibility to consent to distributions and imposes on other members, subsection (a) liability applies to other members).

[#ULLCA406(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(c) (person receiving distribution knowing it violated § 405 is personally liable to company but only to extent distribution received exceeded amount that could have been properly paid).

[#ULLCA406(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(d) (person against which action commenced under subsection (a) may implead other persons liable under subsection (a) or persons who received distribution in violation of subsection (c) and seek contribution).

[#ULLCA406(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(d)(1) (may implead any other person liable under subsection (a) and seek contribution).

[#ULLCA406(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(d)(2) (may implead person who received distribution in violation of subsection (c) and seek contribution in amount person received in violation).

[#ULLCA406(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 406(e) (action under this section barred unless commenced not later than two years after distribution).

[#ULLCA407]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407 (management of limited liability company).

[#ULLCA407(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(a) (company is member-managed unless operating agreement expressly provides company is or will be manager-managed or managed by managers, or includes words of similar import).

[#ULLCA407(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(a)(1) (company manager-managed if operating agreement expressly provides company is or will be manager-managed, managed by managers, or management vested in managers).

[#ULLCA407(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(a)(2) (company manager-managed if operating agreement includes words of similar import).

[#ULLCA407(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b) (in member-managed company, management vested in members; each member has equal rights; majority decides ordinary matters; all members required for acts outside ordinary course or to amend operating agreement).

[#ULLCA407(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b)(1) (except as expressly provided in act, management and conduct vested in members).

[#ULLCA407(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b)(2) (each member has equal rights in management and conduct of activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA407(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b)(3) (difference among members as to ordinary matter may be decided by majority of members).

[#ULLCA407(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b)(4) (affirmative vote or consent of all members required to undertake act outside ordinary course or amend operating agreement).

[#ULLCA407(b)(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b)(4)(A) (all members required to undertake act outside ordinary course of activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA407(b)(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(b)(4)(B) (all members required to amend operating agreement).

[#ULLCA407(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c) (in manager-managed company, managers decide matters; each manager has equal rights; all members required for acts outside ordinary course or to amend operating agreement; manager may be chosen by majority of members and removed without cause).

[#ULLCA407(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(1) (except as expressly provided in act, any matter relating to activities and affairs decided exclusively by manager or majority of managers).

[#ULLCA407(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(2) (each manager has equal rights in management and conduct of activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA407(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(3) (affirmative vote or consent of all members required to undertake act outside ordinary course or amend operating agreement).

[#ULLCA407(c)(3)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(3)(A) (all members required to undertake act outside ordinary course of activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA407(c)(3)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(3)(B) (all members required to amend operating agreement).

[#ULLCA407(c)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(4) (manager may be chosen by affirmative vote or consent of majority of members and remains manager until successor chosen unless earlier resignation, removal, death, or termination; may be removed by majority without notice or cause).

[#ULLCA407(c)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(5) (person need not be member to be manager, but dissociation of member who is also manager removes person as manager; person ceasing to be manager not dissociated as member by that cessation alone).

[#ULLCA407(c)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(c)(6) (person's ceasing to be manager does not discharge debt, obligation, or liability incurred while manager).

[#ULLCA407(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(d) (action requiring vote or consent of members may be taken without meeting, and member may appoint proxy or agent to vote or consent by signing appointing record).

[#ULLCA407(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(e) (dissolution does not affect applicability of this section; person wrongfully causing dissolution loses right to participate in management as member and manager).

[#ULLCA407(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(f) (company shall reimburse member for advance to company beyond amount of capital member agreed to contribute).

[#ULLCA407(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(g) (payment or advance by member giving rise to company obligation under subsection (f) or § 408(a) constitutes loan to company accruing interest from date of payment or advance).

[#ULLCA407(h)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 407(h) (member not entitled to remuneration for services performed for member-managed company, except reasonable compensation for services rendered in winding up).

[#ULLCA408]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 408 (reimbursement; indemnification; advancement; and insurance).

[#ULLCA408(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 408(a) (company shall reimburse member or manager for any payment made in course of activities on behalf of company, if member or manager complied with §§ 405, 407, and 409 in making payment).

[#ULLCA408(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 408(b) (company shall indemnify and hold harmless person with respect to claim or demand by reason of person's capacity as member or manager, if claim does not arise from person's breach of § 405, 407, or 409).

[#ULLCA408(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 408(c) (in ordinary course, company may advance reasonable expenses incurred by person in connection with claim by reason of capacity as member or manager, if person promises to repay if ultimately determined not entitled to indemnification).

[#ULLCA408(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 408(d) (company may purchase and maintain insurance on behalf of member or manager against liability incurred in that capacity even if operating agreement could not eliminate or limit liability under § 105(c)(7)).

[#ULLCA409]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409 (standards of conduct for members and managers).

[#ULLCA409(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(a) (member of member-managed company owes to company and other members duties of loyalty and care stated in subsections (b) and (c), subject to § 801).

[#ULLCA409(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b) (fiduciary duty of loyalty of member in member-managed company includes specified duties).

[#ULLCA409(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b)(1) (duty to account to company and hold as trustee any property, profit, or benefit derived in conduct or winding up, from use of company property, or from appropriation of company opportunity).

[#ULLCA409(b)(1)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b)(1)(A) (duty to account for property, profit, or benefit derived in conduct or winding up of activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA409(b)(1)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b)(1)(B) (duty to account for property, profit, or benefit from use by member of company property).

[#ULLCA409(b)(1)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b)(1)(C) (duty to account for property, profit, or benefit from appropriation of company opportunity).

[#ULLCA409(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b)(2) (duty to refrain from dealing with company in conduct or winding up as or on behalf of person having interest adverse to company).

[#ULLCA409(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(b)(3) (duty to refrain from competing with company in conduct of activities and affairs before dissolution).

[#ULLCA409(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(c) (duty of care of member in member-managed company is to refrain from grossly negligent or reckless conduct, willful or intentional misconduct, or knowing violation of law).

[#ULLCA409(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(d) (member shall discharge duties and obligations under act or operating agreement and exercise rights consistently with contractual obligation of good faith and fair dealing).

[#ULLCA409(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(e) (member does not violate duty or obligation solely because member's conduct furthers member's own interest).

[#ULLCA409(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(f) (all members or managers may authorize or ratify, after full disclosure of all material facts, specific act or transaction that otherwise would violate duty of loyalty).

[#ULLCA409(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(g) (it is defense to claim under subsection (b)(2) and any comparable claim in equity or at common law that transaction was fair to company).

[#ULLCA409(h)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(h) (if member enters into transaction with company permitted by subsection (f) or (i)(6) or operating agreement that otherwise would be prohibited by subsection (b)(2), member's rights and obligations arising from transaction are same as person not member).

[#ULLCA409(i)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i) (in manager-managed company, specified rules apply).

[#ULLCA409(i)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i)(1) (subsections (a), (b), (c), and (g) apply to manager or managers and not members).

[#ULLCA409(i)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i)(2) (duty stated under subsection (b)(3) continues until winding up completed).

[#ULLCA409(i)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i)(3) (subsection (d) applies to managers and members).

[#ULLCA409(i)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i)(4) (subsection (e) applies only to members).

[#ULLCA409(i)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i)(5) (power to ratify under subsection (f) applies only to members).

[#ULLCA409(i)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 409(i)(6) (subject to subsection (d), member does not have duty to company or other member solely by reason of being member).

[#ULLCA410]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410 (rights to information of member, manager, and person dissociated as member).

[#ULLCA410(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(a) (in member-managed company, member may inspect and copy company records on reasonable notice and company shall furnish information to members).

[#ULLCA410(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(a)(1) (on reasonable notice, member may inspect and copy during regular business hours any record maintained by company regarding activities, affairs, financial condition, and other circumstances material to member's rights and duties).

[#ULLCA410(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(a)(2) (company shall furnish to each member without demand information material to proper exercise of member's rights and duties and on demand any other information except to extent demand unreasonable or improper).

[#ULLCA410(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(a)(2)(A) (company shall furnish without demand any information company knows and is material to proper exercise of member's rights and duties, except to extent company can establish reasonably believes member already knows information).

[#ULLCA410(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(a)(2)(B) (company shall furnish on demand any other information concerning activities, affairs, financial condition, and other circumstances, except to extent demand unreasonable or otherwise improper).

[#ULLCA410(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(a)(3) (duty to furnish information under paragraph (2) also applies to each member to extent member knows any of information described in paragraph (2)).

[#ULLCA410(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b) (in manager-managed company, informational rights and duties apply to managers; members may inspect information if sought for proper purpose and directly connected).

[#ULLCA410(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(1) (informational rights stated in subsection (a) and duty stated in subsection (a)(3) apply to managers and not members).

[#ULLCA410(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(2) (during regular business hours, member may inspect and copy information as just and reasonable if member seeks information for purpose reasonably related to member's interest, makes demand describing information and purpose, and information directly connected to purpose).

[#ULLCA410(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(2)(A) (member seeks information for purpose reasonably related to member's interest as member).

[#ULLCA410(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(2)(B) (member makes demand in record received by company, describing with reasonable particularity information sought and purpose for seeking information).

[#ULLCA410(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(2)(C) (information sought directly connected to member's purpose).

[#ULLCA410(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(3) (not later than 10 days after receiving demand, company shall inform member in record what information will be provided, when and where, and reasons for declining if declining to provide any demanded information).

[#ULLCA410(b)(3)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(3)(A) (company shall inform what information will provide in response to demand and when and where will provide).

[#ULLCA410(b)(3)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(3)(B) (company shall inform reasons for declining if declining to provide any demanded information).

[#ULLCA410(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(b)(4) (whenever act or operating agreement provides for member to vote or consent, before vote cast or consent given or withheld, company shall without demand provide member with all information known to company and material to member's decision).

[#ULLCA410(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(c) (subject to subsection (h), on 10 days demand in record, person dissociated as member may have access to information to which entitled while member if information pertains to period during which person was member, person seeks in good faith, and satisfies requirements imposed on member by subsection (b)(2)).

[#ULLCA410(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(c)(1) (information pertains to period during which person was member).

[#ULLCA410(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(c)(2) (person seeks information in good faith).

[#ULLCA410(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(c)(3) (person satisfies requirements imposed on member by subsection (b)(2)).

[#ULLCA410(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(d) (company shall respond to demand pursuant to subsection (c) in manner provided in subsection (b)(3)).

[#ULLCA410(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(e) (company may charge person making demand under this section reasonable costs of copying, limited to costs of labor and material).

[#ULLCA410(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(f) (member or person dissociated as member may exercise rights under this section through agent or legal representative; restriction or condition in operating agreement or under subsection (h) applies to agent or representative and to member or dissociated person).

[#ULLCA410(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(g) (subject to § 504, rights under this section do not extend to person as transferee).

[#ULLCA410(h)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 410(h) (in addition to restriction or condition in operating agreement, company as matter within ordinary course may impose reasonable restrictions and conditions on access to and use of information, including designating information confidential and imposing nondisclosure and safeguarding obligations; in dispute concerning reasonableness, company has burden of proving reasonableness).


[#ULLCA501]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 501 (transferable interest is personal property).

[#ULLCA502]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502 (transfer of transferable interest).

[#ULLCA502(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(a) (subject to § 503(f), transfer in whole or part of transferable interest is permissible, does not cause dissociation or dissolution, and does not entitle transferee to participate in management or have access to records except as provided in subsection (c)).

[#ULLCA502(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(a)(1) (transfer is permissible).

[#ULLCA502(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(a)(2) (transfer does not by itself cause person's dissociation as member or dissolution and winding up of company's activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA502(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(a)(3) (subject to § 504, transfer does not entitle transferee to participate in management or conduct or have access to records except as provided in subsection (c)).

[#ULLCA502(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(b) (transferee has right to receive, in accordance with transfer, distributions to which transferor would otherwise be entitled).

[#ULLCA502(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(c) (in dissolution and winding up, transferee entitled to account of company's transactions only from date of dissolution).

[#ULLCA502(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(d) (transferable interest may be evidenced by certificate issued by company in record, and interest represented by certificate may be transferred by transfer of certificate).

[#ULLCA502(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(e) (company need not give effect to transferee's rights until company knows or has notice of transfer).

[#ULLCA502(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(f) (transfer of transferable interest in violation of restriction on transfer in operating agreement ineffective if intended transferee has knowledge or notice of restriction at time of transfer).

[#ULLCA502(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(g) (except as otherwise provided in § 602(5)(B), if member transfers transferable interest, transferor retains rights of member other than interest transferred and retains all duties and obligations of member).

[#ULLCA502(h)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 502(h) (if member transfers transferable interest to person that becomes member with respect to transferred interest, transferee liable for member's obligations under §§ 403 and 406 known to transferee when transferee becomes member).

[#ULLCA503]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503 (charging order).

[#ULLCA503(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(a) (on application by judgment creditor of member or transferee, court may enter charging order against transferable interest of judgment debtor for unsatisfied amount; except as provided in subsection (f), charging order constitutes lien and requires company to pay over distributions that otherwise would be paid to judgment debtor).

[#ULLCA503(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(b) (to extent necessary to effectuate collection of distributions, court may appoint receiver with power to make inquiries judgment debtor might have made and make all other orders necessary to give effect to charging order).

[#ULLCA503(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(b)(1) (court may appoint receiver of distributions subject to charging order, with power to make all inquiries judgment debtor might have made).

[#ULLCA503(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(b)(2) (court may make all other orders necessary to give effect to charging order).

[#ULLCA503(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(c) (upon showing that distributions under charging order will not pay judgment debt within reasonable time, court may foreclose lien and order sale of transferable interest; except as provided in subsection (f), purchaser at foreclosure sale obtains only transferable interest, does not become member, and is subject to § 502).

[#ULLCA503(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(d) (at any time before foreclosure, member or transferee whose transferable interest is subject to charging order may extinguish charging order by satisfying judgment and filing certified copy of satisfaction with court that issued charging order).

[#ULLCA503(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(e) (at any time before foreclosure, company or members whose transferable interests not subject to charging order may pay to judgment creditor full amount due and thereby succeed to rights of judgment creditor, including charging order).

[#ULLCA503(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(f) (if court orders foreclosure of charging order lien against sole member, court shall confirm sale, purchaser obtains member's entire interest, purchaser thereby becomes member, and person whose interest was subject to foreclosed charging order is dissociated as member).

[#ULLCA503(f)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(f)(1) (court shall confirm sale).

[#ULLCA503(f)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(f)(2) (purchaser at sale obtains member's entire interest, not only member's transferable interest).

[#ULLCA503(f)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(f)(3) (purchaser thereby becomes member).

[#ULLCA503(f)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(f)(4) (person whose interest was subject to foreclosed charging order is dissociated as member).

[#ULLCA503(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(g) (act does not deprive any member or transferee of benefit of any exemption law applicable to transferable interest).

[#ULLCA503(h)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 503(h) (this section provides exclusive remedy by which person seeking in capacity of judgment creditor to enforce judgment against member or transferee may satisfy judgment from judgment debtor's transferable interest).

[#ULLCA504]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 504 (power of legal representative of deceased member).

[#ULLCA504(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 504(1) (deceased member's legal representative may exercise rights of transferee provided in § 502(c)).

[#ULLCA504(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 504(2) (for purposes of settling estate, deceased member's legal representative may exercise rights deceased member had under § 410).


[#ULLCA601]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601 (power to dissociate as member; wrongful dissociation).

[#ULLCA601(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(a) (person has power to dissociate as member at any time, rightfully or wrongfully, by withdrawing as member by express will under § 602(1)).

[#ULLCA601(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b) (person's dissociation as member is wrongful only if dissociation is in breach of express provision of operating agreement or occurs before completion of winding up in specified circumstances).

[#ULLCA601(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b)(1) (dissociation wrongful if in breach of express provision of operating agreement).

[#ULLCA601(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b)(2) (dissociation wrongful if occurs before completion of winding up and person withdraws by express will, is expelled by judicial order, is dissociated under § 602(8), or willfully dissolved or terminated).

[#ULLCA601(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b)(2)(A) (dissociation wrongful if person withdraws as member by express will).

[#ULLCA601(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b)(2)(B) (dissociation wrongful if person expelled as member by judicial order under § 602(6)).

[#ULLCA601(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b)(2)(C) (dissociation wrongful if person dissociated under § 602(8)).

[#ULLCA601(b)(2)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(b)(2)(D) (in case of person not trust, estate, or individual, dissociation wrongful if person expelled or otherwise dissociated because it willfully dissolved or terminated).

[#ULLCA601(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 601(c) (person that wrongfully dissociates as member liable to company and, subject to § 801, to other members for damages caused by dissociation; liability in addition to any other debt, obligation, or liability to company or other members).

[#ULLCA602]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602 (events causing dissociation).

[#ULLCA602(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(1) (person dissociated when company knows or has notice of person's express will to withdraw, or on later withdrawal date specified by person).

[#ULLCA602(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(2) (person dissociated when event stated in operating agreement as causing dissociation occurs).

[#ULLCA602(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(3) (person dissociated when person's entire interest transferred in foreclosure sale under § 503(f)).

[#ULLCA602(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(4) (person dissociated when expelled as member pursuant to operating agreement).

[#ULLCA602(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(5) (person dissociated when expelled as member by affirmative vote or consent of all other members in specified circumstances).

[#ULLCA602(5)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(5)(A) (person expelled if unlawful to carry on company's activities and affairs with person as member).

[#ULLCA602(5)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(5)(B) (person expelled if there has been transfer of all person's transferable interest, other than transfer for security purposes or charging order under § 503 not foreclosed).

[#ULLCA602(5)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(5)(C) (person expelled if person is entity that filed statement of dissolution or equivalent, was administratively dissolved, had charter revoked, or had right to conduct business suspended, and not cured within 90 days after notification).

[#ULLCA602(5)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(5)(D) (person expelled if person is unincorporated entity that has been dissolved and whose activities and affairs being wound up).

[#ULLCA602(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(6) (person dissociated when expelled as member by judicial order on application by company or member because person engaged in wrongful conduct, committed material breach, or engaged in conduct making it not reasonably practicable to carry on activities with person).

[#ULLCA602(6)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(6)(A) (person expelled if engaged in wrongful conduct that adversely and materially affected or will affect company's activities and affairs).

[#ULLCA602(6)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(6)(B) (person expelled if committed willfully or persistently material breach of operating agreement or duty or obligation under § 409).

[#ULLCA602(6)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(6)(C) (person expelled if engaged in conduct relating to company's activities making it not reasonably practicable to carry on activities with person as member).

[#ULLCA602(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(7) (in case of individual, person dissociated when individual dies or guardian or conservator appointed or court orders individual incapable of performing duties).

[#ULLCA602(7)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(7)(A) (individual dissociated when individual dies).

[#ULLCA602(7)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(7)(B) (in member-managed company, individual dissociated when guardian or conservator appointed or court orders individual incapable of performing duties under act or operating agreement).

[#ULLCA602(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(8) (in member-managed company, person dissociated when person becomes debtor in bankruptcy, signs assignment for benefit of creditors, or seeks or consents to appointment of trustee, receiver, or liquidator).

[#ULLCA602(8)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(8)(A) (person dissociated when becomes debtor in bankruptcy).

[#ULLCA602(8)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(8)(B) (person dissociated when signs assignment for benefit of creditors).

[#ULLCA602(8)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(8)(C) (person dissociated when seeks, consents to, or acquiesces in appointment of trustee, receiver, or liquidator of person or of all or substantially all person's property).

[#ULLCA602(9)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(9) (in case of person that is trust or acting as member by virtue of being trustee, person dissociated when trust's entire transferable interest in company distributed).

[#ULLCA602(10)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(10) (in case of person that is estate or acting as member by virtue of being personal representative, person dissociated when estate's entire transferable interest in company distributed).

[#ULLCA602(11)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(11) (in case of person not individual, person dissociated when existence of person terminates).

[#ULLCA602(12)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(12) (person dissociated when company participates in merger under Article 10 and company not surviving entity or person otherwise ceases to be member as result of merger).

[#ULLCA602(13)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(13) (person dissociated when company participates in interest exchange under Article 10 and person ceases to be member as result).

[#ULLCA602(14)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(14) (person dissociated when company participates in conversion under Article 10).

[#ULLCA602(15)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(15) (person dissociated when company participates in domestication under Article 10 and person ceases to be member as result).

[#ULLCA602(16)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 602(16) (person dissociated when company dissolves and completes winding up).

[#ULLCA603]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 603 (effect of dissociation).

[#ULLCA603(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 603(a) (if person dissociated as member, person's right to participate in management terminates, duties and obligations under § 409 end with regard to matters arising after dissociation, and transferable interest owned by person immediately before dissociation owned solely as transferee).

[#ULLCA603(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 603(a)(1) (person's right to participate as member in management and conduct of company's activities and affairs terminates).

[#ULLCA603(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 603(a)(2) (person's duties and obligations under § 409 as member end with regard to matters arising and events occurring after person's dissociation).

[#ULLCA603(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 603(a)(3) (subject to § 504 and Article 10, any transferable interest owned by person in capacity as member immediately before dissociation is owned by person solely as transferee).

[#ULLCA603(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 603(b) (person's dissociation as member does not itself discharge person from any debt, obligation, or other liability to company or other members which person incurred while member).


[#ULLCA701]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701 (events causing dissolution).

[#ULLCA701(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a) (company dissolved and activities and affairs must be wound up upon occurrence of specified events).

[#ULLCA701(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(1) (dissolution upon event or circumstance that operating agreement states causes dissolution).

[#ULLCA701(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(2) (dissolution upon affirmative vote or consent of all members).

[#ULLCA701(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(3) (dissolution upon passage of 90 consecutive days during which company has no members unless before end of period consent to admit member given by transferees and at least one person becomes member in accordance with consent).

[#ULLCA701(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(4) (dissolution upon entry by court of order dissolving company on grounds that conduct is unlawful, not reasonably practicable to carry on activities in conformity with certificate and operating agreement, or managers or controlling members acted illegally, fraudulently, or oppressively).

[#ULLCA701(a)(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(4)(A) (court order on grounds that conduct of all or substantially all company's activities and affairs is unlawful).

[#ULLCA701(a)(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(4)(B) (court order on grounds that it is not reasonably practicable to carry on company's activities and affairs in conformity with certificate of organization and operating agreement).

[#ULLCA701(a)(4)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(4)(C) (court order on grounds that managers or those members in control have acted, are acting, or will act illegally or fraudulently or have acted or are acting oppressively and directly harmful to applicant).

[#ULLCA701(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(a)(5) (dissolution upon signing and filing of statement of administrative dissolution by Secretary of State under § 708).

[#ULLCA701(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 701(b) (in proceeding brought under subsection (a)(4)(C), court may order remedy other than dissolution).

[#ULLCA702]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702 (winding up).

[#ULLCA702(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(a) (dissolved company shall wind up activities and affairs and, except as otherwise provided in § 703, company continues after dissolution only for purpose of winding up).

[#ULLCA702(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b) (in winding up, company shall discharge debts, obligations, and liabilities, settle and close activities and affairs, and marshal and distribute assets; and may perform specified acts).

[#ULLCA702(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(1) (shall discharge company's debts, obligations, and other liabilities, settle and close company's activities and affairs, and marshal and distribute assets of company).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2) (may deliver statement of dissolution, preserve company as going concern, prosecute and defend actions, transfer property, settle disputes, deliver statement of termination, and perform other necessary acts).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(A) (may deliver to Secretary of State for filing statement of dissolution stating name of company and that company is dissolved).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(B) (may preserve company activities, affairs, and property as going concern for reasonable time).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(C) (may prosecute and defend actions and proceedings, whether civil, criminal, or administrative).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(D) (may transfer company's property).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(E)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(E) (may settle disputes by mediation or arbitration).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(F)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(F) (may deliver to Secretary of State for filing statement of termination stating name of company and that company is terminated).

[#ULLCA702(b)(2)(G)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(b)(2)(G) (may perform other acts necessary or appropriate to winding up).

[#ULLCA702(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(c) (if dissolved company has no members, legal representative of last person to have been member may wind up activities and affairs; if person does so, has powers of sole manager and is deemed manager for purposes of § 304(a)).

[#ULLCA702(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(d) (if legal representative under subsection (c) declines or fails to wind up, person may be appointed by consent of transferees owning majority of rights to receive distributions; appointed person has powers of sole manager, is deemed manager for purposes of § 304(a), and shall deliver amendment to certificate of organization).

[#ULLCA702(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(d)(1) (appointed person has powers of sole manager under § 407(c) and is deemed manager for purposes of § 304(a)).

[#ULLCA702(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(d)(2) (appointed person shall deliver promptly to Secretary of State for filing amendment to certificate of organization stating company has no members, name and addresses of person, and that person appointed to wind up company).

[#ULLCA702(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(e) (court may order judicial supervision of winding up on application of member or transferee in specified circumstances or in connection with proceeding under § 701(a)(4)).

[#ULLCA702(e)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(e)(1) (court may order judicial supervision on application of member if applicant establishes good cause).

[#ULLCA702(e)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(e)(2) (court may order judicial supervision on application of transferee if company has no members, legal representative declines or fails to wind up, and person not appointed within reasonable time).

[#ULLCA702(e)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 702(e)(3) (court may order judicial supervision in connection with proceeding under § 701(a)(4)).

[#ULLCA703]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703 (rescinding dissolution).

[#ULLCA703(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(a) (company may rescind dissolution unless statement of termination has become effective, court has entered order under § 701(a)(4) dissolving company, or Secretary of State has dissolved company under § 708).

[#ULLCA703(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(b) (rescinding dissolution requires affirmative vote or consent of each member and, if statement of dissolution delivered to Secretary of State, delivery of statement of withdrawal or statement of rescission).

[#ULLCA703(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(b)(1) (rescission requires affirmative vote or consent of each member).

[#ULLCA703(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(b)(2) (if company delivered statement of dissolution to Secretary of State, rescission requires delivery of statement of withdrawal if statement not effective or statement of rescission if statement effective).

[#ULLCA703(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(c) (if company rescinds dissolution, company resumes carrying on activities as if dissolution never occurred, any liability incurred after dissolution determined as if dissolution never occurred, and rights of third party relying on dissolution before notice of rescission not adversely affected).

[#ULLCA703(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(c)(1) (company resumes carrying on activities and affairs as if dissolution had never occurred).

[#ULLCA703(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(c)(2) (subject to paragraph (3), any liability incurred by company after dissolution and before rescission becomes effective determined as if dissolution never occurred).

[#ULLCA703(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 703(c)(3) (rights of third party arising out of conduct in reliance on dissolution before third party knew or had notice of rescission may not be adversely affected).

[#ULLCA704]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704 (known claims against dissolved limited liability company).

[#ULLCA704(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(a) (except as otherwise provided in subsection (d), dissolved company may give notice of known claim under subsection (b), which has effect provided in subsection (c)).

[#ULLCA704(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(b) (dissolved company may in record notify known claimants of dissolution; notice must specify information required in claim, state claim must be in writing with mailing address, state deadline for receipt not less than 120 days after notice received, and state claim will be barred if not received by deadline).

[#ULLCA704(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(b)(1) (notice must specify information required to be included in claim).

[#ULLCA704(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(b)(2) (notice must state claim must be in writing and provide mailing address to which claim is to be sent).
