[#ULLCA704(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(b)(3) (notice must state deadline for receipt of claim, which may not be less than 120 days after date notice received by claimant).

[#ULLCA704(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(b)(4) (notice must state claim will be barred if not received by deadline).

[#ULLCA704(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(c) (claim against dissolved company barred if requirements of subsection (b) met and claim not received by specified deadline or if claim timely received but rejected by company, company causes claimant to receive notice that claim rejected and will be barred unless claimant commences action within 90 days and claimant does not commence action within 90 days).

[#ULLCA704(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(c)(1) (claim barred if not received by specified deadline).

[#ULLCA704(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(c)(2) (if claim timely received but rejected by company, claim barred if company causes claimant to receive notice in record that claim rejected and will be barred unless claimant commences action within 90 days and claimant does not commence required action within 90 days).

[#ULLCA704(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 704(d) (section does not apply to claim based on event occurring after date of dissolution or liability that on that date is contingent).

[#ULLCA705]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705 (other claims against dissolved limited liability company).

[#ULLCA705(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(a) (dissolved company may publish notice of dissolution and request persons having claims to present them in accordance with notice).

[#ULLCA705(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(b) (notice must be published at least once in newspaper of general circulation in county where principal office located, describe information required in claim, state claim must be in writing with mailing address, and state claim barred unless action commenced within three years after publication).

[#ULLCA705(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(b)(1) (notice must be published at least once in newspaper of general circulation in county where dissolved company's principal office located or, if not in state, in county where registered agent's office located).

[#ULLCA705(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(b)(2) (notice must describe information required in claim, state claim must be in writing, and provide mailing address).

[#ULLCA705(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(b)(3) (notice must state claim against company barred unless action to enforce claim commenced within three years after publication of notice).

[#ULLCA705(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(c) (if dissolved company publishes notice in accordance with subsection (b), claim of specified claimants barred unless claimant commences action to enforce claim within three years after publication date).

[#ULLCA705(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(c)(1) (claim barred for claimant that did not receive notice in record under § 704).

[#ULLCA705(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(c)(2) (claim barred for claimant whose claim was timely sent to company but not acted on).

[#ULLCA705(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(c)(3) (claim barred for claimant whose claim is contingent at, or based on event occurring after, date of dissolution).

[#ULLCA705(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(d) (claim not barred under this section or § 704 may be enforced against dissolved company to extent of undistributed assets and, except as otherwise provided in § 706, if assets distributed after dissolution, against member or transferee to extent of proportionate share or assets distributed, whichever less, but total liability may not exceed total amount distributed).

[#ULLCA705(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(d)(1) (claim may be enforced against dissolved company to extent of undistributed assets).

[#ULLCA705(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 705(d)(2) (except as otherwise provided in § 706, if assets distributed after dissolution, claim may be enforced against member or transferee to extent of person's proportionate share of claim or assets distributed to person after dissolution, whichever less, but person's total liability may not exceed total amount of assets distributed to person after dissolution).

[#ULLCA706]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 706 (court proceedings).

[#ULLCA706(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 706(a) (dissolved company that published notice under § 705 may file application with court for determination of amount and form of security for payment of claims reasonably expected to arise after dissolution based on facts known and claims that are contingent, not made known, or based on event occurring after dissolution).

[#ULLCA706(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 706(b) (security not required for any claim that is or is reasonably anticipated to be barred under § 705).

[#ULLCA706(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 706(c) (not later than 10 days after filing application, dissolved company shall give notice of proceeding to each claimant holding contingent claim known to company).

[#ULLCA706(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 706(d) (in proceeding under this section, court may appoint guardian ad litem to represent all claimants whose identities unknown; reasonable fees and expenses of guardian must be paid by dissolved company).

[#ULLCA706(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 706(e) (dissolved company that provides security in amount and form ordered by court satisfies company's obligations with respect to contingent claims, claims not made known, or claims based on event occurring after dissolution, and such claims may not be enforced against member or transferee on account of assets received in liquidation).

[#ULLCA707]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707 (disposition of assets in winding up).

[#ULLCA707(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707(a) (in winding up, company shall apply assets to discharge company's obligations to creditors, including members that are creditors).

[#ULLCA707(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707(b) (after complying with subsection (a), any surplus must be distributed in specified order, subject to any charging order in effect under § 503).

[#ULLCA707(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707(b)(1) (surplus distributed to each person owning transferable interest that reflects contributions made and not previously returned, amount equal to value of unreturned contributions).

[#ULLCA707(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707(b)(2) (surplus distributed among persons owning transferable interests in proportion to their respective rights to share in distributions immediately before dissolution).

[#ULLCA707(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707(c) (if company does not have sufficient surplus to comply with subsection (b)(1), any surplus must be distributed among owners of transferable interests in proportion to value of respective unreturned contributions).

[#ULLCA707(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 707(d) (all distributions made under subsections (b) and (c) must be paid in money).

[#ULLCA708]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 708 (administrative dissolution).

[#ULLCA708(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 708(a) (Secretary of State may commence proceeding to dissolve company administratively if company does not pay fee, tax, interest, or penalty within six months after due, deliver biennial report within six months after due, or have registered agent for 60 consecutive days).

[#ULLCA708(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 708(b) (if Secretary of State determines grounds exist for administratively dissolving company, Secretary shall serve company with notice in record of determination).

[#ULLCA708(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 708(c) (if company does not cure or demonstrate nonexistence of grounds within 60 days after service of notice, Secretary of State shall administratively dissolve company by signing statement of administrative dissolution, filing statement, and serving copy on company).

[#ULLCA708(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 708(d) (company that is administratively dissolved continues in existence as entity but may not carry on any activities except as necessary to wind up activities and affairs or to apply for reinstatement).

[#ULLCA708(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 708(e) (administrative dissolution of company does not terminate authority of registered agent).

[#ULLCA709]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709 (reinstatement).

[#ULLCA709(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(a) (company that is administratively dissolved may apply to Secretary of State for reinstatement not later than two years after effective date of dissolution; application must state name of company at time of dissolution, address of principal office and name and addresses of registered agent, effective date of administrative dissolution, and that grounds did not exist or have been cured).

[#ULLCA709(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(b) (to be reinstated, company must pay all fees, taxes, interest, and penalties due at time of administrative dissolution and all that would have been due while administratively dissolved).

[#ULLCA709(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(c) (if Secretary of State determines application contains required information, is satisfied information is correct, and determines all payments made, Secretary shall cancel statement of administrative dissolution, prepare statement of reinstatement, file statement, and serve copy on company).

[#ULLCA709(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(d) (when reinstatement becomes effective, reinstatement relates back to and takes effect as of effective date of administrative dissolution, company resumes carrying on activities as if administrative dissolution had not occurred, and rights of person arising out of act or omission in reliance on dissolution before person knew or had notice of reinstatement not affected).

[#ULLCA709(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(d)(1) (reinstatement relates back to and takes effect as of effective date of administrative dissolution).

[#ULLCA709(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(d)(2) (company resumes carrying on activities and affairs as if administrative dissolution had not occurred).

[#ULLCA709(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 709(d)(3) (rights of person arising out of act or omission in reliance on dissolution before person knew or had notice of reinstatement not affected).

[#ULLCA710]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 710 (judicial review of denial of reinstatement).

[#ULLCA710(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 710(a) (if Secretary of State denies company's application for reinstatement following administrative dissolution, Secretary shall serve company with notice in record that explains reasons for denial).

[#ULLCA710(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 710(b) (company may seek judicial review of denial of reinstatement in appropriate court not later than 30 days after service of notice of denial).


[#ULLCA801]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 801 (direct action by member).

[#ULLCA801(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 801(a) (subject to subsection (b), member may maintain direct action against another member, manager, or company to enforce member's rights and protect member's interests, including rights under operating agreement or act or arising independently of membership relationship).

[#ULLCA801(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 801(b) (member maintaining direct action must plead and prove actual or threatened injury that is not solely result of injury suffered or threatened to be suffered by company).

[#ULLCA802]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 802 (derivative action).

[#ULLCA802(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 802(1) (member may maintain derivative action to enforce right of company if member first makes demand on other members or managers requesting they cause company to bring action and they do not bring action within reasonable time).

[#ULLCA802(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 802(2) (member may maintain derivative action if demand under paragraph (1) would be futile).

[#ULLCA803]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 803 (proper plaintiff).

[#ULLCA803(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 803(1) (derivative action may be maintained only by person that is member at time action commenced and was member when conduct giving rise to action occurred).

[#ULLCA803(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 803(2) (derivative action may be maintained by person whose status as member devolved by operation of law or pursuant to operating agreement from person that was member at time of conduct).

[#ULLCA804]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 804 (pleading).

[#ULLCA804(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 804(1) (in derivative action, complaint must state with particularity date and content of plaintiff's demand and response to demand by managers or other members).

[#ULLCA804(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 804(2) (in derivative action, complaint must state why demand should be excused as futile).

[#ULLCA805]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805 (special litigation committee).

[#ULLCA805(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(a) (if company named as or made party in derivative proceeding, company may appoint special litigation committee to investigate claims and determine whether pursuing action is in best interests; on committee motion, court shall stay discovery for time reasonably necessary to permit committee to investigate, except court may enforce right to information under § 410 or grant extraordinary relief).

[#ULLCA805(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(a)(1) (stay does not prevent court from enforcing person's right to information under § 410).

[#ULLCA805(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(a)(2) (stay does not prevent court from granting extraordinary relief in form of temporary restraining order or preliminary injunction).

[#ULLCA805(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(b) (special litigation committee must be composed of one or more disinterested and independent individuals, who may be members).

[#ULLCA805(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(c) (special litigation committee may be appointed by specified vote).

[#ULLCA805(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(c)(1) (in member-managed company, appointed by affirmative vote or consent of majority of members not named as parties or, if all members named as parties, by majority of members named as defendants).

[#ULLCA805(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(c)(2) (in manager-managed company, appointed by majority of managers not named as parties or, if all managers named as parties, by majority of managers named as defendants).

[#ULLCA805(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(d) (after appropriate investigation, special litigation committee may determine that it is in best interests of company that proceeding continue under control of plaintiff, continue under control of committee, be settled on terms approved by committee, or be dismissed).

[#ULLCA805(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(d)(1) (committee may determine proceeding should continue under control of plaintiff).

[#ULLCA805(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(d)(2) (committee may determine proceeding should continue under control of committee).

[#ULLCA805(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(d)(3) (committee may determine proceeding should be settled on terms approved by committee).

[#ULLCA805(d)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(d)(4) (committee may determine proceeding should be dismissed).

[#ULLCA805(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 805(e) (after making determination, committee shall file statement of determination and report with court and serve each party; court shall determine whether committee members were disinterested and independent and whether committee conducted investigation and made recommendation in good faith, independently, and with reasonable care, with committee having burden of proof; if court finds affirmatively, court shall enforce determination, otherwise court shall dissolve stay and allow action to continue under plaintiff's control).

[#ULLCA806]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 806 (proceeds and expenses).

[#ULLCA806(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 806(a) (except as otherwise provided in subsection (b), any proceeds or other benefits of derivative action belong to company and not to plaintiff, and if plaintiff receives proceeds, plaintiff shall remit them immediately to company).

[#ULLCA806(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 806(a)(1) (proceeds or benefits of derivative action belong to company and not to plaintiff).

[#ULLCA806(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 806(a)(2) (if plaintiff receives proceeds, plaintiff shall remit them immediately to company).

[#ULLCA806(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 806(b) (if derivative action successful in whole or in part, court may award plaintiff reasonable expenses, including reasonable attorneys' fees and costs, from recovery of company).

[#ULLCA806(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 806(c) (derivative action on behalf of company may not be voluntarily dismissed or settled without court's approval).


[#ULLCA901]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901 (governing law).

[#ULLCA901(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901(a) (law of jurisdiction of formation of foreign company governs internal affairs, liability of member as member and manager as manager for debt or liability of company, and liability of series of company).

[#ULLCA901(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901(a)(1) (law of jurisdiction of formation governs internal affairs of company).

[#ULLCA901(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901(a)(2) (law of jurisdiction of formation governs liability of member as member and manager as manager for debt, obligation, or other liability of company).

[#ULLCA901(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901(a)(3) (law of jurisdiction of formation governs liability of series of company).

[#ULLCA901(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901(b) (foreign company not precluded from registering to do business in state because of any difference between law of its jurisdiction of formation and law of this state).

[#ULLCA901(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 901(c) (registration of foreign company to do business in state does not authorize foreign company to engage in any activities and affairs or exercise any power that company may not engage in or exercise in this state).

[#ULLCA902]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 902 (registration to do business in this state).

[#ULLCA902(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 902(a) (foreign company may not do business in state until it registers with Secretary of State under this article).

[#ULLCA902(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 902(b) (foreign company doing business in state may not maintain action or proceeding in state unless it is registered to do business in state).

[#ULLCA902(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 902(c) (failure of foreign company to register to do business in state does not impair validity of contract or act of company or preclude it from defending action or proceeding in state).

[#ULLCA902(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 902(d) (limitation on liability of member or manager of foreign company not waived solely because company does business in state without registering to do business in state).

[#ULLCA902(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 902(e) (§ 901(a) and (b) applies even if foreign company fails to register under this article).

[#ULLCA903]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 903 (foreign registration statement).

[#ULLCA903(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 903(1) (foreign registration statement must state name of company and, if name does not comply with § 112, alternate name adopted pursuant to § 906(a)).

[#ULLCA903(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 903(2) (foreign registration statement must state that company is foreign limited liability company).

[#ULLCA903(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 903(3) (foreign registration statement must state company's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA903(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 903(4) (foreign registration statement must state street and mailing addresses of company's principal office and, if law of company's jurisdiction of formation requires company to maintain office in that jurisdiction, street and mailing addresses of required office).

[#ULLCA903(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 903(5) (foreign registration statement must state name and street and mailing addresses of company's registered agent in this state).

[#ULLCA904]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 904 (amendment of foreign registration statement).

[#ULLCA904(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 904(1) (registered foreign company shall deliver amendment to Secretary of State for filing if there is change in name of company).

[#ULLCA904(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 904(2) (registered foreign company shall deliver amendment to Secretary of State for filing if there is change in company's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA904(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 904(3) (registered foreign company shall deliver amendment to Secretary of State for filing if there is change in address required by § 903(4)).

[#ULLCA904(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 904(4) (registered foreign company shall deliver amendment to Secretary of State for filing if there is change in information required by § 903(5)).

[#ULLCA905]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905 (activities not constituting doing business).

[#ULLCA905(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a) (activities of foreign company which do not constitute doing business in state include specified activities).

[#ULLCA905(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(1) (not doing business by maintaining, defending, mediating, arbitrating, or settling action or proceeding).

[#ULLCA905(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(2) (not doing business by carrying on any activity concerning internal affairs, including holding meetings of members or managers).

[#ULLCA905(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(3) (not doing business by maintaining accounts in financial institutions).

[#ULLCA905(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(4) (not doing business by maintaining offices or agencies for transfer, exchange, and registration of securities or maintaining trustees or depositories with respect to those securities).

[#ULLCA905(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(5) (not doing business by selling through independent contractors).

[#ULLCA905(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(6) (not doing business by soliciting or obtaining orders by any means if orders require acceptance outside state before they become contracts).

[#ULLCA905(a)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(7) (not doing business by creating or acquiring indebtedness, mortgages, or security interests in property).

[#ULLCA905(a)(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(8) (not doing business by securing or collecting debts or enforcing mortgages or security interests in property securing debts and holding, protecting, or maintaining property).

[#ULLCA905(a)(9)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(9) (not doing business by conducting isolated transaction that is not in course of similar transactions).

[#ULLCA905(a)(10)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(10) (not doing business by owning, without more, property).

[#ULLCA905(a)(11)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(a)(11) (not doing business by doing business in interstate commerce).

[#ULLCA905(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(b) (person does not do business in state solely by being member or manager of foreign company that does business in state).

[#ULLCA905(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 905(c) (this section does not apply in determining contacts or activities that may subject foreign company to service of process, taxation, or regulation under law of state other than this act).

[#ULLCA906]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 906 (noncomplying name of foreign limited liability company).

[#ULLCA906(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 906(a) (foreign company whose name does not comply with § 112 may not register to do business in state until it adopts alternate name that complies with § 112; company that registers under alternate name need not comply with state's assumed or fictitious name statute; after registering with alternate name, company shall do business in state under alternate name, company's name with addition of its jurisdiction of formation, or name company is authorized to use under state's assumed or fictitious name statute).

[#ULLCA906(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 906(a)(1) (company shall do business under alternate name).

[#ULLCA906(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 906(a)(2) (company shall do business under company's name, with addition of its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA906(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 906(a)(3) (company shall do business under name company is authorized to use under state's assumed or fictitious name statute).

[#ULLCA906(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 906(b) (if registered foreign company changes its name to one that does not comply with § 112, it may not do business in state until it complies with subsection (a) by amending its registration to adopt alternate name that complies with § 112).

[#ULLCA907]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 907 (withdrawal deemed on conversion to domestic filing entity or domestic limited liability partnership; registered foreign company that converts to domestic limited liability partnership or to domestic entity whose formation requires delivery of record to Secretary of State for filing is deemed to have withdrawn its registration on effective date of conversion).

[#ULLCA908]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908 (withdrawal on dissolution or conversion to nonfiling entity other than limited liability partnership).

[#ULLCA908(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a) (registered foreign company that has dissolved and completed winding up or has converted to domestic or foreign entity whose formation does not require public filing of record, other than limited liability partnership, shall deliver statement of withdrawal to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA908(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(1) (in case of company that has completed winding up, statement must state company's name and jurisdiction of formation and that company surrenders its registration to do business in state).

[#ULLCA908(a)(1)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(1)(A) (statement must state company's name and jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA908(a)(1)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(1)(B) (statement must state that company surrenders its registration to do business in state).

[#ULLCA908(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(2) (in case of company that has converted, statement must state name of converting company and its jurisdiction of formation, type of entity to which company has converted and its jurisdiction of formation, that converted entity surrenders converting company's registration and revokes authority of converting company's registered agent, and mailing address to which service of process may be made under subsection (b)).

[#ULLCA908(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(2)(A) (statement must state name of converting company and its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA908(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(2)(B) (statement must state type of entity to which company has converted and its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA908(a)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(2)(C) (statement must state that converted entity surrenders converting company's registration and revokes authority of converting company's registered agent to act as registered agent in state on behalf of company or converted entity).

[#ULLCA908(a)(2)(D)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(a)(2)(D) (statement must state mailing address to which service of process may be made under subsection (b)).

[#ULLCA908(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 908(b) (after withdrawal under this section has become effective, service of process in any action or proceeding based on cause of action arising during time foreign company was registered to do business in state may be made pursuant to § 119).

[#ULLCA909]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909 (transfer of registration).

[#ULLCA909(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a) (when registered foreign company has merged into foreign entity not registered to do business in state or has converted to foreign entity required to register with Secretary of State to do business in state, foreign entity shall deliver application for transfer of registration to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA909(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a)(1) (application must state name of registered foreign company before merger or conversion).

[#ULLCA909(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a)(2) (application must state that before merger or conversion registration pertained to foreign limited liability company).

[#ULLCA909(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a)(3) (application must state name of applicant foreign entity into which foreign company has merged or to which it has been converted and, if name does not comply with § 112, alternate name adopted pursuant to § 906(a)).

[#ULLCA909(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a)(4) (application must state type of entity of applicant foreign entity and its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA909(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a)(5) (application must state street and mailing addresses of principal office of applicant foreign entity and, if law of entity's jurisdiction of formation requires entity to maintain office in that jurisdiction, street and mailing addresses of that office).

[#ULLCA909(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(a)(6) (application must state name and street and mailing addresses of applicant foreign entity's registered agent in this state).

[#ULLCA909(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 909(b) (when application for transfer of registration takes effect, registration of foreign company to do business in state is transferred without interruption to foreign entity into which company has merged or to which it has been converted).

[#ULLCA910]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910 (termination of registration).

[#ULLCA910(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(a) (Secretary of State may terminate registration of registered foreign company if company does not pay fee, tax, interest, or penalty within 60 days after due date, deliver biennial report within 60 days after due date, have registered agent as required by § 115, or deliver statement of change within 30 days after change in name or address of registered agent).

[#ULLCA910(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(a)(1) (may terminate if company does not pay fee, tax, interest, or penalty not later than 60 days after due date).

[#ULLCA910(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(a)(2) (may terminate if company does not deliver biennial report not later than 60 days after due date).

[#ULLCA910(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(a)(3) (may terminate if company does not have registered agent as required by § 115).

[#ULLCA910(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(a)(4) (may terminate if company does not deliver statement of change not later than 30 days after change in name or address of registered agent).

[#ULLCA910(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(b) (Secretary of State may terminate registration by filing notice of termination or noting termination in records and delivering copy to company's registered agent or, if company does not have registered agent, to company's principal office).

[#ULLCA910(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(b)(1) (Secretary may terminate by filing notice of termination or noting termination in records of Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA910(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(b)(2) (Secretary may terminate by delivering copy of notice or information in notation to company's registered agent or, if company does not have registered agent, to company's principal office).

[#ULLCA910(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(c) (notice must state or information in notation must include effective date of termination, which must be at least 60 days after date Secretary of State delivers copy, and grounds for termination under subsection (a)).

[#ULLCA910(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(c)(1) (notice or notation must include effective date of termination, which must be at least 60 days after date Secretary of State delivers copy).

[#ULLCA910(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(c)(2) (notice or notation must include grounds for termination under subsection (a)).

[#ULLCA910(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 910(d) (authority of registered foreign company to do business in state ceases on effective date of notice of termination or notation, unless before that date company cures each ground for termination; if company cures each ground, Secretary of State shall file record so stating).

[#ULLCA911]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911 (withdrawal of registration of registered foreign limited liability company).

[#ULLCA911(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911(a) (registered foreign company may withdraw its registration by delivering statement of withdrawal to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA911(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911(a)(1) (statement of withdrawal must state name of company and its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA911(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911(a)(2) (statement of withdrawal must state that company is not doing business in state and that it withdraws its registration to do business in state).

[#ULLCA911(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911(a)(3) (statement of withdrawal must state that company revokes authority of its registered agent to accept service on its behalf in state).

[#ULLCA911(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911(a)(4) (statement of withdrawal must state address to which service of process may be made under subsection (b)).

[#ULLCA911(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 911(b) (after withdrawal of registration of foreign company, service of process in any action or proceeding based on cause of action arising during time company was registered to do business in state may be made pursuant to § 119).

[#ULLCA912]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 912 (action by attorney general; Attorney General may maintain action to enjoin foreign limited liability company from doing business in state in violation of this article).



[#ULLCA1001]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001 (definitions for article 10).

[#ULLCA1001(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(1) ("acquired entity" means entity, all of one or more classes or series of interests of which are acquired in interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1001(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(2) ("acquiring entity" means entity that acquires all of one or more classes or series of interests of acquired entity in interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1001(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(3) ("conversion" means transaction authorized by Part 4).

[#ULLCA1001(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(4) ("converted entity" means converting entity as it continues in existence after conversion).

[#ULLCA1001(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(5) ("converting entity" means domestic entity that approves plan of conversion pursuant to § 1043 or foreign entity that approves conversion pursuant to law of its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1001(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(6) ("distributional interest" means right under unincorporated entity's organic law and organic rules to receive distributions from entity).

[#ULLCA1001(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(7) ("domestic" with respect to entity means governed as to its internal affairs by law of this state).

[#ULLCA1001(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(8) ("domesticated limited liability company" means domesticating limited liability company as it continues in existence after domestication).

[#ULLCA1001(9)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(9) ("domesticating limited liability company" means domestic limited liability company that approves plan of domestication pursuant to § 1053 or foreign limited liability company that approves domestication pursuant to law of its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1001(10)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(10) ("domestication" means transaction authorized by Part 5).

[#ULLCA1001(11)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(11) ("entity" means business corporation, nonprofit corporation, general partnership including limited liability partnership, limited partnership including limited liability limited partnership, limited liability company, general cooperative association, limited cooperative association, unincorporated nonprofit association, statutory trust, business trust, common-law business trust, or other person that has legal existence separate from any interest holder or power to acquire interest in real property in its own name; does not include individual, trust with predominantly donative purpose or charitable trust, association or relationship that is not entity listed and is not partnership, decedent's estate, or government or governmental subdivision).

[#ULLCA1001(11)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(11)(A) (entity includes business corporation, nonprofit corporation, general partnership, limited partnership, limited liability company, cooperative associations, unincorporated nonprofit association, and trusts with separate legal existence or power to acquire real property).

[#ULLCA1001(11)(A)(i)-(x)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(11)(A)(i)-(x) (listing types of entities).

[#ULLCA1001(11)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(11)(B) (entity does not include individual, donative trust, charitable trust, non-entity association, decedent's estate, or government).

[#ULLCA1001(12)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(12) ("filing entity" means entity whose formation requires filing of public organic record; term does not include limited liability partnership).

[#ULLCA1001(13)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(13) ("foreign" with respect to entity means entity governed as to its internal affairs by law of jurisdiction other than this state).

[#ULLCA1001(14)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(14) ("governance interest" means right under organic law or organic rules of unincorporated entity, other than as governor, agent, assignee, or proxy, to receive or demand access to information or books and records, vote for or consent to election of governors, or receive notice of or vote on issues involving internal affairs).

[#ULLCA1001(15)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(15) ("governor" means director of business corporation or nonprofit corporation, general partner of general or limited partnership, manager of manager-managed LLC, member of member-managed LLC, director of cooperative association, manager of unincorporated nonprofit association, trustee of trust, or other person under whose authority powers of entity are exercised and under whose direction activities and affairs are managed).

[#ULLCA1001(16)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(16) ("interest" means share in business corporation, membership in nonprofit corporation, partnership interest, membership interest in LLC, share or member's interest in cooperative association, membership in unincorporated nonprofit association, beneficial interest in trust, or governance or distributional interest in other unincorporated entity).

[#ULLCA1001(17)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(17) ("interest exchange" means transaction authorized by Part 3).

[#ULLCA1001(18)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(18) ("interest holder" means shareholder of business corporation, member of nonprofit corporation, general or limited partner, member of LLC, shareholder or member of cooperative association, member of unincorporated nonprofit association, beneficiary of trust, or other direct holder of interest).

[#ULLCA1001(19)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(19) ("interest holder liability" means personal liability for liability of entity imposed on person solely by reason of status as interest holder or by organic rules, or obligation of interest holder under organic rules to contribute to entity).

[#ULLCA1001(20)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(20) ("merger" means transaction authorized by Part 2).

[#ULLCA1001(21)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(21) ("merging entity" means entity that is party to merger and exists immediately before merger becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1001(22)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(22) ("organic law" means law of entity's jurisdiction of formation governing internal affairs of entity).

[#ULLCA1001(23)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(23) ("organic rules" means public organic record and private organic rules of entity).

[#ULLCA1001(24)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(24) ("plan" means plan of merger, plan of interest exchange, plan of conversion, or plan of domestication).

[#ULLCA1001(25)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(25) ("plan of conversion" means plan under § 1042).

[#ULLCA1001(26)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(26) ("plan of domestication" means plan under § 1052).

[#ULLCA1001(27)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(27) ("plan of interest exchange" means plan under § 1032).

[#ULLCA1001(28)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(28) ("plan of merger" means plan under § 1022).

[#ULLCA1001(29)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(29) ("private organic rules" means rules, whether or not in record, that govern internal affairs of entity, are binding on all interest holders, and are not part of public organic record; includes bylaws, partnership agreements, operating agreements, governing principles, and trust instruments).

[#ULLCA1001(30)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(30) ("protected agreement" means record evidencing indebtedness and related agreement in effect on effective date of act, agreement binding on entity on effective date, organic rules in effect on effective date, or agreement binding on governors or interest holders on effective date).

[#ULLCA1001(31)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(31) ("public organic record" means record whose filing by Secretary of State is required to form entity and any amendment or restatement; includes articles of incorporation, certificate of limited partnership, certificate of organization, and certificate of trust).

[#ULLCA1001(32)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(32) ("registered foreign entity" means foreign entity that is registered to do business in this state pursuant to record filed by Secretary of State).

[#ULLCA1001(33)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(33) ("statement of conversion" means statement under § 1045).

[#ULLCA1001(34)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(34) ("statement of domestication" means statement under § 1055).

[#ULLCA1001(35)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(35) ("statement of interest exchange" means statement under § 1035).

[#ULLCA1001(36)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(36) ("statement of merger" means statement under § 1025).

[#ULLCA1001(37)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(37) ("surviving entity" means entity that continues in existence after or is created by merger).

[#ULLCA1001(38)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1001(38) ("type of entity" means generic form of entity recognized at common law or formed under organic law).

[#ULLCA1002]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1002 (relationship of article to other laws).

[#ULLCA1002(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1002(a) (article does not authorize act prohibited by and does not affect application or requirements of law other than article).

[#ULLCA1002(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1002(b) (transaction under article may not create or impair right, duty or obligation under statutory law of state other than article relating to change in control, takeover, business combination, control-share acquisition, or similar transaction involving domestic merging, acquired, converting, or domesticating business corporation unless transaction satisfies requirements of law or approval is by sufficient vote).

[#ULLCA1003]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1003 (required notice or approval).

[#ULLCA1003(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1003(a) (domestic or foreign entity required to give notice to or obtain approval of governmental agency or officer to be party to merger must give notice or obtain approval to be party to interest exchange, conversion, or domestication).

[#ULLCA1003(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1003(b) (property held for charitable purpose under law of state by domestic or foreign entity immediately before transaction may not be diverted from objects for which transferred unless entity obtains appropriate order of court specifying disposition).

[#ULLCA1003(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1003(c) (bequest, devise, gift, grant, or promise to merging entity that is not surviving entity which takes effect or remains payable after merger inures to surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1003(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1003(d) (trust obligation that would govern property if transferred to nonsurviving entity applies to property transferred to surviving entity).


[#ULLCA1021]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1021 (merger authorized).

[#ULLCA1021(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1021(a) (by complying with this part, one or more domestic limited liability companies may merge with one or more domestic or foreign entities into domestic or foreign surviving entity, or two or more foreign entities may merge into domestic limited liability company).

[#ULLCA1021(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1021(a)(1) (one or more domestic limited liability companies may merge with one or more domestic or foreign entities into domestic or foreign surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1021(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1021(a)(2) (two or more foreign entities may merge into domestic limited liability company).

[#ULLCA1021(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1021(b) (by complying with provisions applicable to foreign entities, foreign entity may be party to merger or surviving entity if merger is authorized by law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1022]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022 (plan of merger).

[#ULLCA1022(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a) (domestic limited liability company may become party to merger by approving plan of merger; plan must be in record and contain specified information).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(1) (plan must state name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of each merging entity).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(2) (if surviving entity to be created in merger, plan must include statement to that effect and entity's name, jurisdiction of formation, and type).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(3) (plan must state manner of converting interests in each party to merger into interests, securities, obligations, money, other property, rights to acquire interests or securities, or any combination).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(4) (if surviving entity exists before merger, plan must include proposed amendments to public organic record, if any, and private organic rules in record).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(4)(A) (proposed amendments to public organic record).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(4)(B) (proposed amendments to private organic rules in record).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(5) (if surviving entity to be created in merger, plan must include proposed public organic record, if any, and full text of private organic rules proposed to be in record).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(5)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(5)(A) (proposed public organic record).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(5)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(5)(B) (full text of private organic rules proposed to be in record).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(6) (plan must include other terms and conditions of merger).

[#ULLCA1022(a)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(a)(7) (plan must include any other provision required by law of merging entity's jurisdiction of formation or organic rules).

[#ULLCA1022(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1022(b) (in addition to requirements of subsection (a), plan may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1023]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023 (approval of merger).

[#ULLCA1023(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(a) (plan of merger not effective unless approved by domestic merging limited liability company and in record by each member with interest holder liability after merger, subject to exceptions).

[#ULLCA1023(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(a)(1) (plan must be approved by domestic merging limited liability company by all members entitled to vote on or consent to any matter).

[#ULLCA1023(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(a)(2) (plan must be approved in record by each member of domestic merging company that will have interest holder liability for debts incurred after merger, unless operating agreement provides for approval by fewer than all members or member consented to or voted for such provision or became member after adoption).

[#ULLCA1023(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(a)(2)(A) (exception if operating agreement provides in record for approval by affirmative vote or consent of fewer than all members).

[#ULLCA1023(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(a)(2)(B) (exception if member consented in record to or voted for operating agreement provision or became member after adoption).

[#ULLCA1023(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(b) (merger involving domestic merging entity that is not limited liability company not effective unless approved in accordance with organic law).

[#ULLCA1023(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1023(c) (merger involving foreign merging entity not effective unless approved in accordance with law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1024]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024 (amendment or abandonment of plan of merger).

[#ULLCA1024(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(a) (plan of merger may be amended only with consent of each party to plan, except as otherwise provided in plan).

[#ULLCA1024(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(b) (domestic merging limited liability company may approve amendment in same manner as plan was approved or by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on merger is entitled to vote on certain amendments).

[#ULLCA1024(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(b)(1) (amendment may be approved in same manner as plan was approved if plan does not provide manner of amendment).

[#ULLCA1024(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(b)(2) (amendment may be approved by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on merger entitled to vote on amendments changing consideration, organic records/rules of surviving entity, or other terms adversely affecting member).

[#ULLCA1024(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(b)(2)(A) (member may vote on amendment changing amount or kind of consideration to be received).

[#ULLCA1024(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(b)(2)(B) (member may vote on amendment changing public organic record or private organic rules of surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1024(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(b)(2)(C) (member may vote on amendment changing other terms or conditions if change would adversely affect member in material respect).

[#ULLCA1024(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(c) (after plan approved and before statement of merger effective, plan may be abandoned as provided in plan; unless prohibited, domestic merging company may abandon in same manner as approved).

[#ULLCA1024(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(d) (if plan abandoned after statement of merger delivered but before effective, statement of abandonment signed by party must be delivered to Secretary of State for filing; statement takes effect on filing and merger is abandoned).

[#ULLCA1024(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(d)(1) (statement of abandonment must contain name of each party to plan).

[#ULLCA1024(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(d)(2) (statement of abandonment must contain date statement of merger was filed).

[#ULLCA1024(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1024(d)(3) (statement of abandonment must state that merger has been abandoned in accordance with this section).

[#ULLCA1025]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025 (statement of merger; effective date of merger).

[#ULLCA1025(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(a) (statement of merger must be signed by each merging entity and delivered to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA1025(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b) (statement of merger must contain specified information).

[#ULLCA1025(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b)(1) (statement must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of each merging entity that is not surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1025(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b)(2) (statement must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1025(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b)(3) (statement must state merger was approved by each domestic merging entity in accordance with this part and by each foreign merging entity in accordance with law of its jurisdiction).

[#ULLCA1025(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b)(4) (if surviving entity exists before merger and is domestic filing entity, statement must include any amendment to its public organic record approved as part of plan).

[#ULLCA1025(b)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b)(5) (if surviving entity created by merger and is domestic filing entity, statement must include its public organic record as attachment).

[#ULLCA1025(b)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(b)(6) (if surviving entity created by merger and is domestic limited liability partnership, statement must include its statement of qualification as attachment).

[#ULLCA1025(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(c) (in addition to requirements of subsection (b), statement may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1025(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(d) (if surviving entity is domestic entity, its public organic record must satisfy requirements of law of state, except need not be signed).

[#ULLCA1025(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(e) (plan of merger signed by all merging entities that meets all requirements of subsection (b) may be filed instead of statement and has same effect; references to statement of merger refer to plan filed under this subsection).

[#ULLCA1025(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1025(f) (if surviving entity is domestic limited liability company, merger becomes effective when statement is effective; in all other cases, effective on later of date and time provided by organic law of surviving entity or when statement is effective).

[#ULLCA1026]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026 (effect of merger).

[#ULLCA1026(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a) (when merger becomes effective, specified consequences follow).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(1) (surviving entity continues or comes into existence).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(2) (each merging entity that is not surviving entity ceases to exist).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(3) (all property of each merging entity vests in surviving entity without transfer, reversion, or impairment).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(4) (all debts, obligations, and other liabilities of each merging entity are debts, obligations, and other liabilities of surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(5) (except as otherwise provided by law or plan, all rights, privileges, immunities, powers, and purposes of each merging entity vest in surviving entity).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(6) (if surviving entity exists before merger, all its property continues vested, it remains subject to all debts and liabilities, and all its rights continue vested).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(6)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(6)(A) (all property continues vested without transfer, reversion, or impairment).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(6)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(6)(B) (entity remains subject to all debts, obligations, and other liabilities).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(6)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(6)(C) (all rights, privileges, immunities, powers, and purposes continue vested).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(7) (name of surviving entity may be substituted for name of any merging entity in any pending action or proceeding).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(8) (if surviving entity exists before merger, its public organic record is amended to extent provided in statement and private organic rules are amended to extent provided in plan).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(8)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(8)(A) (public organic record amended to extent provided in statement of merger).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(8)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(8)(B) (private organic rules amended to extent provided in plan).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(9)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(9) (if surviving entity created by merger, its private organic rules are effective and, if filing entity, public organic record becomes effective, or if limited liability partnership, statement of qualification becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(9)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(9)(A) (if filing entity, public organic record becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(9)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(9)(B) (if limited liability partnership, statement of qualification becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1026(a)(10)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(a)(10) (interests in each merging entity to be converted are converted, and interest holders entitled only to rights provided under plan and any appraisal rights under § 1006 and organic law).

[#ULLCA1026(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(b) (except as otherwise provided in organic law or organic rules, merger does not give rise to rights that interest holder, governor, or third party would have upon dissolution, liquidation, or winding up).

[#ULLCA1026(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(c) (person without interest holder liability who becomes subject to it as result of merger has liability only to extent provided by organic law and only for debts incurred after merger becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1026(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(d) (when merger becomes effective, interest holder liability of person ceasing to hold interest in domestic merging company subject to specified rules).

[#ULLCA1026(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(d)(1) (merger does not discharge interest holder liability incurred before merger became effective).

[#ULLCA1026(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(d)(2) (person does not have interest holder liability for debt incurred after merger becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1026(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(d)(3) (act continues to apply to release, collection, or discharge of preserved interest holder liability as if merger had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1026(d)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(d)(4) (person has whatever rights of contribution provided by act, other law, or operating agreement with respect to preserved liability as if merger had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1026(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(e) (when merger becomes effective, foreign entity that is surviving entity may be served with process in state for collection and enforcement of debts and liabilities of domestic merging company as provided in § 119).

[#ULLCA1026(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1026(f) (when merger becomes effective, registration to do business in state of any foreign merging entity that is not surviving entity is canceled).


[#ULLCA1031]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1031 (interest exchange authorized).

[#ULLCA1031(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1031(a) (by complying with this part, domestic limited liability company may acquire all of one or more classes or series of interests of another domestic or foreign entity, or all of one or more classes or series of interests of domestic limited liability company may be acquired by another domestic or foreign entity).

[#ULLCA1031(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1031(a)(1) (domestic limited liability company may acquire all of one or more classes or series of interests of another domestic or foreign entity in exchange for interests, securities, obligations, money, other property, rights to acquire interests or securities, or any combination).

[#ULLCA1031(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1031(a)(2) (all of one or more classes or series of interests of domestic limited liability company may be acquired by another domestic or foreign entity in exchange for interests, securities, obligations, money, other property, rights to acquire interests or securities, or any combination).

[#ULLCA1031(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1031(b) (by complying with provisions applicable to foreign entities, foreign entity may be acquiring or acquired entity if interest exchange authorized by law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1031(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1031(c) (if protected agreement contains provision applying to merger but not referring to interest exchange, provision applies to interest exchange in which domestic limited liability company is acquired entity as if interest exchange were merger until provision amended after effective date of act).

[#ULLCA1032]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032 (plan of interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1032(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a) (domestic limited liability company may be acquired entity by approving plan of interest exchange in record containing specified information).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(1) (plan must contain name of acquired entity).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(2) (plan must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of acquiring entity).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(3) (plan must contain manner of converting interests in acquired entity into interests, securities, obligations, money, other property, rights to acquire interests or securities, or any combination).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(4) (plan must contain any proposed amendments to certificate of organization and operating agreement of acquired entity that are or are proposed to be in record).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(4)(A) (proposed amendments to certificate of organization).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(4)(B) (proposed amendments to operating agreement that are or are proposed to be in record).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(5) (plan must contain other terms and conditions of interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1032(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(a)(6) (plan must contain any other provision required by law of state or operating agreement of acquired entity).

[#ULLCA1032(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1032(b) (in addition to requirements of subsection (a), plan may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1033]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033 (approval of interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1033(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(a) (plan not effective unless approved by domestic acquired limited liability company and in record by each member with interest holder liability, subject to exceptions).

[#ULLCA1033(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(a)(1) (plan must be approved by all members of domestic acquired limited liability company entitled to vote on or consent to any matter).

[#ULLCA1033(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(a)(2) (plan must be approved in record by each member that will have interest holder liability after interest exchange, unless operating agreement provides for approval by fewer than all members or member consented to or voted for such provision or became member after adoption).

[#ULLCA1033(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(a)(2)(A) (exception if operating agreement provides in record for approval by affirmative vote or consent of fewer than all members).

[#ULLCA1033(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(a)(2)(B) (exception if member consented in record to or voted for operating agreement provision or became member after adoption).

[#ULLCA1033(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(b) (interest exchange involving domestic acquired entity that is not limited liability company not effective unless approved in accordance with organic law).

[#ULLCA1033(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(c) (interest exchange involving foreign acquired entity not effective unless approved in accordance with law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1033(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1033(d) (except as otherwise provided in organic law or organic rules, interest holders of acquiring entity not required to approve interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1034]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034 (amendment or abandonment of plan of interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1034(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(a) (plan may be amended only with consent of each party to plan, except as otherwise provided in plan).

[#ULLCA1034(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(b) (domestic acquired limited liability company may approve amendment in same manner as plan was approved or by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on interest exchange entitled to vote on certain amendments).

[#ULLCA1034(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(b)(1) (amendment may be approved in same manner as plan was approved if plan does not provide manner of amendment).

[#ULLCA1034(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(b)(2) (amendment may be approved by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on interest exchange entitled to vote on amendments changing consideration, organic records/rules, or other terms adversely affecting member).

[#ULLCA1034(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(b)(2)(A) (member may vote on amendment changing amount or kind of consideration to be received).

[#ULLCA1034(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(b)(2)(B) (member may vote on amendment changing certificate of organization or operating agreement that will be in effect after interest exchange, except for changes not requiring member approval).

[#ULLCA1034(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(b)(2)(C) (member may vote on amendment changing other terms or conditions if change would adversely affect member in material respect).

[#ULLCA1034(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(c) (after plan approved and before statement effective, plan may be abandoned as provided in plan; unless prohibited, domestic acquired company may abandon in same manner as approved).

[#ULLCA1034(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(d) (if plan abandoned after statement delivered but before effective, statement of abandonment signed by acquired company must be delivered to Secretary of State for filing; statement takes effect on filing and interest exchange abandoned).

[#ULLCA1034(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(d)(1) (statement must contain name of acquired company).

[#ULLCA1034(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(d)(2) (statement must contain date statement of interest exchange was filed).

[#ULLCA1034(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1034(d)(3) (statement must state that interest exchange has been abandoned in accordance with this section).

[#ULLCA1035]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035 (statement of interest exchange; effective date of interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1035(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(a) (statement of interest exchange must be signed by domestic acquired limited liability company and delivered to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA1035(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(b) (statement must contain specified information).

[#ULLCA1035(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(b)(1) (statement must contain name of acquired limited liability company).

[#ULLCA1035(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(b)(2) (statement must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of acquiring entity).

[#ULLCA1035(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(b)(3) (statement must state plan was approved by acquired company in accordance with this part).

[#ULLCA1035(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(b)(4) (statement must contain any amendments to acquired company's certificate of organization approved as part of plan).

[#ULLCA1035(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(c) (in addition to requirements of subsection (b), statement may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1035(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(d) (plan signed by domestic acquired company that meets all requirements may be filed instead of statement and has same effect; references to statement refer to plan filed under this subsection).

[#ULLCA1035(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1035(e) (interest exchange becomes effective when statement is effective).

[#ULLCA1036]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036 (effect of interest exchange).

[#ULLCA1036(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(a) (when interest exchange becomes effective, specified consequences follow).

[#ULLCA1036(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(a)(1) (interests in acquired company that are subject of interest exchange are converted, and members holding those interests entitled only to rights under plan and any appraisal rights under § 1006).

[#ULLCA1036(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(a)(2) (acquiring entity becomes interest holder of interests stated in plan to be acquired).

[#ULLCA1036(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(a)(3) (certificate of organization of acquired company amended to extent provided in statement).

[#ULLCA1036(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(a)(4) (provisions of operating agreement of acquired company that are to be in record amended to extent provided in plan).

[#ULLCA1036(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(b) (except as otherwise provided in operating agreement, interest exchange does not give rise to rights that member, manager, or third party would have upon dissolution, liquidation, or winding up).

[#ULLCA1036(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(c) (person without interest holder liability who becomes subject to it has liability only to extent provided by organic law and only for debts incurred after interest exchange becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1036(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(d) (when interest exchange becomes effective, interest holder liability of person ceasing to hold interest in domestic acquired company subject to specified rules).

[#ULLCA1036(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(d)(1) (interest exchange does not discharge interest holder liability incurred before interest exchange became effective).

[#ULLCA1036(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(d)(2) (person does not have interest holder liability for debt incurred after interest exchange becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1036(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(d)(3) (act continues to apply to release, collection, or discharge of preserved interest holder liability as if interest exchange had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1036(d)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1036(d)(4) (person has whatever rights of contribution provided by act, other law, or operating agreement with respect to preserved liability as if interest exchange had not occurred).


[#ULLCA1041]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1041 (conversion authorized).

[#ULLCA1041(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1041(a) (by complying with this part, domestic limited liability company may become domestic entity that is different type of entity or foreign entity that is different type of entity if conversion authorized by law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1041(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1041(a)(1) (domestic limited liability company may become domestic entity that is different type of entity).

[#ULLCA1041(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1041(a)(2) (domestic limited liability company may become foreign entity that is different type of entity if conversion authorized by law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1041(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1041(b) (by complying with provisions applicable to foreign entities, foreign entity that is not foreign limited liability company may become domestic limited liability company if conversion authorized by law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1041(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1041(c) (if protected agreement contains provision applying to merger but not referring to conversion, provision applies to conversion of company as if conversion were merger until provision amended after effective date of act).

[#ULLCA1042]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042 (plan of conversion).

[#ULLCA1042(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a) (domestic limited liability company may convert by approving plan of conversion in record containing specified information).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(1) (plan must contain name of converting limited liability company).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(2) (plan must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of converted entity).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(3) (plan must contain manner of converting interests in converting company into interests, securities, obligations, money, other property, rights to acquire interests or securities, or any combination).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(4) (plan must contain proposed public organic record of converted entity if it will be filing entity).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(5) (plan must contain full text of private organic rules of converted entity which are proposed to be in record).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(6) (plan must contain other terms and conditions of conversion).

[#ULLCA1042(a)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(a)(7) (plan must contain any other provision required by law of state or operating agreement of converting company).

[#ULLCA1042(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1042(b) (in addition to requirements of subsection (a), plan may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1043]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043 (approval of conversion).

[#ULLCA1043(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(a) (plan not effective unless approved by domestic converting limited liability company and in record by each member with interest holder liability, subject to exceptions).

[#ULLCA1043(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(a)(1) (plan must be approved by all members of domestic converting company entitled to vote on or consent to any matter).

[#ULLCA1043(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(a)(2) (plan must be approved in record by each member that will have interest holder liability after conversion, unless operating agreement provides for approval by fewer than all members or member consented to or voted for such provision or became member after adoption).

[#ULLCA1043(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(a)(2)(A) (exception if operating agreement provides in record for approval by affirmative vote or consent of fewer than all members).

[#ULLCA1043(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(a)(2)(B) (exception if member voted for or consented in record to operating agreement provision or became member after adoption).

[#ULLCA1043(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(b) (conversion involving domestic converting entity that is not limited liability company not effective unless approved in accordance with organic law).

[#ULLCA1043(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1043(c) (conversion of foreign converting entity not effective unless approved in accordance with law of foreign entity's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1044]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044 (amendment or abandonment of plan of conversion).

[#ULLCA1044(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(a) (plan may be amended in same manner as approved or by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on conversion entitled to vote on certain amendments).

[#ULLCA1044(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(a)(1) (plan may be amended in same manner as approved if plan does not provide manner of amendment).
