[#ULLCA1044(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(a)(2) (plan may be amended by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on conversion entitled to vote on amendments changing consideration, organic records/rules, or other terms adversely affecting member).

[#ULLCA1044(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(a)(2)(A) (member may vote on amendment changing amount or kind of consideration to be received).

[#ULLCA1044(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(a)(2)(B) (member may vote on amendment changing public organic record or private organic rules of converted entity except for changes not requiring approval).

[#ULLCA1044(a)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(a)(2)(C) (member may vote on amendment changing other terms or conditions if change would adversely affect member in material respect).

[#ULLCA1044(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(b) (after plan approved and before statement effective, plan may be abandoned as provided in plan; unless prohibited, domestic converting company may abandon in same manner as approved).

[#ULLCA1044(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(c) (if plan abandoned after statement delivered but before effective, statement of abandonment signed by converting entity must be delivered to Secretary of State for filing; statement takes effect on filing and conversion abandoned).

[#ULLCA1044(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(c)(1) (statement must contain name of converting company).

[#ULLCA1044(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(c)(2) (statement must contain date statement of conversion was filed).

[#ULLCA1044(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1044(c)(3) (statement must state conversion has been abandoned in accordance with this section).

[#ULLCA1045]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045 (statement of conversion; effective date of conversion).

[#ULLCA1045(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(a) (statement of conversion must be signed by converting entity and delivered to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA1045(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(b) (statement must contain specified information).

[#ULLCA1045(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(b)(1) (statement must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of converting entity).

[#ULLCA1045(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(b)(2) (statement must contain name, jurisdiction of formation, and type of entity of converted entity).

[#ULLCA1045(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(b)(3) (if converting entity is domestic limited liability company, statement must state plan was approved in accordance with this part; if foreign entity, statement must state conversion approved in accordance with law of its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1045(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(b)(4) (if converted entity is domestic filing entity, statement must include its public organic record as attachment).

[#ULLCA1045(b)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(b)(5) (if converted entity is domestic limited liability partnership, statement must include its statement of qualification as attachment).

[#ULLCA1045(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(c) (in addition to requirements of subsection (b), statement may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1045(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(d) (if converted entity is domestic entity, its public organic record must satisfy requirements of law of state, except need not be signed).

[#ULLCA1045(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(e) (plan signed by domestic converting company that meets all requirements may be filed instead of statement and has same effect; references to statement refer to plan filed under this subsection).

[#ULLCA1045(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1045(f) (if converted entity is domestic limited liability company, conversion becomes effective when statement is effective; in all other cases, effective on later of date and time provided by organic law of converted entity or when statement is effective).

[#ULLCA1046]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046 (effect of conversion).

[#ULLCA1046(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a) (when conversion becomes effective, specified consequences follow).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(1) (converted entity is organized under and subject to organic law of converted entity and is same entity without interruption as converting entity).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(1)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(1)(A) (converted entity organized under and subject to organic law of converted entity).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(1)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(1)(B) (converted entity same entity without interruption as converting entity).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(2) (all property of converting entity continues to be vested in converted entity without transfer, reversion, or impairment).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(3) (all debts, obligations, and other liabilities of converting entity continue as debts, obligations, and other liabilities of converted entity).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(4) (except as otherwise provided by law or plan, all rights, privileges, immunities, powers, and purposes of converting entity remain in converted entity).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(5) (name of converted entity may be substituted for name of converting entity in any pending action or proceeding).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(6) (certificate of organization of converted entity becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(7) (provisions of operating agreement of converted entity which are to be in record, if any, approved as part of plan become effective).

[#ULLCA1046(a)(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(a)(8) (interests in converting entity are converted, and interest holders entitled only to rights under plan and any appraisal rights under § 1006).

[#ULLCA1046(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(b) (except as otherwise provided in operating agreement of domestic converting company, conversion does not give rise to rights that member, manager, or third party would have upon dissolution, liquidation, or winding up).

[#ULLCA1046(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(c) (person without interest holder liability who becomes subject to it has liability only to extent provided by organic law and only for debts incurred after conversion becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1046(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(d) (when conversion becomes effective, interest holder liability of person ceasing to hold interest in domestic converting company subject to specified rules).

[#ULLCA1046(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(d)(1) (conversion does not discharge interest holder liability incurred before conversion became effective).

[#ULLCA1046(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(d)(2) (person does not have interest holder liability for debt incurred after conversion becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1046(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(d)(3) (act continues to apply to release, collection, or discharge of preserved interest holder liability as if conversion had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1046(d)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(d)(4) (person has whatever rights of contribution provided by act, other law, or organic rules with respect to preserved liability as if conversion had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1046(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(e) (when conversion becomes effective, foreign entity that is converted entity may be served with process in state for collection and enforcement of debts and liabilities as provided in § 119).

[#ULLCA1046(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(f) (if converting entity is registered foreign entity, its registration to do business in state is canceled when conversion becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1046(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1046(g) (conversion does not require entity to wind up its affairs and does not constitute or cause dissolution of entity).

[#ULLCA1051(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1051(b) (by complying with provisions applicable to foreign companies, foreign limited liability company may become domestic limited liability company if domestication authorized by law of foreign company's jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1051(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1051(c) (if protected agreement contains provision applying to merger but not referring to domestication, provision applies to domestication as if domestication were merger until provision amended after effective date of act).

[#ULLCA1053]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1053 (approval of domestication).

[#ULLCA1054]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054 (amendment or abandonment of plan of domestication).

[#ULLCA1054(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(a)(1) (plan may be amended in same manner as approved if plan does not provide manner of amendment).

[#ULLCA1054(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(a)(2) (plan may be amended by managers or members as provided in plan, but member entitled to vote on domestication entitled to vote on amendments changing consideration, organic records/rules, or other terms adversely affecting member).

[#ULLCA1054(a)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(a)(2)(A) (member may vote on amendment changing amount or kind of consideration to be received).

[#ULLCA1054(a)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(a)(2)(B) (member may vote on amendment changing certificate of organization or operating agreement of domesticated company except for changes not requiring member approval).

[#ULLCA1054(a)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(a)(2)(C) (member may vote on amendment changing other terms or conditions if change would adversely affect member in material respect).

[#ULLCA1054(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(b) (after plan approved and before statement effective, plan may be abandoned as provided in plan; unless prohibited, domestic domesticating company may abandon in same manner as approved).

[#ULLCA1054(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(c) (if plan abandoned after statement delivered but before effective, statement of abandonment signed by domesticating company must be delivered to Secretary of State for filing; statement takes effect on filing and domestication abandoned).

[#ULLCA1054(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(c)(1) (statement must contain name of domesticating company).

[#ULLCA1054(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(c)(2) (statement must contain date statement of domestication was filed).

[#ULLCA1054(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1054(c)(3) (statement must state domestication has been abandoned in accordance with this section).

[#ULLCA1055]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055 (statement of domestication; effective date of domestication).

[#ULLCA1055(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(a) (statement of domestication must be signed by domesticating company and delivered to Secretary of State for filing).

[#ULLCA1055(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(b) (statement must contain specified information).

[#ULLCA1055(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(b)(1) (statement must contain name and jurisdiction of formation of domesticating company).

[#ULLCA1055(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(b)(2) (statement must contain name and jurisdiction of formation of domesticated company).

[#ULLCA1055(b)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(b)(3) (if domesticating company is domestic, statement must state plan was approved in accordance with this part; if foreign, statement must state domestication approved in accordance with law of its jurisdiction of formation).

[#ULLCA1055(b)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(b)(4) (statement must contain certificate of organization of domesticated company as attachment).

[#ULLCA1055(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(c) (in addition to requirements of subsection (b), statement may contain any other provision not prohibited by law).

[#ULLCA1055(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(d) (certificate of organization of domestic domesticated company must satisfy requirements of act, but need not be signed).

[#ULLCA1055(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(e) (plan signed by domesticating domestic company that meets all requirements may be filed instead of statement and has same effect; references to statement refer to plan filed under this subsection).

[#ULLCA1055(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1055(f) (if domesticated entity is domestic company, domestication becomes effective when statement is effective; if foreign company, effective on later of date and time provided by organic law or when statement is effective).

[#ULLCA1056]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056 (effect of domestication).

[#ULLCA1056(a)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a) (when domestication becomes effective, specified consequences follow).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(1) (domesticated entity organized under and subject to organic law of domesticated entity and is same entity without interruption as domesticating entity).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(1)(A)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(1)(A) (domesticated entity organized under and subject to organic law of domesticated entity).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(1)(B)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(1)(B) (domesticated entity same entity without interruption as domesticating entity).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(2) (all property of domesticating entity continues to be vested in domesticated entity without transfer, reversion, or impairment).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(3) (all debts, obligations, and other liabilities of domesticating entity continue as debts, obligations, and other liabilities of domesticated entity).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(4) (except as otherwise provided by law or plan, all rights, privileges, immunities, powers, and purposes of domesticating entity remain in domesticated entity).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(5)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(5) (name of domesticated entity may be substituted for name of domesticating entity in any pending action or proceeding).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(6)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(6) (certificate of organization of domesticated entity becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(7)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(7) (provisions of operating agreement of domesticated entity which are to be in record, if any, approved as part of plan become effective).

[#ULLCA1056(a)(8)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(a)(8) (interests in domesticating entity are converted to extent and as approved in connection with domestication, and members entitled only to rights under plan and any appraisal rights under § 1006).

[#ULLCA1056(b)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(b) (except as otherwise provided in organic law or operating agreement, domestication does not give rise to rights that member, manager, or third party would have upon dissolution, liquidation, or winding up).

[#ULLCA1056(c)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(c) (person without interest holder liability who becomes subject to it has liability only to extent provided by act and only for debts incurred after domestication becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1056(d)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(d) (when domestication becomes effective, interest holder liability of person ceasing to hold interest in domestic domesticating company subject to specified rules).

[#ULLCA1056(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(d)(1) (domestication does not discharge interest holder liability incurred before domestication became effective).

[#ULLCA1056(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(d)(2) (person does not have interest holder liability for debt incurred after domestication becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1056(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(d)(3) (act continues to apply to release, collection, or discharge of preserved interest holder liability as if domestication had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1056(d)(4)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(d)(4) (person has whatever rights of contribution provided by act, other law, or operating agreement with respect to preserved liability as if domestication had not occurred).

[#ULLCA1056(e)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(e) (when domestication becomes effective, foreign limited liability company that is domesticated company may be served with process in state for collection and enforcement of debts and liabilities as provided in § 119).

[#ULLCA1056(f)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(f) (if domesticating company is registered foreign entity, registration of company is canceled when domestication becomes effective).

[#ULLCA1056(g)]: Revised Unif. Ltd. Liab. Co. Act § 1056(g) (domestication does not require domestic domesticating company to wind up its affairs and does not constitute or cause dissolution of company).

[#RUPA101]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 101 (short title).

[#RUPA102]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102 (definitions).

[#RUPA102(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(1) (definition of "business" includes every trade, occupation, and profession).

[#RUPA102(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(2) (definition of "contribution" as property or benefit provided to become a partner).

[#RUPA102(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(3) (definition of "debtor in bankruptcy" under federal or comparable state/foreign insolvency law).

[#RUPA102(4)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(4) (definition of "distribution" as transfer of money or property on account of transferable interest or partnership capacity).

[#RUPA102(5)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(5) (definition of "foreign limited liability partnership" with partners having limited liability).

[#RUPA102(6)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(6) (definition of "foreign partnership" as unincorporated entity formed under another jurisdiction's law).

[#RUPA102(7)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(7) (definition of "jurisdiction" as political entity including states and foreign countries).

[#RUPA102(8)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(8) (definition of "jurisdiction of formation" as jurisdiction governing internal affairs).

[#RUPA102(9)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(9) (definition of "limited liability partnership" that has filed statement of qualification).

[#RUPA102(10)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(10) (definition of "partner" as person becoming partner under § 402 or when partnership became subject to RUPA).

[#RUPA102(11)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(11) (definition of "partnership" as association of two or more persons carrying on business for profit).

[#RUPA102(12)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(12) (definition of "partnership agreement" as agreement of all partners on matters in § 105(a)).

[#RUPA102(13)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(13) (definition of "partnership at will" as partnership with no agreed term or particular undertaking).

[#RUPA102(14)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(14) (definition of "person" as individual, entity, or other legal/commercial entity).

[#RUPA102(15)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(15) (definition of "principal office" as executive office location).

[#RUPA102(16)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(16) (definition of "property" as all property real, personal, tangible, or intangible).

[#RUPA102(17)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(17) (definition of "record" as information inscribed on tangible or electronic medium).

[#RUPA102(18)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(18) (definition of "registered agent" authorized to receive service of process on partnership).

[#RUPA102(19)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(19) (definition of "registered foreign limited liability partnership" registered to do business).

[#RUPA102(20)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(20) (definition of "sign" as execution/adoption of tangible symbol or electronic symbol with intent to authenticate).

[#RUPA102(21)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(21) (definition of "state" as US state, DC, Puerto Rico, or territorial possession).

[#RUPA102(22)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(22) (definition of "transfer" includes assignment, conveyance, sale, lease, encumbrance, gift, operation of law).

[#RUPA102(23)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(23) (definition of "transferable interest" as right to receive distributions as partner).

[#RUPA102(24)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 102(24) (definition of "transferee" as person to which transferable interest transferred).

[#RUPA103]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103 (knowledge; notice).

[#RUPA103(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(a) (person knows fact if has actual knowledge or deemed to know under subsection (d)).

[#RUPA103(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(b) (person has notice of fact if has reason to know or deemed to have notice under subsection (d)).

[#RUPA103(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(c) (person notifies another by taking steps reasonably required in ordinary course).

[#RUPA103(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(d) (person not partner deemed to know limitations on real property transfer authority; notice of dissociation, dissolution, termination, or structural change 90 days after filing).

[#RUPA103(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(d)(1) (non-partner deemed to know limitation on authority to transfer real property under § 303(g)).

[#RUPA103(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(d)(2) (non-partner deemed to have notice of dissociation within 90 days after statement of dissociation becomes effective; dissolution, termination, or structural change 90 days after filing).

[#RUPA103(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 103(e) (partner's knowledge or notice effective immediately as knowledge/notice to partnership except fraud with partner consent).

[#RUPA104]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 104 (governing law).

[#RUPA104(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 104(1) (limited liability partnership governed by law of this state).

[#RUPA104(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 104(2) (partnership not LLP governed by law of jurisdiction of principal office).

[#RUPA105]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105 (partnership agreement; scope, function, and limitations).

[#RUPA105(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(a) (partnership agreement governs relations among partners and between partners and partnership).

[#RUPA105(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(a)(1) (agreement governs relations among partners and between partners and partnership).

[#RUPA105(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(a)(2) (agreement governs business and conduct of business).

[#RUPA105(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(a)(3) (agreement governs means and conditions for amending agreement).

[#RUPA105(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(b) (act governs matters agreement does not address).

[#RUPA105(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c) (partnership agreement may not vary specified provisions).

[#RUPA105(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(1) (cannot vary law applicable under § 104(1)).

[#RUPA105(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(2) (cannot vary provisions of § 110).

[#RUPA105(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(3) (cannot vary provisions of § 307).

[#RUPA105(c)(4)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(4) (cannot unreasonably restrict information rights under § 408).

[#RUPA105(c)(5)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(5) (cannot alter or eliminate duty of loyalty or care except as provided in subsection (d)).

[#RUPA105(c)(6)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(6) (cannot eliminate contractual obligation of good faith under § 409(d)).

[#RUPA105(c)(7)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(7) (cannot unreasonably restrict right to maintain action under § 410(b)).

[#RUPA105(c)(8)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(8) (cannot relieve liability for bad faith or misconduct).

[#RUPA105(c)(9)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(9) (cannot vary power to dissociate except to require notice in record).

[#RUPA105(c)(10)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(10) (cannot vary grounds for expulsion under § 601(5)).

[#RUPA105(c)(11)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(11) (cannot vary causes of dissolution under § 801(4)-(5)).

[#RUPA105(c)(12)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(12) (cannot vary requirement to wind up business).

[#RUPA105(c)(13)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(13) (cannot vary right to vote on cancellation of LLP statement of qualification).

[#RUPA105(c)(14)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(14) (cannot vary right to approve merger, interest exchange, conversion, domestication).

[#RUPA105(c)(15)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(15) (cannot vary required contents of structural change plan).

[#RUPA105(c)(16)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(16) (cannot vary provisions pertaining to registered agents or Secretary of State).

[#RUPA105(c)(17)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(c)(17) (cannot restrict rights of non-partners except as provided).

[#RUPA105(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(d) (partnership agreement may specify method for authorization/ratification of acts).

[#RUPA105(d)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(d)(1) (may specify authorization/ratification; may alter distribution prohibition in § 406(a)(2)).

[#RUPA105(d)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(d)(2) (may eliminate fiduciary duty when relieving partner of responsibility).

[#RUPA105(d)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(d)(3) (may alter/eliminate duty of loyalty, identify non-violating activities, alter care if not manifestly unreasonable).

[#RUPA105(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 105(e) (court decides whether term manifestly unreasonable based on purpose, business, and circumstances at adoption).

[#RUPA106]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 106 (partnership agreement effect on partnership and person becoming partner; preformation agreement).

[#RUPA106(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 106(a) (partnership bound by agreement whether or not manifested assent).

[#RUPA106(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 106(b) (person becoming partner deemed to assent to agreement).

[#RUPA106(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 106(c) (intending initial partners may make preformation agreement).

[#RUPA107]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 107 (partnership agreement effect on third parties and relationship to filed records).

[#RUPA107(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 107(a) (agreement may specify amendment requires approval or condition).

[#RUPA107(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 107(b) (obligations to transferee governed by agreement; post-dissociation amendments limited).

[#RUPA107(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 107(c) (if filed record contains ineffective provision under § 105(c) or (d)(3), provision ineffective in record).

[#RUPA107(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 107(d) (if filed record conflicts with agreement, agreement prevails with partners and transferees; record prevails with third parties).

[#RUPA108]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108 (signing of records delivered for filing to Secretary of State).

[#RUPA108(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(a) (record must be signed as specified).

[#RUPA108(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(a)(1) (record signed by partnership must be signed by authorized person).

[#RUPA108(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(a)(2) (record for dissolved partnership signed by person winding up or appointed to wind up).

[#RUPA108(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(a)(3) (statement of denial signed by person making denial).

[#RUPA108(a)(4)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(a)(4) (other record on behalf of person signed by that person).

[#RUPA108(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(b) (record may be signed by agent; deceased/incompetent by legal representative).

[#RUPA108(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 108(c) (person signing affirms authorized to sign).

[#RUPA109]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 109 (liability for inaccurate information in filed record).

[#RUPA109(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 109(a) (person suffering loss may recover from signer knowing information inaccurate or partner with knowledge/notice of inaccuracy).

[#RUPA109(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 109(a)(1) (person that signed knowing information inaccurate).

[#RUPA109(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 109(a)(2) (partner with knowledge/notice who could have corrected via amendment, petition, or statement of change).

[#RUPA109(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 109(b) (partnership agreement may relieve partner and impose responsibility on other partner).

[#RUPA109(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 109(c) (signer affirms under penalty of perjury information is accurate).

[#RUPA110]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 110 (application to existing relationships).

[#RUPA110(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 110(a) (before all-inclusive date, act governs only partnerships formed after effective date or electing to be subject).

[#RUPA110(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 110(b) (on and after all-inclusive date, act governs all partnerships).

[#RUPA110(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 110(c) (liability provisions for partnerships electing RUPA apply to new third parties immediately; existing third parties only with knowledge or notice until all-inclusive date).

[#RUPA111]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 111 (delivery of record).

[#RUPA111(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 111(b) (delivery to Secretary of State effective only when received).

[#RUPA112]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 112 (signing and filing pursuant to judicial order).

[#RUPA112(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 112(b) (if petitioner not partnership, must make partnership party to action).

[#RUPA112(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 112(c) (record filed unsigned is effective without being signed).

[#RUPA114(4)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 114(4) (if delayed date but no time specified, effective at 12:01 a.m. on date).

[#RUPA115]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 115 (withdrawal of filed record before effectiveness).

[#RUPA115(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 115(b) (statement of withdrawal must be signed, identify record withdrawn, state withdrawal per agreement if partially signed).

[#RUPA116]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 116 (correcting filed record).

[#RUPA116(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 116(a) (record may be corrected if inaccurate, defectively signed, or electronically defective at time of filing).

[#RUPA116(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 116(b) (to correct, deliver statement of correction to Secretary of State).

[#RUPA116(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 116(c) (statement of correction cannot state delayed effective date; must be signed; must identify, specify, and correct inaccuracy).

[#RUPA116(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 116(d) (statement of correction effective as of effective date of corrected record except for § 103(d) and relying third parties).

[#RUPA117(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 117(c) (Secretary of State must return record or notify of refusal within 15 business days with explanation).

[#RUPA117(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 117(e) (filing or refusal does not affect validity or create presumption of accuracy).

[#RUPA117(f)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 117(f) (Secretary of State may deliver records to person via direct delivery, registered agent, principal office, or provided address).

[#RUPA119]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 119 (supplemental principles of law apply unless displaced by act provisions).


[#RUPA201]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 201 (partnership as entity).

[#RUPA201(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 201(a) (partnership is entity distinct from partners).

[#RUPA201(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 201(b) (partnership is same entity regardless of LLP statement of qualification status).

[#RUPA202]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202 (formation of partnership).

[#RUPA202(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(a) (association of two or more persons carrying on business for profit forms partnership regardless of intent).

[#RUPA202(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(b) (association formed under other statute not partnership under RUPA).

[#RUPA202(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c) (rules for determining whether partnership formed; joint tenancy/property sharing insufficient; presumption of partnership from profit sharing with exceptions).

[#RUPA202(c)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(1) (joint tenancy, tenancy in common, co-ownership does not establish partnership).

[#RUPA202(c)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(2) (sharing gross returns does not establish partnership).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3) (profit sharing creates presumption of partnership unless profits received as debt payment, compensation, rent, retirement benefit, loan interest, or sale of goodwill).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)(A)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3)(A) (profit sharing exception: debt payment by installments).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)(B)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3)(B) (profit sharing exception: compensation for services or wages).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)(C)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3)(C) (profit sharing exception: rent).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)(D)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3)(D) (profit sharing exception: retirement/health benefit to deceased partner or beneficiary).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)(E)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3)(E) (profit sharing exception: interest on loan including variable returns from collateral).

[#RUPA202(c)(3)(F)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 202(c)(3)(F) (profit sharing exception: sale of goodwill or property by installments).

[#RUPA203]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 203 (partnership property).

[#RUPA203(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 203(a) (property acquired by partnership is partnership property not individual partner property).

[#RUPA204]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 204 (when property is partnership property).

[#RUPA204(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 204(a) (property is partnership property if acquired in partnership name or partner's name with indication of partner capacity/partnership existence).

[#RUPA204(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 204(b) (property acquired in partnership name via transfer to partnership in its name or to partners in capacity as partners).

[#RUPA204(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 204(c) (property presumed partnership property if purchased with partnership assets even without name indication).

[#RUPA204(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 204(d) (property in individual partner names without partnership indication presumed separate property even if used for partnership purposes).


[#RUPA301]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 301 (partner agent of partnership).

[#RUPA301(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 301(1) (partner is agent for partnership business; acts apparently for ordinary course business bind partnership unless partner lacked authority and other party knew/had notice).

[#RUPA301(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 301(2) (non-ordinary course acts bind partnership only if actually authorized by all other partners).

[#RUPA302]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302 (transfer of partnership property).

[#RUPA302(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(a) (partnership property transfer rules; subject to statement of partnership authority under § 303).

[#RUPA302(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(a)(1) (property in partnership name transferable by partner signature).

[#RUPA302(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(a)(2) (property in partners' names with capacity/partnership indication transferable by those persons).

[#RUPA302(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(a)(3) (property in other persons' names without partnership indication transferable by those persons).

[#RUPA302(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(b) (partnership may recover property from transferee if initial signing did not bind partnership and subsequent transferee knew/had notice or gave value for § 302(a)(3) property).

[#RUPA302(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(c) (partnership cannot recover from subsequent transferee if could not recover from earlier transferee).

[#RUPA302(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 302(d) (if person holds all partners' interests, partnership property vests in that person).

[#RUPA303]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303 (statement of partnership authority).

[#RUPA303(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(a) (partnership may file statement of partnership authority with Secretary of State).

[#RUPA303(a)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(a)(1) (statement must include partnership name and principal office address or LLP registered agent).

[#RUPA303(a)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(a)(2) (statement may specify authority/limitations of positions regarding real property transfer or partnership transactions).

[#RUPA303(a)(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(a)(3) (statement may specify authority/limitations of specific persons).

[#RUPA303(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(b) (to amend/cancel statement, partnership delivers amendment/cancellation stating partnership name, office/agent address, effective date, and contents).

[#RUPA303(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(c) (statement of authority affects only power to bind partnership to non-partners).

[#RUPA303(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(d) (limitation in statement not evidence of knowledge/notice except as provided in § 303).

[#RUPA303(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(e) (grant of non-real property authority in effective statement conclusive in favor of person giving value except with knowledge, statement cancellation, or contrary limitation).

[#RUPA303(f)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(f) (statement granting real property authority, if recorded, conclusive in favor of person giving value without knowledge unless statement canceled, restrictively amended, or limited by later statement).

[#RUPA303(g)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(g) (statement denying authority of person/position regarding real property transfer, if recorded, is conclusive limitation on apparent authority without knowledge).

[#RUPA303(h)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 303(h) (§ 303 does not affect apparent authority resulting from conduct separate from filing).

[#RUPA304]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 304 (statement of denial).

[#RUPA304(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 304(a) (partner may file statement of denial of statement of authority filed by another partner).

[#RUPA304(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 304(b) (statement of denial is limitation on authority for § 303 purposes).

[#RUPA305]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 305 (partnership liable for partner's actionable conduct).

[#RUPA305(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 305(a) (partnership liable for tort, wrongful act, breach of trust by partner committed in ordinary course or with apparent authority).

[#RUPA306]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 306 (partner's liability).

[#RUPA306(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 306(a) (partner liable jointly and severally for partnership obligations).

[#RUPA306(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 306(b) (judgment against partnership is not by itself judgment against partner; creditor must pursue partnership assets first).

[#RUPA306(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 306(c) (in LLP, partner not personally liable for partnership obligations or other partner misconduct; exception for partner's personal misconduct).

[#RUPA307]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 307 (actions by and against partnership and partners).

[#RUPA307(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 307(a) (partnership may be party to action; partnership may sue/be sued in partnership name).

[#RUPA307(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 307(b) (judgment against partnership may be enforced against partnership property and individual partner property).

[#RUPA307(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 307(c) (judgment debtor partner may be joined in action).

[#RUPA307(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 307(d) (partner may be independently liable for own misconduct).

[#RUPA308]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 308 (liability of purported partner).

[#RUPA308(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 308(a) (person representing self as partner liable to relying creditor as if partner; person believing self partner liable if partnership accepts benefits).

[#RUPA308(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 308(b) (partnership not liable for purported partner obligations unless partnership benefits or ratifies).


[#RUPA401]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401 (partner's rights and duties).

[#RUPA401(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(a) (each partner is equal co-owner of partnership property for partnership purposes not individual use).

[#RUPA401(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(b) (partner may not sell/transfer/pledge individual partnership property interest without consent; not binding transfer).

[#RUPA401(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(c) (partnership shall indemnify partner for partnership liabilities incurred in ordinary course or authorized).

[#RUPA401(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(d) (partner has right to participate in management/conduct of business; unless limited by agreement).

[#RUPA401(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(e) (partner does not have transferable right to sell interest without consent; may assign economic interest).

[#RUPA401(f)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(f) (unless agreement specifies otherwise, partners share distributions equally).

[#RUPA401(g)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(g) (unless agreement specifies, partners share losses equal to distribution shares).

[#RUPA401(h)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 401(h) (partner has right to inspect books/records).

[#RUPA402]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 402 (becoming partner).

[#RUPA402(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 402(a) (person becomes partner by agreement and meeting definition requirements).

[#RUPA402(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 402(b) (person may become partner without contribution).

[#RUPA402(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 402(c) (new partner does not have rights in pre-existing partnership property except through income/capital interest).

[#RUPA403]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 403 (form of contribution).

[#RUPA403(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 403(a) (partner contribution may be tangible/intangible property or services).

[#RUPA403(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 403(b) (partnership agreement governs promissory note obligations; unless agreed, note is not contribution).

[#RUPA404]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 404 (liability for contribution).

[#RUPA404(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 404(a) (partner obligated to perform contribution agreement).

[#RUPA404(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 404(b) (partner liable to partnership for promised contribution failure; liability enforceable by other partners).

[#RUPA404(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 404(c) (partnership may release partner from contribution obligation; other partners may claim indemnification from released partner).

[#RUPA405]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 405 (sharing of and right to distributions before dissolution).

[#RUPA405(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 405(a) (each partner entitled to share in distributions per partnership agreement; unless agreement specifies, equal shares).

[#RUPA405(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 405(b) (partner has no right to distributions before partnership dissolution unless agreement provides).

[#RUPA405(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 405(c) (in no event may distributions reduce partnership assets below liabilities unless otherwise agreed or stated in filing).

[#RUPA406]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 406 (limitations on distributions by limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA406(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 406(a) (LLP may not make distribution if after distribution partnership assets less than liabilities except per agreement).

[#RUPA406(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 406(b) (LLP may not make distribution if knowing/having notice insolvency would result).

[#RUPA406(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 406(c) (LLP member liable to return distribution received violating limitations unless in good faith reliance on partner representation).

[#RUPA406(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 406(d) (partner implementing improper distribution liable to partnership unless acting under authority).

[#RUPA407]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 407 (liability for improper distributions by limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA407(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 407(a) (partner liable to partnership for distribution violating § 406; liability enforceable by partnership and creditors).

[#RUPA407(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 407(b) (partner may recover return of improper distribution).

[#RUPA408]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 408 (rights to information of partners and persons dissociated as partner).

[#RUPA408(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 408(a) (partner entitled to access to books/records at principal office for partnership purposes).

[#RUPA408(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 408(b) (partnership shall provide books/records copies; partnership agreement may reasonably restrict availability/use).

[#RUPA408(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 408(c) (partnership shall provide financial information, tax information, and status information to partners in writing).

[#RUPA408(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 408(d) (partner may inspect books/records concerning specified transactions/activities for purpose stated in request).

[#RUPA408(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 408(e) (person dissociated as partner has access rights per agreement or to information continuing partnership business).

[#RUPA409]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409 (standards of conduct for partners).

[#RUPA409(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409(a) (partner is fiduciary regarding partnership business/property).

[#RUPA409(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409(b) (partner's fiduciary duty includes duty of loyalty: no competing business advantage, no secret profits, no self-dealing benefit).

[#RUPA409(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409(c) (partner owes duty of care: refrains from grossly negligent/reckless/intentional misconduct/knowing violation of law).

[#RUPA409(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409(d) (partner's contractual obligation of good faith and fair dealing; partnership agreement may define performance standards).

[#RUPA409(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409(e) (partner may engage in competing business not violating duty of loyalty if not using partnership assets/information).

[#RUPA409(f)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 409(f) (partnership agreements may alter/eliminate fiduciary duties and define manifestly unreasonable standards per § 105(d)).

[#RUPA410]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 410 (actions by partnership and partners).

[#RUPA410(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 410(a) (partnership may maintain action for breach of partnership agreement or fiduciary duty).

[#RUPA410(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 410(b) (partner may maintain action for proper accounting and remedies; standing rules as provided).

[#RUPA411]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 411 (continuation of partnership beyond definite term or particular undertaking).

[#RUPA411(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 411(a) (if partnership continues after term/undertaking expiration, partnership is at-will unless agreement indicates otherwise).

[#RUPA411(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 411(b) (if partnership continues after expiration, past terms/conditions control future until amended/waived).


[#RUPA501]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 501 (partner not co-owner of partnership property).

[#RUPA501(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 501(a) (partner is not co-owner of partnership property; partnership property vests in partnership not individual partners).

[#RUPA502]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 502 (nature of transferable interest).

[#RUPA502(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 502(a) (transferable interest is right to receive distributions; not right to manage/participate; not property interest in partnership).

[#RUPA503]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 503 (transfer of transferable interest).

[#RUPA503(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 503(a) (partner may transfer transferable interest; transfers not binding on partnership unless authorized).

[#RUPA503(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 503(b) (transferee has no partnership rights unless admitted as partner or agreement provides).

[#RUPA503(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 503(c) (partnership agreement may restrict transfers).

[#RUPA504]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 504 (charging order).

[#RUPA504(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 504(a) (judgment creditor may seek charging order against partner's transferable interest).

[#RUPA504(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 504(b) (court may grant charging order; creditor entitled to distributions but not partnership rights).

[#RUPA504(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 504(c) (charging order obtained, partnership may redeem interest or may elect to dissolve).

[#RUPA504(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 504(d) (redeemed interest has charging order priority over creditor claims).

[#RUPA505]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 505 (power of legal representative of deceased partner).

[#RUPA505(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 505(a) (legal representative of deceased partner has rights partner had; estate is transferee).


[#RUPA601]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601 (events causing dissociation).

[#RUPA601(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(1) (express will to withdraw as partner per § 602(a)).

[#RUPA601(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(2) (by agreement/consent to become member of another partnership).

[#RUPA601(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(3) (partner becomes debtor in bankruptcy).

[#RUPA601(4)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(4) (notice by partnership to partner that partnership intends to expel; notice or consent to expulsion).

[#RUPA601(5)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(5) (court order dissolving partnership expels partner on partner application for expulsion).

[#RUPA601(6)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(6) (death of individual partner or termination of non-individual partner).

[#RUPA601(7)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(7) (liquidation value of partner's interest to less than $0 in multiple distributions).

[#RUPA601(8)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(8) (partnership has effect of declaring partnership dissolved if not dissolving; partner dissociated unless partnership notices otherwise).

[#RUPA601(9)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(9) (merger where surviving entity not partnership).

[#RUPA601(10)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(10) (interest exchange resulting in cessation of partnership interest; conversion; domestication resulting in cessation).

[#RUPA601(11)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(11) (merger where surviving entity not partnership or interest exchange results in ceasing partnership interest).

[#RUPA601(12)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(12) (conversion under Article 11).

[#RUPA601(13)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(13) (domestication under Article 11 where person ceases as partner).

[#RUPA601(14)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(14) (domestication resulting in cessation of partner status).

[#RUPA601(15)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 601(15) (partnership dissolution and completion of winding up).

[#RUPA602]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602 (power to dissociate as partner; wrongful dissociation).

[#RUPA602(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(a) (partner has power to dissociate at any time by withdrawing as partner).

[#RUPA602(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b) (partner's dissociation is wrongful if in breach of partnership agreement or in definite-term partnership before expiration/completion under specified circumstances).

[#RUPA602(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b)(1) (wrongful dissociation: withdrawal in breach of agreement).

[#RUPA602(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b)(2) (wrongful dissociation in definite-term partnership: withdrawal before expiration absent death/other event; expulsion; natural event dissociation; willful dissolution of non-individual).

[#RUPA602(b)(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b)(2)(A) (wrongful dissociation: withdrawal before expiration unless follows 90-day death/other event or wrongful dissociation).

[#RUPA602(b)(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b)(2)(B) (wrongful dissociation: judicial expulsion before expiration).

[#RUPA602(b)(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b)(2)(C) (wrongful dissociation: natural event dissociation before expiration).

[#RUPA602(b)(2)(D)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(b)(2)(D) (wrongful dissociation: willful dissolution/termination of non-individual partner).

[#RUPA602(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 602(c) (wrongfully dissociating partner liable to partnership for damages; liable in addition to other liabilities).

[#RUPA603]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 603 (effect of dissociation).

[#RUPA603(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 603(a) (dissociation causing dissolution triggers Article 8; otherwise Article 7 applies).

[#RUPA603(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 603(b) (dissociated partner loses management/conduct right; duties/obligations end regarding post-dissociation matters except winding up).

[#RUPA603(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 603(c) (dissociation does not discharge partner from pre-dissociation liabilities).


[#RUPA701]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701 (purchase of interest of person dissociated as partner).

[#RUPA701(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(a) (partnership shall purchase dissociated partner interest if dissociation not resulting in dissolution/winding up).

[#RUPA701(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(b) (buyout price is amount distributable under § 806(b) if sold as going concern; liquidation value or going concern value, whichever greater).

[#RUPA701(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(c) (interest accrues from dissociation to payment; damages for wrongful dissociation offset against buyout price).

[#RUPA701(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(d) (partnership shall defend/indemnify dissociated partner against liabilities except partner's own wrongful conduct acts).

[#RUPA701(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(e) (if purchase agreement reached, parties perform per agreement; if no agreement within 120 days, partnership pays/offers payment).

[#RUPA701(f)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(f) (if deferred payment authorized under § 701(h), partnership may tender written offer with terms/security).

[#RUPA701(g)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(g) (payment/tender must include partnership asset/liability statement, latest balance sheet/income statement, calculation explanation, payment satisfaction notice).

[#RUPA701(h)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(h) (wrongfully dissociating partner in definite-term partnership may not receive payment until expiration unless court determines earlier payment not undue hardship; deferred payment must be secured with interest).

[#RUPA701(i)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 701(i) (dissociated partner may sue to determine buyout price, offsets, terms; must commence within 120 days of tender or one year of demand; court determines price/offsets/terms and may assess attorney/expert fees).

[#RUPA702]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 702 (power to bind and liability of person dissociated as partner).

[#RUPA702(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 702(a) (dissociated partner is agent of partnership regarding ordinary course business; acts bind partnership per § 301 until apparent authority ends).

[#RUPA702(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 702(b) (dissociated partner apparent authority ends immediately for real property; ends within 2 years for other acts unless party knows/has notice otherwise).

[#RUPA702(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 702(c) (dissociated partner liable for obligations binding partnership under § 702(a) if within 2 years and other party lacks knowledge/notice and reasonably believes partner still partner).

[#RUPA703]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 703 (liability of person dissociated as partner to other persons).

[#RUPA703(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 703(a) (dissociated partner not liable for partnership obligations incurred after dissociation).

[#RUPA703(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 703(b) (dissociated partner liable on post-dissociation transaction only if partner would be liable and less than 2 years passed and other party lacks knowledge/notice).

[#RUPA703(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 703(c) (dissociated partner may be released from liability by creditor agreement).

[#RUPA703(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 703(d) (dissociated partner released from liability if creditor, knowing/noticing dissociation, agrees to material alteration in payment terms).

[#RUPA704]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 704 (statement of dissociation).

[#RUPA704(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 704(a) (dissociated partner or partnership may file statement of dissociation with Secretary of State).

[#RUPA704(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 704(b) (statement of dissociation is limitation on authority per § 303).

[#RUPA705]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 705 (continued use of partnership name).

[#RUPA705(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 705(a) (continued use of partnership name or dissociated partner name does not make dissociated partner liable for obligations of continuing business).


[#RUPA801]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801 (events causing dissolution).

[#RUPA801(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(1) (partnership at will dissolves upon partner's express will to withdraw; if withdrawal date specified, dissolution on later date).

[#RUPA801(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(2) (definite-term partnership dissolves upon: at-least-half partner vote to wind up within 90 days of death/other dissociation; all-partner vote to wind up; term/undertaking expiration).

[#RUPA801(2)(A)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(2)(A) (definite-term dissolution: at-least-half partner affirmative vote/consent to wind up within 90 days of death or wrongful dissociation).

[#RUPA801(2)(B)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(2)(B) (definite-term dissolution: affirmative vote/consent of all partners to wind up).

[#RUPA801(2)(C)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(2)(C) (definite-term dissolution: expiration of term or completion of undertaking).

[#RUPA801(3)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(3) (dissolution upon event/circumstance stated in partnership agreement).

[#RUPA801(4)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(4) (dissolution by court order on partner application upon grounds: unlawful conduct, unreasonable frustration of economic purpose, another partner conduct, not reasonably practicable).

[#RUPA801(4)(A)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(4)(A) (court dissolution: all/substantially all business unlawful).

[#RUPA801(4)(B)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(4)(B) (court dissolution: economic purpose unreasonably frustrated).

[#RUPA801(4)(C)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(4)(C) (court dissolution: another partner conduct making partnership not reasonably practicable).

[#RUPA801(4)(D)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(4)(D) (court dissolution: otherwise not reasonably practicable per agreement).

[#RUPA801(5)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(5) (court dissolution by transferee application: equitable to wind up; definite-term or at-will partnership).

[#RUPA801(5)(A)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(5)(A) (transferee court dissolution: definite-term after expiration/completion).

[#RUPA801(5)(B)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(5)(B) (transferee court dissolution: at-will partnership at any time).

[#RUPA801(6)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 801(6) (dissolution upon 90 consecutive days without at least two partners).

[#RUPA802]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802 (winding up).

[#RUPA802(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802(a) (dissolved partnership winds up business and continues only for winding up unless Article 8 provides otherwise).

[#RUPA802(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802(b) (partnership winds up: discharges debts/obligations/liabilities, settles/closes business, marshals/distributes assets; may file dissolution statement, preserve going concern, prosecute actions, continue business as reasonably necessary).

[#RUPA802(b)(1)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802(b)(1) (winding up duties: discharge liabilities, settle, close, marshal/distribute assets).

[#RUPA802(b)(2)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802(b)(2) (winding up powers: file dissolution statement, preserve going concern, prosecute/defend actions, continue business).

[#RUPA802(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802(c) (all partners participate in winding up except expelled partner; partner not involved unless partnership determines necessary).

[#RUPA802(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 802(d) (on final settlement, remaining assets distributed per partnership agreement; if agreement silent, equal per capital contributions).

[#RUPA803]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 803 (rescinding dissolution).

[#RUPA803(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 803(a) (all partners may rescind dissolution unless winding up has begun or third party relies).

[#RUPA803(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 803(b) (rescission statement filed with Secretary of State; partnership re-establishes as if dissolution not occurred).

[#RUPA804]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 804 (power to bind partnership after dissolution).

[#RUPA804(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 804(a) (dissolved partnership acts bind partnership for winding up or liquidation; acts not binding unless necessary for winding up).

[#RUPA804(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 804(b) (dissolved partnership bound for ordinary course business or authorized acts).

[#RUPA804(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 804(c) (third party unaware of dissolution may treat partnership as not dissolved).

[#RUPA805]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 805 (liability after dissolution of partner and person dissociated as partner).

[#RUPA805(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 805(a) (after dissolution, partner liable for partnership obligations incurred before/after dissolution unless bound under § 804).

[#RUPA805(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 805(b) (after dissolution, partner liable for partnership obligations incurred after dissolution if bound per § 804).

[#RUPA805(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 805(c) (after dissolution, dissociated person liable per § 703 if partnership obligation attributable to pre-dissociation action).

[#RUPA805(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 805(d) (after dissolution, dissociated person not liable for partnership obligation incurred after dissociation).

[#RUPA806]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 806 (disposition of assets in winding up; when contributions required).

[#RUPA806(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 806(a) (partnership assets applied to settlement/close business in this order: partnership liabilities (excluding partner contributions), capital contributions, remaining distributable per partnership agreement or per capita).

[#RUPA806(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 806(b) (partner entitled to share of partnership assets applied per § 806(a) as if liquidated on dissociation date).

[#RUPA806(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 806(c) (if partnership assets insufficient, partners contribute to cover liabilities per capital contribution ratio unless agreement provides otherwise).

[#RUPA806(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 806(d) (if partner fails to contribute, other partners may enforce contribution obligation; liable for share of unpaid contributions).

[#RUPA807]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 807 (known claims against dissolved limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA807(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 807(a) (dissolved LLP may file notice of intent to dissolve; claims must be presented by deadline or barred).

[#RUPA807(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 807(b) (LLP shall notify known claimants of notice; send copies; invite claim presentation per deadline).

[#RUPA807(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 807(c) (LLP shall promptly pay meritorious claims or establish reserves; claims may be contested).

[#RUPA808]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 808 (other claims against dissolved limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA808(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 808(a) (LLP may make provision for unknown claims via trust, escrow, or insurance; creditor may pursue partnership assets/partners limited by liability shield).

[#RUPA809]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 809 (court proceedings).

[#RUPA809(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 809(a) (court may approve arrangement for partnership liabilities per §§ 807-808).

[#RUPA810]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 810 (liability of partner and person dissociated as partner when claim against partnership barred).

[#RUPA810(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 810(a) (if claim against partnership barred, partner/dissociated person not liable unless they agreed otherwise or partnership assets insufficient).


[#RUPA901]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901 (statement of qualification).

[#RUPA901(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901(a) (partnership may file statement of qualification to become LLP; statement includes name, principal office, declaration that partnership is LLP).

[#RUPA901(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901(b) (statement of qualification is effective upon filing; partnership is LLP).

[#RUPA901(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901(c) (partnership may file new statement of qualification; prior statement superseded).

[#RUPA901(d)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901(d) (statement of qualification may state effective date not more than 90 days after filing).

[#RUPA901(e)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901(e) (if statement canceled, partnership no longer LLP as of cancellation date).

[#RUPA901(f)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 901(f) (becoming/remaining LLP requires partnership agreement vote; partners may amend/cancel statement).

[#RUPA902]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 902 (permitted names).

[#RUPA902(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 902(a) (LLP name includes "Registered Limited Liability Partnership", "Limited Liability Partnership" or abbreviations).

[#RUPA902(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 902(b) (LLP may use name not per § 902(a) if word/phrase distinguishes it per law).

[#RUPA903]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 903 (administrative revocation of statement of qualification).

[#RUPA903(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 903(a) (Secretary of State may administratively revoke LLP statement if partnership fails filing requirements; must notify partnership before revocation).

[#RUPA903(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 903(b) (revocation effective 90 days after notice; partnership may reinstate per § 904).

[#RUPA904]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 904 (reinstatement).

[#RUPA904(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 904(a) (partnership may reinstate after administrative revocation via restated statement of qualification and late filings/fees).

[#RUPA904(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 904(b) (reinstatement effective upon filing).

[#RUPA905]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 905 (judicial review of denial of reinstatement).

[#RUPA905(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 905(a) (partnership may petition court if Secretary of State denies reinstatement).

[#RUPA906]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 906 (reservation of name).

[#RUPA906(a)]: Revised Unif. P'shop Act § 906(a) (prospective LLP may reserve name with Secretary of State).

[#RUPA907]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 907 (registration of name).

[#RUPA907(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 907(a) (person entitled to register LLP name with Secretary of State).

[#RUPA908]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 908 (registered agent).

[#RUPA908(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 908(a) (LLP shall continuously maintain registered agent; statement of qualification must list agent name/address).

[#RUPA908(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 908(b) (registered agent must maintain office and accept service on LLP's behalf).

[#RUPA909]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 909 (change of registered agent or address for registered agent by limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA909(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 909(a) (LLP may change registered agent/address via statement of change filed with Secretary of State).

[#RUPA910]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 910 (resignation of registered agent).

[#RUPA910(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 910(a) (registered agent may resign via statement delivered to Secretary of State; notice to LLP).

[#RUPA910(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 910(b) (after resignation effective date, LLP shall appoint new agent or file statement).

[#RUPA911]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 911 (change of name or address by registered agent).

[#RUPA911(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 911(a) (registered agent may change name/address via statement to Secretary of State).

[#RUPA912]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 912 (service of process, notice, or demand).

[#RUPA912(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 912(a) (service on LLP registered agent satisfies service on LLP).

[#RUPA912(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 912(b) (service on registered agent in registered agent capacity satisfies service on LLP and partner).

[#RUPA913]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 913 ([annual] [biennial] report for Secretary of State).

[#RUPA913(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 913(a) (LLP shall file annual or biennial report as specified by jurisdiction).

P'ship Act § 1005(a) (foreign LLP may engage in specified activities without registration: maintains office, business meetings, bank accounts, sales through independent contractors, transactions securing debts, activities completing prior transactions, business within 90 days of registration intent if registered within 90 days).

[#RUPA1006]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1006 (noncomplying name of foreign limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA1007]: Revised Unif. P'shop Act § 1007 (withdrawal deemed on conversion to domestic filing entity or domestic limited liability partnership).

[#RUPA1125]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1125 (statement of merger; effective date of merger).

[#RUPA1125(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1125(a) (merger effective upon statement of merger filing or later date specified).

[#RUPA1126]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1126 (effect of merger).

[#RUPA1126(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1126(a) (upon merger, surviving entity assumes merging entity property/liabilities).

[#RUPA1126(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1126(b) (merging entity ceases as entity; surviving entity continues).

[#RUPA1126(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1126(c) (merged partners become surviving entity members if surviving entity partnership).


[#RUPA1131]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1131 (interest exchange authorized).

[#RUPA1131(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1131(a) (partnership may exchange partners' interests for acquired entity interests per plan).

[#RUPA1132]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1132 (plan of interest exchange).

[#RUPA1134]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1134 (amendment or abandonment of plan of interest exchange).

[#RUPA1134(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1134(a) (plan may be amended/abandoned per process in plan or by all entities before statement effective).

[#RUPA1135]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1135 (statement of interest exchange; effective date of interest exchange).

[#RUPA1135(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1135(a) (interest exchange effective upon filing or later date specified).

[#RUPA1136]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1136 (effect of interest exchange).

[#RUPA1136(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1136(a) (acquired entity receives partnership interests per plan; partnership interests transfer to acquiring entity).


[#RUPA1141]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1141 (conversion authorized).

[#RUPA1141(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1141(a) (partnership may convert to other entity form per plan).

[#RUPA1142]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1142 (plan of conversion).

[#RUPA1143]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1143 (approval of conversion).

[#RUPA1144]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1144 (amendment or abandonment of plan of conversion).

[#RUPA1144(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1144(a) (plan may be amended/abandoned per process or by all entities before statement effective).

[#RUPA1145]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1145 (statement of conversion; effective date of conversion).

[#RUPA1145(a)]: Revised Unif. P'shop Act § 1145(a) (conversion effective upon filing or later date specified).

[#RUPA1146]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1146 (effect of conversion).

[#RUPA1146(a)]: Revised Unif. P'shop Act § 1146(a) (upon conversion, partnership property vests in converted entity; partnership ceases).

[#RUPA1146(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1146(b) (converted entity assumes partnership liabilities and obligations).

[#RUPA1146(c)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1146(c) (partner interests convert to converted entity interests per plan).


[#RUPA1151]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1151 (domestication authorized).

[#RUPA1151(a)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1151(a) (partnership may domesticate to jurisdiction via plan).

[#RUPA1156(b)]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1156(b) (domesticated partnership's property, liabilities, and interests continue unchanged).


[#RUPA1201]: Revised Unif. P'ship Act § 1201 (uniformity of application and construction).

[#RUPA1201(a)]: Revised Unif. P'shop Act § 1201(a) (law should be applied/constructed to effectuate uniform application in all jurisdictions).
